# Codex Code Review Skill

## Trigger Conditions

Triggered when user input contains:

- "代码审核", "代码审查", "审查代码", "审核代码"
- "review", "code review", "review code", "codex 审核"
- "帮我审核", "检查代码", "审一下", "看看代码"

## Core Concept: Intention vs Implementation

Running `codex review --uncommitted` alone only shows AI "what was done (Implementation)".
Recording intention first tells AI "what you wanted to do (Intention)".

**"Code changes + intention description" as combined input is the most effective way to improve AI code review quality.**

## Skill Architecture

This skill operates in two phases:

1. **Preparation Phase** (current context): Check working directory, update CHANGELOG
2. **Review Phase** (isolated context): Invoke Task tool to execute Lint + codex review (using context: fork to reduce context waste)

## Execution Steps

### 0. [First] Check Working Directory Status

```bash
git diff --name-only && git status --short
```

**Decide review mode based on output:**

- **Has uncommitted changes** → Continue with steps 1-4 (normal flow)
- **Clean working directory** → Directly invoke codex-runner: `codex review --commit HEAD`

### 1. [Mandatory] Check if CHANGELOG is Updated

**Before any review, must check if CHANGELOG.md contains description of current changes.**

```bash
# Check if CHANGELOG.md is in uncommitted changes
git diff --name-only | grep -E "(CHANGELOG|changelog)"
```

**If CHANGELOG is not updated, you must automatically perform the following (don't ask user to do it manually):**

1. **Analyze changes**: Run `git diff --stat` and `git diff` to get complete changes
2. **Auto-generate CHANGELOG entry**: Generate compliant entry based on code changes
3. **Write to CHANGELOG.md**: Use Edit tool to insert entry at top of `[Unreleased]` section
4. **Continue review flow**: Immediately proceed to next steps after CHANGELOG update

**Auto-generated CHANGELOG entry format:**

```markdown
## [Unreleased]

### Added / Changed / Fixed

- Feature description: what problem was solved or what functionality was implemented
- Affected files: main modified files/modules
```

**Example - Auto-generation Flow:**

```
1. Detected CHANGELOG not updated
2. Run git diff --stat, found handlers/responses.go modified (+88 lines)
3. Run git diff to analyze details: added CompactHandler function
4. Auto-generate entry:
   ### Added
   - Added `/v1/responses/compact` endpoint for conversation context compression
   - Supports multi-channel failover and request body size limits
5. Use Edit tool to write to CHANGELOG.md
6. Continue with lint and codex review
```

### 2. [Critical] Stage All New Files

**Before invoking codex review, must add all new files (untracked files) to git staging area, otherwise codex will report P1 error.**

```bash
# Check for new files
git status --short | grep "^??"
```

**If there are new files, automatically execute:**

```bash
# Safely stage all new files (handles empty list and special filenames)
git ls-files --others --exclude-standard -z | while IFS= read -r -d '' f; do git add -- "$f"; done
```

**Explanation:**

- `-z` uses null character to separate filenames, correctly handles filenames with spaces/newlines
- `while IFS= read -r -d ''` reads filenames one by one
- `git add -- "$f"` uses `--` separator, correctly handles filenames starting with `-`
- When no new files exist, loop body doesn't execute, safely skipped
- This won't stage modified files, only handles new files
- codex needs files to be tracked by git for proper review

### 3. Evaluate Task Difficulty and Invoke codex-runner

**Count change scale:**

```bash
# Count number of changed files and lines of code
git diff --stat | tail -1
```

**Difficulty Assessment Criteria:**

**Difficult Tasks** (meets any condition):

- Modified files ≥ 10
- Total code changes (insertions + deletions) ≥ 500 lines
- Single metric: insertions ≥ 300 lines OR deletions ≥ 300 lines
- Involves core architecture/algorithm changes
- Cross-module refactoring
- Config: `model_reasoning_effort=xhigh`, timeout 30 minutes

**Normal Tasks** (other cases):

- Config: `model_reasoning_effort=high`, timeout 10 minutes

**Evaluation Method:**

You MUST parse the `git diff --stat` output correctly to determine difficulty:

```bash
# Get the summary line (last line of git diff --stat)
git diff --stat | tail -1
# Example outputs:
# "20 files changed, 342 insertions(+), 985 deletions(-)"
# "1 file changed, 50 insertions(+)"  # No deletions
# "3 files changed, 120 deletions(-)"  # No insertions
```

**Parsing Rules:**
1. Extract file count from "X file(s) changed" (handle both "1 file" and "N files")
2. Extract insertions from "Y insertion(s)(+)" if present (handle both "1 insertion" and "N insertions"), otherwise 0
3. Extract deletions from "Z deletion(s)(-)" if present (handle both "1 deletion" and "N deletions"), otherwise 0
4. Calculate total changes = insertions + deletions

**Important Edge Cases:**
- Single file: `"1 file changed"` (singular form)
- No insertions: Git omits `"insertions(+)"` entirely → treat as 0
- No deletions: Git omits `"deletions(-)"` entirely → treat as 0
- Pure rename: May show `"0 insertions(+), 0 deletions(-)"` or omit both

**Decision Logic (ANY condition triggers xhigh):**
- IF file_count >= 10 → xhigh
- IF total_changes >= 500 → xhigh
- IF insertions >= 300 → xhigh
- IF deletions >= 300 → xhigh
- ELSE → high

**Example Cases:**
- ✅ "20 files changed, 342 insertions(+), 985 deletions(-)" → xhigh (files=20≥10, total=1327≥500, deletions=985≥300)
- ✅ "5 files changed, 600 insertions(+), 50 deletions(-)" → xhigh (total=650≥500, insertions=600≥300)
- ✅ "12 files changed, 100 insertions(+), 50 deletions(-)" → xhigh (files=12≥10)
- ✅ "1 file changed, 400 deletions(-)" → xhigh (deletions=400≥300)
- ❌ "3 files changed, 150 insertions(+), 80 deletions(-)" → high (all conditions fail)
- ❌ "1 file changed, 50 insertions(+)" → high (no deletions, total=50<500)

**Invoke codex-runner Subtask:**

Use Task tool to invoke codex-runner, passing complete command (including Lint + codex review):

```
Task parameters:
- subagent_type: Bash
- description: "Execute Lint and codex review"
- timeout: 1800000 (30 minutes for difficult tasks) or 600000 (10 minutes for normal tasks)
- prompt: Choose corresponding command based on project type and difficulty

Go project - Difficult task:
  go fmt ./... && go vet ./... && codex review --uncommitted --config model_reasoning_effort=xhigh
  (timeout: 1800000)

Go project - Normal task:
  go fmt ./... && go vet ./... && codex review --uncommitted --config model_reasoning_effort=high
  (timeout: 600000)

Node project - Difficult task:
  npm run lint:fix && codex review --uncommitted --config model_reasoning_effort=xhigh
  (timeout: 1800000)

Node project - Normal task:
  npm run lint:fix && codex review --uncommitted --config model_reasoning_effort=high
  (timeout: 600000)

Python project - Difficult task:
  black . && ruff check --fix . && codex review --uncommitted --config model_reasoning_effort=xhigh
  (timeout: 1800000)

Python project - Normal task:
  black . && ruff check --fix . && codex review --uncommitted --config model_reasoning_effort=high
  (timeout: 600000)

Clean working directory:
  codex review --commit HEAD --config model_reasoning_effort=high
  (timeout: 600000)

    23	## v2 changes vs v1 (調査後の修正、参考)
    24	
    25	| v1 の誤り | v2 の修正 |
    26	|---|---|
    27	| 「Tier 3 で HPKE RFC 9180 vectors を取り込む」 | (v3 で再修正) v2 では「Turnkey HPKE は RFC 9180 でない独自方式」とした上で RFC 9180 vectors を撤回したが、これも誤り。v3 で再評価 |
    28	| proof.ts は scope 外で確定 | proof-tests.ts に**実 enclave 由来の `v1AppProof` / `v1BootProof` JSON ゴールデン**があり、cross-language 借用に最適。**proof ポート要否は別計画**を維持しつつ、本プランで `tests/Fixtures/proofs/` を Tier-1 として置く準備 (verify 実装は別計画) を含める |
    29	| 「他言語 SDK に cross-language vector があるかもしれない」 | 公式 cross-language fixture セットは**存在しない**。代わりに `mockSenderPrivateKey=67ee05fc…` 等のハードコード値が `tkhq/sdk` / `swift-sdk` / `dart-sdk` で**完全一致でコピー**。実質的 reference vector として **Tier-1 で借用** |
    30	| Tier-4 (live) | 維持。live e2e は `tkhq/python-sdk` のみが CI に組み込んでおり、他 SDK は mock 中心 |
    31	
    32	## 1. Intent
    33	
    34	`KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk` が **Turnkey 公式 TypeScript SDK
    35	(@turnkey/{crypto,http,api-key-stamper,encoding} の peak-pinned 版)
    36	と機能的に等価** であることを、後付け的なレビューではなく
    37	**機械検証可能な公式由来テストアセット** で恒常的に担保する。
    38	
    39	本プランは、既存の Codex 3-round 行ごと等価レビュー
    40	(`codex-crypto-reviews/`) と既存の Tier-1 fixture
    41	(`tests/Fixtures/{encoding,crypto,api-key-stamper}/*.json`) を
    42	**置き換えるものではない**。
    43	それらが「**人が読んで一致を確認した**」レベルの保証であるのに対し、
    44	本プランは「**入力に対する観測可能な出力を機械で照合し、
    45	上流が変わったら自動で気付く**」レベルの保証を上乗せする。
    46	
    47	「観測可能な出力」は具体的には以下のいずれか:
    48	
    49	- 決定論経路: 入力が同じなら byte 等価 (例: stamp の DER 署名は
    50	  `purejs` runtime で RFC 6979 deterministic-k、credential-bundle decrypt は
    51	  入力 ciphertext + receiver private key で plaintext が一意)。
    52	- 非決定論経路: ephemeral key/nonce を生成するため byte 等価は取れない
    53	  ものに対しては (a) decrypt round-trip での plaintext 等価、
    54	  (b) 構造的 assertion (フィールド長、ヘッダ、JSON キー順、署名検証成功)。
    55	
    56	## 2. Goals (must-have)
    57	
    58	1. **Coverage matrix**: 公式 `__tests__/*.ts` の各 `test()` ブロックが
    59	   C# のどの `[Fact]` / `[Theory]` メソッドに対応するかを 1:1 で
    60	   ドキュメント化する。欠落は CI で fail する。
    61	2. **Byte-equal fixtures**: 公式 npm パッケージを `npm install` した
    62	   Node 環境で生成した実バイト (stamp, signed-request body,
    63	   credential-bundle decrypt 等) を `tests/Fixtures/**` に固定し、
    64	   C# が同一入力で同一バイトを生成することを assert する。
    65	3. **Standard test vectors (primitives + 条件付きで HPKE)**:
    66	   HKDF (RFC 5869)、ECDSA P-256 deterministic-k (RFC 6979)、
    67	   AES-GCM-256 (NIST CAVP)、SHA-256 (NIST SHS)、HMAC-SHA256 (RFC 4231)、
    68	   Ed25519 (RFC 8032、SOLANA export 用) の **個別 primitive** で C# 実装を検証する。
    69	   secp256k1 SEC2 / Base58Check Bitcoin double-SHA256 もここに含める。
    70	   **HPKE 全体 (RFC 9180) の取り込みは条件付き**:
    71	   PR-7a で 「pinned `@turnkey/crypto@2.8.8` の `hpkeEncrypt` が
    72	   RFC 9180 base mode (DHKEM(P-256,HKDF-SHA256) + HKDF-SHA256 + AES-256-GCM)
    73	   と byte-equal か」を `__tests__/crypto-test.ts` の HPKE 経路を
    74	   実 Node で動かして固定 ephemeral key を inject (もし可能なら) し評価する。
    75	   評価結果が **byte-equal なら RFC 9180 Appendix A vectors を取り込み**、
    76	   **byte-equal でなければ取り込まない** (Tier-2 で SDK 生成 bytes を信頼)。
    77	   ※ JSdoc は RFC 9180 を明示するが ([crypto.ts:88-91](../codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-crypto-2.8.8/ts-source/crypto.ts))、
    78	   実装の suite_id/labels と RFC 9180 base mode の literal が**完全一致するかは未確認**。
    79	   QOS `quorumKeyEncrypt` は C# **未ポート**であり本プラン scope 外
    80	   (Section 2 canonical 説明を参照)。
    81	4. **Drift detection**: 公式 `__tests__/` の sha256 を pin し、
    82	   月次 cron で再取得して差分があれば **upstream-drift というラベルの
    83	   single open issue を idempotent に update/create する**
    84	   (Section 6.4 / Section 8 / Section 9 で一貫した定義)。
    85	   この workflow は **main CI gate ではない** (= PR をブロックしない)。
    86	   issue が立ったら人手で再 pin と対応 C# テスト更新の PR を立てる。
    87	5. **不確定要素の明示**: 公式 P-256 ECDSA が non-deterministic な
    88	   `nodecrypto.ts` ランタイムでは byte-equal にならない、という事実を
    89	   プランで明示し、`purejs` ランタイム相当 (RFC 6979 + low-S) を
    90	   検証スコープと宣言する (これは既に `ApiKeyStamper.cs-codex-findings-reconciliation.md` で
    91	   合意済みの方針)。
    92	
    93	### Non-goals
    94	
    95	- 既存の `codex-crypto-reviews/` SOP の置き換え (補強のみ)。
    96	- nuget.org への公開条件の変更。
    97	- 新規機能 (proof.ts 完全移植、QOS `quorumKeyEncrypt` ポートなど) の追加。
    98	  **proof モジュールに対するポート方針は本プランの第 12 章「未スコープ依存」で別計画とする。**
    99	- 公式 Backend に対する live e2e の必須化 (live 経路は opt-in のまま)。
   100	
   101	### 2.1. 暗号構成の canonical 用語 (重要)
   102	
   103	以下の用語は本プラン全体で **canonical** にこの定義で使う。他章 (3, 4, 6.3, 9, 10, 12) は
   104	**この章を再記述せず参照する**。
   105	
   106	- **SDK HPKE**: pinned `@turnkey/crypto@2.8.8` の `hpkeEncrypt` / `hpkeDecrypt` /
   107	  `hpkeAuthEncrypt` 経路。([crypto.ts:88-203](../codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-crypto-2.8.8/ts-source/crypto.ts))
   108	  - JSdoc が RFC 9180 を明示。
   109	  - `SUITE_ID_1 = "KEM\0\x10"` (DHKEM(P-256, HKDF-SHA256))、
   110	    `SUITE_ID_2 = "HPKE\0\x10\0\x01\0\x02"` (kem_id=0x0010, kdf_id=0x0001, aead_id=0x0002)
   111	    の literal を使う ([Crypto.cs:77-79](../src/Crypto.cs))。
   112	  - これらの suite_id literal は **RFC 9180 base mode の値と一致**:
   113	    `kem_id=0x0010 = DHKEM(P-256, HKDF-SHA256)`,
   114	    `kdf_id=0x0001 = HKDF-SHA256`, `aead_id=0x0002 = AES-256-GCM`。
   115	    `extractAndExpand(..., 32)` で 32-byte AES key、`extractAndExpand(..., 12)` で
   116	    12-byte IV を派生するのも AES-256-GCM の使用と整合。
   117	  - ただし上記 suite_id 一致は「実装が RFC 9180 と完全互換」を即座に意味しない。
   118	    HPKE label の literal バイト列 (`HPKE-v1`, `eae_prk`, `secret`, `shared_secret`)
   119	    も RFC 9180 と完全一致するかは PR-7a で確認する。
   120	  - **C# `Turnkey.Crypto.HpkeEncrypt` / `HpkeDecrypt` がポートしているのはこの経路のみ**。
   121	    ([Crypto.cs:404-456](../src/Crypto.cs))。
   122	- **QOS encryption**: 同じファイルの `quorumKeyEncrypt` ([crypto.ts:219+](../codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-crypto-2.8.8/ts-source/crypto.ts))。
   123	  - jsdoc に「Algorithm originally implemented in qos」と明示。
   124	  - `QOS_ENCRYPTION_HMAC_MESSAGE = "qos_encryption_hmac_message"`、
   125	    SHA-512 HMAC + AES-GCM-256、borsh serialization。
   126	  - **C# **未ポート**。本プラン scope 外**。
   127	- **RFC 9180**: IETF Hybrid Public Key Encryption 仕様。SDK HPKE と完全一致するかは
   128	  PR-7a で評価する別タスク。「SDK HPKE = RFC 9180 と等価」とは現時点で言わない。
   129	
   130	### 2.2. C# が ports している upstream 経路の一覧 (Non-Goal 確認用)
   131	
   132	| C# public API | upstream 関数 | upstream 経路 | C# port 状況 |
   133	|---|---|---|---|
   134	| `Turnkey.Crypto.HpkeEncrypt` | `hpkeEncrypt` | SDK HPKE (RFC 9180 を意図) | **済** |
   135	| `Turnkey.Crypto.HpkeDecrypt` | `hpkeDecrypt` | SDK HPKE | **済** |
   136	| `Turnkey.Crypto.DecryptCredentialBundle` | `decryptCredentialBundle` | SDK HPKE + base58check + AES-GCM | **済** |
   137	| `Turnkey.Crypto.DecryptExportBundle` | `decryptExportBundle` | SDK HPKE + mnemonic/PKCS#8 | **済** |
   138	| `Turnkey.Crypto.EncryptPrivateKeyToBundle` | `encryptPrivateKeyToBundle` | SDK HPKE + base58check | **済** |
   139	| (なし) | `quorumKeyEncrypt` (QOS) | QOS 独自 | **未ポート (scope 外)** |
   140	| (なし) | `verify` / `verifyAppProofSignature` (proof) | P-256/P-384 + COSE/X.509 | **未ポート (proof scope 外)** |
   141	
   142	## 3. 現状アセスメント (Where we are)
   143	
   144	| 項目 | 既存状態 | 備考 |
   145	|---|---|---|
   146	| Upstream pinned snapshots | 4 パッケージ (`crypto@2.8.8`, `http@3.16.0`, `api-key-stamper@0.5.0`, `encoding@0.6.0`) を `codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/` に tarball + sha256 で固定 | [turnkey-source-pins.md](../codex-crypto-reviews/turnkey-source-pins.md) |
   147	| Tier-1 hand-transcribed fixtures | `tests/Fixtures/{encoding,crypto,api-key-stamper}/turnkey-*-vectors.json` の 3 ファイル。`_provenance` メタデータと `_source_line` 付き | `tests/Fixtures/http/` は**未整備** |
   148	| 3-round Codex review | 6 ファイル全部 review-clean、`FINAL-INTEGRATED-REVIEW-20260523.md` で v0.1.0-alpha GO 済み | [FINAL-INTEGRATED-REVIEW-20260523.md](../codex-crypto-reviews/FINAL-INTEGRATED-REVIEW-20260523.md) |
   149	| C# test 数 (合計約 113 `[Fact]/[Theory]`) | Encoding 48 / Crypto ~45 / Stamper 10 / Http 11 | 公式 (~30 `test()`) より細かいが、対応マッピングは未文書化 |
   150	| Drift 検知 | `tarball-checksums.txt` のみ。`__tests__/*.ts` 自体の sha256 pin は無し | 公式テスト更新時に気付かないリスク |
   151	| Node 生成 byte fixture | **なし** (`tests/Fixtures/Generators/` 未作成) | `Tier-1 README.md` に「node-generated 予定」と明記済み |
   152	| RFC / NIST vectors | HKDF RFC 5869 A1-A3 のみ (`tests/CryptoTests.cs:91/111/149`) | HPKE 9180、ECDSA 6979 単独、AES-GCM CAVP は未取り込み |
   153	
   154	### 公式テストの実状 (2026-05-27 時点・調査済み)
   155	
   156	公式 `__tests__/*.ts` は **`__fixtures__/api-key.{private,public,public.pem}`**
   157	というローカルファイルを `readFixture()` で読む構造で、
   158	他言語に直接持ち込める JSON 形式の test vector dataset は**公開されていない**。
   159	npm tarball にはテストもフィクスチャも含まれないため、
   160	**GitHub の `tkhq/sdk` リポジトリの該当タグからコピーする**のが唯一の入口。
   161	これは既存の `upstream-snapshots/.../ts-source/__fixtures__/` で対応済み。
   162	
   163	公式テストの assertion 強度は (1) DER ECDSA 検証 + (2) スキーム文字列 +
   164	(3) JSON キー順 + (4) publicKey 等価 のみ。**バイト等価 snapshot は無い**
   165	(P-256 `nodecrypto.ts` は random-k なため bytes が毎回変わる)。
   166	したがって C# 側で「`purejs` 等価のバイト」を追加で検証することは、
   167	**公式テストより厳しい superset の検証**になる (=価値が高い)。
   168	
   169	#### 公式他言語 SDK の検証スタイル (調査結果)
   170	
   171	- **cross-language fixture セットは存在しない**。
   172	  代わりに `mockSenderPrivateKey="67ee05fc..."`、
   173	  `mockPrivateKey="20fa65df..."`、`mockCredentialBundle="w99a5xV6..."`、
   174	  ニーモニック `"leaf lady until indicate praise final route toast cake minimum insect unknown"`、
   175	  PEM 鍵 `487f361d…0213c` / 圧縮公開鍵 `02f739f8…0316` が
   176	  **`tkhq/sdk` / `swift-sdk` / `dart-sdk` の 3 レポで完全一致のコピー**で
   177	  共有されており、実質的な reference vector になっている。
   178	  → C# でも同じ hex / mnemonic を使えば、3 言語と機械的に三角検証できる。
   179	- **`tkhq/sdk/packages/crypto/src/__tests__/proof-tests.ts`** には
   180	  **実 enclave が発行した複数の `v1AppProof` / `v1BootProof` JSON**
   181	  がフルで埋め込み済。署名検証ロジックの cross-language ゴールデン
   182	  として現状最高品質。
   183	- **`tkhq/go-sdk/pkg/enclave_encrypt/encrypt_test.go::TestP256Verify`**
   184	  は `// Values generated by rust code` コメント付きの **Go↔Rust の
   185	  cross-language ECDSA vector**。「ある言語の出力を別言語の入力に使う」
   186	  という稀有な明示例。
   187	- **`tkhq/qos/src/qos_p256/SPEC.md`** は **QOS encryption の独自仕様書**
   188	  (SDK HPKE とは別経路。Section 2.1 参照)。
   189	  ECDH(P-256) → HMAC-SHA512 で AES-GCM-256 の key を派生、
   190	  `QOS_ENCRYPTION_HMAC_MESSAGE` 定数、nonce 12B など、
   191	  **RFC 9180 とは互換性のない独自構成**。
   192	  C# は QOS をポートしておらず本プラン scope 外。
   193	- 公式 backend に対する live e2e を CI に組み込んでいるのは
   194	  `tkhq/python-sdk` のみ。他はすべて mocked。
   195	
   196	## 4. 既存の検証ギャップ (Why this plan)
   197	
   198	GAP-1. **Coverage matrix 不在** — 公式 `test("...")` と C# `[Fact]` Method の
   199	       対応表が無く、公式が test を追加したときに C# 側で漏れる。
   200	GAP-2. **HTTP fixture 不在** — `tests/Fixtures/http/turnkey-http-vectors.json`
   201	       が無い ([Http.cs-codex-findings-reconciliation.md セクション F](../codex-crypto-reviews/Http.cs-codex-findings-reconciliation.md))。
   202	GAP-3. **Node 生成バイト fixture 不在** — `Generators/` 機構が無いので
   203	       `purejs` モードで実 Node が吐く DER 署名や `SignedRequest.body`
   204	       バイトと C# 出力を比較できない。
   205	GAP-4. **Drift 検知 (テスト側) 不在** — `__tests__/*.ts` 自体の sha256 が
   206	       pin されていない。上流テスト更新を catch できない。
   207	GAP-5. **Primitive 単独ベクトル不足** — HKDF 以外 (ECDSA P-256 RFC 6979 単独・
   208	       AES-GCM-256 NIST CAVP・HMAC-SHA256 RFC 4231・SHA-256 NIST SHS・
   209	       Ed25519 RFC 8032・secp256k1 SEC2・Base58Check Bitcoin double-SHA256) の
   210	       単体テストが無い。SDK HPKE 全体 (RFC 9180 互換性は未確認、Section 2.1 参照)
   211	       の取り込みは PR-7a の評価結果次第とし、それまでは primitives 単独ベクトル
   212	       でカバーする。
   213	GAP-6. **proof モジュール非対応** — `crypto/proof.ts` (129 行) と
   214	       `proof-tests.ts` (実 enclave 由来の JSON ゴールデン) が C# に
   215	       存在しない。**proof のポート要否は別計画**だが、本プランでは
   216	       「ゴールデン JSON を Fixture 側に取り込む準備」 (実コード非実装) は
   217	       含める。proof 検証は ECDSA P-256 + base64url 復号で実現できるため、
   218	       既存 C# プリミティブで verify ロジックだけ書ける見込みが立つかは
   219	       別プランで判定する。
   220	GAP-7. **他言語 SDK との同名 hex 値共有が活用されていない** —
   221	       `mockSenderPrivateKey` 等の同名定数が 3 言語で完全一致。
   222	       これを C# 側でも採用すれば三角検証ができるが、現状ローカルで
   223	       別の値を生成しているテストがある (例: `Hpke_EncryptThenDecrypt_RoundTripsArbitraryPayload`)。
   224	
   225	## 5. 検証戦略 (4 Tier)
   226	
   227	```
   228	Tier 1: Upstream-transcribed JSON vectors    [PARTIAL — encoding/crypto/stamper のみ]
   229	        ↑ どこから来た値か Provenance 必須
   230	Tier 2: Node-generated byte snapshots        [NEW]
   231	        ↑ 公式 npm を実 Node で動かして固定。`purejs` ランタイム選択
   232	Tier 3: Standard RFC / NIST vectors          [NEW (HKDF を除き)]
   233	        ↑ 上流が間違うリスクの保険
   234	Tier 4: Live backend (opt-in)                [既存スキップ条件付き]
   235	        ↑ env 変数があるときのみ
   236	```
   237	
   238	各 Tier の **provenance** を `tests/Fixtures/README.md` のレベル分類
   239	(`upstream-test-vectors` / `node-generated` / `rfc` / `nist` /
   240	`turnkey-sample`) で必ず明示する。
   241	
   242	## 6. 設計 — コンポーネント分解
   243	
   244	### 6.1 Coverage matrix generator (新規)
   245	
   246	**目的**: 公式 `__tests__/*.ts` の `test()/it()` ブロック名一覧と、
   247	C# テストの `[Fact]` メソッド名一覧をクロス参照し、対応表を生成する。
   248	
   249	**実装案**: TypeScript ではなく **POSIX `awk` + dotnet test 一覧** のシェル
   250	スクリプト1本で実装する。理由: 既存リポジトリに Node ランタイムへの
   251	依存が無く、`codex-crypto-review.sh` も pure shell。一貫性を保つ。
   252	
   253	ファイル:
   254	- `codex-crypto-reviews/coverage-map.sh` — 解析スクリプト
   255	- `codex-crypto-reviews/coverage-map.tsv` — 生成結果 (上流 test 名 \t C# メソッド名 \t 状態)
   256	- `codex-crypto-reviews/coverage-map.md` — レビュー用 markdown レンダリング
   257	
   258	**マッピング規約 (人手部分)**:
   259	- C# テストメソッドの XML doc コメントに `/// upstream: <file>:line "<test name>"`
   260	  を 1 行付ける。スクリプトはこれを正として読む。

exec
/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba plans/PLAN-EQUIVALENCE-VERIFICATION.md | sed -n '261,560p'" in /Users/takeshi/Kyuzan/src/turnkey-sdk-csharp/.claude/worktrees/laughing-hertz-048cd4
 succeeded in 0ms:
   261	- 上流 `test()` 名 → C# メソッド名の 1:N マッピングを許容
   262	  (例: 公式 `pointDecode -> uncompressed valid` は C# で
   263	  `UncompressRawPublicKey_UpstreamVector_Valid_*` 等に細分化される)。
   264	- どの C# テストにも紐付かない上流 test は `MISSING` で出力。
   265	
   266	**CI gate**:
   267	```bash
   268	./codex-crypto-reviews/coverage-map.sh --check
   269	# exit non-zero if any MISSING row present.
   270	```
   271	
   272	### 6.1.1 PR-3 候補テスト一覧 (Codex r1 で列挙された欠落 / N/A 必須)
   273	
   274	PR-3 で追加 or 明示的に `N/A` マッピングが必要な上流テスト
   275	(`codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/.../__tests__/`):
   276	
   277	| 上流 file | 上流 test 名 | C# 側の現状 |
   278	|---|---|---|
   279	| `api-key-stamper/elliptic-curves-test.ts` | `pointDecode -> uncompressed invalid` | 似た振る舞いは `CryptoTests.UncompressRawPublicKey_BadPrefix_Throws` 等にあるが明示マップ要 |
   280	| 同 | `pointDecode -> uncompressed valid` | 同上 |
   281	| 同 | `pointDecode -> compressed` | 同上 |
   282	| `api-key-stamper/signature-test.ts` | `sign with Turnkey fixture: sign (node crypto)` | C# 側 N/A (`nodecrypto.ts` runtime は port しない) |
   283	| 同 | `sign with Turnkey fixture: sign (WebCrypto)` | C# 側 N/A (同) |
   284	| 同 | `sign with Turnkey fixture: sign (PureJS)` | `ApiKeyStamperTests.SignWithApiKey_DeterministicWithRfc6979` 等にマップ |
   285	| 同 | `sign with Turnkey fixture: sign (universal)` | C# 側 N/A |
   286	| 同 | `sign with openssl generated key pairs: stamp (node/WebCrypto/universal)` | 各 N/A 理由を明示 |
   287	| `api-key-stamper/stamp-test.ts` | `uses provided signature to make stamp` | `ApiKeyStamperTests.Stamp_UpstreamFixture_ProducesValidWireBytes` にマップ |
   288	| `crypto/crypto-test.ts` | `hpkeAuthEncrypt and hpkeDecrypt - end-to-end encryption and decryption` | C# Auth モード未確認、PR-3 で対応要 |
   289	| 同 | `hpkeEncrypt and hpkeDecrypt - standard mode (ephemeral sender key)` | `CryptoTests.Hpke_EncryptThenDecrypt_RoundTripsArbitraryPayload` にマップ |
   290	| 同 | `decryptExportBundle ... mnemonic` | 未対応、PR-3 で追加 |
   291	| 同 | `decryptExportBundle ... non-mnemonic` | 未対応 |
   292	| 同 | `getPublicKey/generateP256KeyPair/compressRawPublicKey/decryptCredentialBundle` 各 | 既存マップあり |
   293	| 同 | `extractPrivateKeyFromPKCS8Bytes` | 未対応 (PKCS#8 経路の単体テスト) |
   294	| 同 | `verifyRequestStamp` | 未対応、PR-3 で対応要 |
   295	| 同 | `uncompressRawPublicKey` happy/invalid prefix/invalid length | 既存マップあり (`Uncompress*Tests`) |
   296	| 同 | DER parser 14 ケース (2 valid at `crypto-test.ts:263-282` + 12 invalid/edge at `:287-454`) | 既存 DER 関連 tests と要 1:1 mapping (Codex r2 が pinned snapshot で確認した実数) |
   297	| 同 | `Session JWT signature: verifies the provided JWT against its public key` | `CryptoTests.VerifySessionJwtSignature_*` にマップ |
   298	| `crypto/proof-tests.ts` | `should verify valid app proof signatures` | C# 側 N/A (proof 未ポート、Fixture のみ PR-11) |
   299	| 同 | `should verify correct app proof / boot proof combos` | C# 側 N/A |
   300	| 同 | `should NOT verify with malformed app proofs` | C# 側 N/A |
   301	| 同 | `should NOT verify with malformed boot proofs` | C# 側 N/A |
   302	| `http/async-test.ts` | `withAsyncPolling` 6 ケース | C# 側 N/A (peak monorepo は `withAsyncPolling` 経路を使わない方針を確認要 → Phase A) |
   303	| `http/request-test.ts` | `requests are stamped after initialization` | C# 側 `HttpTests.Stamp_*` 群にマップ |
   304	| 同 | `requests return grpc status details as part of their errors` | C# 側 N/A 検討 (peak monorepo の error 表面実装を確認) |
   305	| `encoding/index-test.ts` | 5 ケース全部 | 既存 EncodingTests にマップ済 |
   306	
   307	すべて `N/A` を出すには **理由テキスト** を `coverage-map.tsv` に書く義務を課す
   308	(空 N/A は不可、CI で `awk` でブロック)。
   309	
   310	### 6.2 Node-generated fixture generator (新規)
   311	
   312	**目的**: pinned npm パッケージを実 Node で動かし、
   313	C# が再現すべきバイト列を JSON にスナップショットする。
   314	
   315	ディレクトリ:
   316	```
   317	tests/Fixtures/Generators/
   318	├── package.json                — pinned exact versions, no semver range
   319	├── package-lock.json           — committed (lock transitive deps)
   320	├── generate-http-vectors.mjs   — emits tests/Fixtures/http/turnkey-http-vectors.json
   321	├── generate-stamper-vectors.mjs — emits tests/Fixtures/api-key-stamper/turnkey-stamper-node-vectors.json
   322	├── generate-crypto-vectors.mjs  — emits tests/Fixtures/crypto/turnkey-crypto-node-vectors.json
   323	└── README.md                    — Node version pin, reproduction steps, output sha256
   324	```
   325	
   326	**重要な決定 (v3 改訂)**:
   327	
   328	- **決定論経路のみ byte snapshot を取る**:
   329	  - `ApiKeyStamper.stamp({ runtimeOverride: "purejs" })` の出力 (RFC 6979 + low-S)。
   330	  - `decryptCredentialBundle(ciphertext, embeddedKey)` の plaintext (受信側演算なので決定論)。
   331	  - `decryptExportBundle(...)` の plaintext。
   332	  - `SignedRequest.body` の JSON.stringify bytes (stamp signature を含まないので決定論)。
   333	- **非決定論経路は byte snapshot を取らない**:
   334	  - `hpkeEncrypt`, `hpkeAuthEncrypt`, `quorumKeyEncrypt` (現状 scope 外) は
   335	    ephemeral key/nonce を内部生成。**byte 等価検証は撤回**。
   336	  - 代わりに「encrypt → decrypt round-trip で plaintext 等価」と
   337	    「encrypt 出力の構造的 assertion (encapsulated key 長 33, ciphertext 長,
   338	    AAD 構成)」を C# 側で確認する。
   339	  - **追加調査**: pinned `crypto.ts` を grep して `hpkeEncrypt` に
   340	    ephemeral key を外から inject できる private path があるか確認。
   341	    あれば限定的に byte snapshot を復活する。なければ前述方針で確定。
   342	- `purejs` 確実化のための **pre-flight test in generator**:
   343	  - Generator 起動時に **既知ベクトル**
   344	    (`api-key.private` を `purejs.sign("hello from TKHQ!")` した既知 DER 16 進)
   345	    を実行し、`@noble/curves@1.3.0` の transitive resolution が
   346	    low-S RFC 6979 を実際に出すことを assert。失敗したら exit non-zero。
   347	- 入力は **公式 `__fixtures__/api-key.{private,public}` をそのまま使う**。
   348	  Crypto-test.ts の `decryptCredentialBundle` ベクトルも同様に流用。
   349	- 生成スクリプトは **新たに値を作らない**。既存の固定された入力で
   350	  「公式が吐くであろうバイト」を確定するだけ。
   351	- 出力 JSON は `_provenance` で
   352	  `{ level: "node-generated", node_version, npm_lockfile_sha256, generator_sha256, output_sha256, transitive_lock_sha256 }`
   353	  を必ず記録。`transitive_lock_sha256` は `npm ls --json` の sha256 で
   354	  `@noble/curves` の解決バージョン drift を検知。
   355	
   356	**CI 統合**:
   357	- 通常 CI では fixture を**再生成しない**。生成済み JSON を read-only で
   358	  使う (Node 不在環境でもテストが走る)。
   359	- 月 1 回 (`schedule: cron`) または手動 `workflow_dispatch` で
   360	  fixture 再生成 + diff チェックを別ワークフロー
   361	  (`.github/workflows/fixture-regen.yml`) で実行。差分が出たら PR を起こす。
   362	- `tests/Fixtures/Generators/` 配下は **csproj から除外**:
   363	  PR-4 で `tests/turnkey-sdk-csharp.Tests.csproj` (現在 line 23-26 の
   364	  `<None Include="Fixtures\**\*">` ItemGroup) を以下のいずれかに修正する:
   365	  ```xml
   366	  <None Include="Fixtures\**\*"
   367	        Exclude="Fixtures\Generators\**"
   368	        CopyToOutputDirectory="PreserveNewest" />
   369	  <Content Remove="Fixtures\Generators\**" />
   370	  <None Remove="Fixtures\Generators\**\*.json"
   371	        Condition="false" /> <!-- 念のための明示的 None Remove (no-op) -->
   372	  ```
   373	  最低でも `Exclude="Fixtures\Generators\**"` と
   374	  `<Content Remove="Fixtures\Generators\**" />` の両方を必須とし、
   375	  `dotnet build` が `Generators/` 配下の `.mjs` / `package.json` / `node_modules`
   376	  を巻き込まないことを `dotnet build -bl` で確認する。
   377	  これは **PR-4 のスコープ**に含める (Codex r1/r2 指摘)。
   378	
   379	### 6.3 標準テストベクトル取り込み (primitives + 条件付き HPKE)
   380	
   381	(canonical 用語は Section 2.1 を参照。)
   382	
   383	#### 6.3.1 必須 primitives ベクトル
   384	
   385	ファイル配置:
   386	```
   387	tests/Fixtures/rfc/
   388	├── hkdf-rfc5869/                  — A.1, A.2, A.3 (既存 CryptoTests.cs と同期)
   389	│   ├── README.md
   390	│   └── vectors.json
   391	├── ecdsa-p256-rfc6979/            — Appendix A.2.5 (P-256, SHA-256)
   392	│   ├── README.md
   393	│   └── vectors.json
   394	├── hmac-sha256-rfc4231/           — Section 4 test cases 1-7
   395	│   ├── README.md                    (SDK HPKE が HKDF-SHA256 内で使う HMAC-SHA256)
   396	│   └── vectors.json
   397	└── ed25519-rfc8032/               — Section 7.1 test cases (SOLANA export 経路で使用)
   398	    ├── README.md
   399	    └── vectors.json
   400	tests/Fixtures/nist/
   401	├── aes-gcm-cavp/                  — KeySize=128/256, TagSize=128, IV=96bit
   402	│   ├── README.md                    (HPKE は 128bit AES、credential bundle は 256bit AES の可能性あり、両方カバー)
   403	│   └── vectors.json
   404	├── ecdsa-p256-sigver-fips186-4/   — FIPS 186-4 SigVer (P-256, SHA-256)
   405	│   ├── README.md
   406	│   └── vectors.json
   407	└── sha-256-shs-bytevectors/       — NIST SHS Byte test vectors
   408	    ├── README.md
   409	    └── vectors.json
   410	tests/Fixtures/sec/                — secp256k1 関連 (`uncompressRawPublicKey(curve=secp256k1)` のため)
   411	└── secp256k1-sec2/
   412	    ├── README.md
   413	    └── vectors.json
   414	tests/Fixtures/bitcoin/            — Base58Check Bitcoin double-SHA256 known addresses
   415	└── base58check-bip39/
   416	    ├── README.md
   417	    └── vectors.json
   418	```
   419	
   420	#### 6.3.2 条件付き: HPKE RFC 9180 ベクトル
   421	
   422	**判定 step (PR-7a)**:
   423	1. pinned `@turnkey/crypto@2.8.8` の `hpkeEncrypt` を、固定 ephemeral key を
   424	   inject できる経路があるか調べる (`grep -n "ephemeralKeyPair" crypto.ts`)。
   425	2. 注入できない場合は、Node generator から `hpkeEncrypt` をオーバーライド
   426	   (関数 wrapping) して固定 ephemeral key を渡せるかを確認。
   427	3. 確認できれば、RFC 9180 Appendix A.4 (DHKEM(P-256, HKDF-SHA256), HKDF-SHA256,
   428	   AES-256-GCM) の test vector を `tests/Fixtures/rfc/hpke-rfc9180/` に取り込む。
   429	4. **C# 側が同じ ephemeral key 注入で**同 byte を出すか assert する。
   430	5. 一致しない場合は本仕様の差分点 (suite_id, label, info 順序等) を
   431	   `codex-crypto-reviews/sdk-hpke-vs-rfc9180.md` に文書化し、RFC 9180 ベクトル
   432	   取り込みは見送る。Tier-2 で SDK 生成 bytes を信頼。
   433	
   434	PR-7a の評価が完了するまでは Tier-3 HPKE ベクトルは入れない。
   435	
   436	#### 6.3.3 抜粋方針
   437	
   438	フル CAVP / SHS テストファイル (数千〜数万行) はコミットせず、
   439	**SDK 経路で実際に使われる組合せ** だけを `vectors.json` に切り出す。
   440	**原 CAVP ファイル URL + SHA256 + 切り出し範囲**を README に明示する。
   441	
   442	#### 6.3.4 実装
   443	
   444	`tests/CryptoTests.cs` / `tests/EncodingTests.cs` に既存の `Hkdf_Rfc5869_A1`
   445	パターンで `EcdsaP256_Rfc6979_A25_<msg>`, `HmacSha256_Rfc4231_TC<n>`,
   446	`Ed25519_Rfc8032_TC<n>`, `AesGcm_Nist_<id>`, `Sha256_Nist_<id>`,
   447	`Secp256k1_Sec2_<id>`, `Base58Check_Bitcoin_<id>` を追加。
   448	Tier 3 は **SDK 実装が組み立てに使う primitives が RFC/NIST 仕様に
   449	従っていることの独立証明**である。SDK HPKE 全体の構造的正しさは
   450	Tier-2 (Node 生成 / round-trip) と (条件付きで) Tier-3 HPKE が担当する。
   451	
   452	### 6.4 上流テストの sha256 pin と drift 検知 (新規)
   453	
   454	ファイル:
   455	- `codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/test-file-checksums.txt` —
   456	  各 `__tests__/*.ts` と `__fixtures__/*` の sha256。
   457	- `.github/workflows/upstream-drift.yml` — 月次 cron で
   458	  GitHub の `tkhq/sdk` 該当タグから `__tests__/` をフェッチ (npm tarball には
   459	  test が無いので、`gh api repos/tkhq/sdk/contents/...?ref=<sha>`) し、
   460	  pin 済 sha256 と比較。差分があれば issue を**idempotent に**起票/更新。
   461	
   462	**Idempotency rule (Codex r1 指摘の解消)**:
   463	
   464	```yaml
   465	# 既存の open issue を 1 つ取得して再利用する
   466	- name: Find or create drift issue
   467	  env:
   468	    GH_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
   469	    DRIFT_LABEL: upstream-drift
   470	    PACKAGE: ${{ matrix.package }}
   471	  run: |
   472	    BODY=$(cat drift-report.md)
   473	    # ラベル + パッケージ名で 1 issue に固定
   474	    EXISTING=$(gh issue list --state open \
   475	      --label "$DRIFT_LABEL" --search "in:title $PACKAGE" \
   476	      --json number --jq '.[0].number // empty')
   477	    if [[ -n "$EXISTING" ]]; then
   478	      gh issue edit "$EXISTING" --body "$BODY"
   479	      gh issue comment "$EXISTING" --body "Re-detected on $(date -u +%FT%TZ)."
   480	    else
   481	      gh issue create --label "$DRIFT_LABEL" \
   482	        --title "Upstream drift: $PACKAGE" --body "$BODY"
   483	    fi
   484	```
   485	
   486	**ポリシー**: 上流テストファイルが変わっていた時、
   487	1. 該当 C# テスト・fixture を更新する PR を作る (人手)。
   488	2. coverage-map.sh の `MISSING` 行が増えていないか確認する。
   489	3. 再 pin と Codex 3-round review を再実行する。
   490	
   491	これにより、上流が test を追加したのに C# 側で気付かない、を防ぐ。
   492	かつ「同じ drift で月ごとに新 issue が無限に増える」も防ぐ。
   493	
   494	### 6.5 HTTP 等価性検証 (Tier-2 で吸収)
   495	
   496	`tests/Fixtures/http/turnkey-http-vectors.json` の中身:
   497	```json
   498	{
   499	  "_provenance": {
   500	    "level": "node-generated",
   501	    "generator": "tests/Fixtures/Generators/generate-http-vectors.mjs",
   502	    "node_version": "20.x.y",
   503	    "npm_lockfile_sha256": "...",
   504	    "output_sha256": "...",
   505	    "note": "@turnkey/http@3.16.0 + @turnkey/api-key-stamper@0.5.0 (purejs) で生成。stamp の signature は RFC 6979 deterministic-k なため byte 一意。"
   506	  },
   507	  "stampGetWhoami": [
   508	    {
   509	      "input": { "organizationId": "<UUID>", "baseUrl": "https://api.turnkey.com", "apiPrivateKey": "<hex>", "apiPublicKey": "<hex>" },
   510	      "expectedSignedRequest": {
   511	        "url": "...",
   512	        "body": "...",         // JSON.stringify そのもの (改行・スペース無し)
   513	        "stampHeaderName": "X-Stamp",
   514	        "stampHeaderValue": "<base64url>"
   515	      }
   516	    }
   517	  ],
   518	  "stampInitImportPrivateKey": [ /* ... */ ],
   519	  "stampImportPrivateKey":     [ /* ... */ ],
   520	  "stampExportPrivateKey":     [ /* ... */ ],
   521	  "stampExportWalletAccount":  [ /* ... */ ]
   522	}
   523	```
   524	
   525	C# 側 (`HttpTests.cs`) の追加 assert:
   526	- `signedRequest.body` (UTF-8 bytes) が**完全一致**。
   527	- `signedRequest.stampHeaderValue` を base64url-decode → JSON 復元 →
   528	  キー順 `["publicKey","scheme","signature"]` 一致。
   529	- `signature` の DER 16 進文字列が**完全一致** (purejs deterministic 前提)。
   530	
   531	これにより、既存の `HttpTests.Stamp_HeaderValueDecodesAndVerifies` の
   532	「DER 形式と検証だけ」というギャップ
   533	([Http.cs-codex-findings-reconciliation.md F](../codex-crypto-reviews/Http.cs-codex-findings-reconciliation.md))
   534	を埋める。
   535

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	# Test fixtures
     2	
     3	Each subdirectory groups fixtures for one production file, plus a
     4	provenance note explaining where the bytes came from.
     5	
     6	## Provenance levels
     7	
     8	- **upstream-test-vectors** — directly copied from the upstream
     9	  `__tests__/` directory inside `codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/`.
    10	- **rfc** — standardized test vectors (RFC 5869, RFC 9180, etc.).
    11	- **nist** — NIST CAVP P-256 vectors.
    12	- **turnkey-sample** — sample bundles published by Turnkey in their
    13	  developer docs (de-identified).
    14	- **node-generated** — bytes generated by running the pinned upstream Node
    15	  package inside `tests/Fixtures/Generators/`. The generator script,
    16	  Node version, and output hash are recorded so reviewers can re-run.
    17	
    18	## Layout
    19	
    20	```
    21	Fixtures/
    22	├── encoding/
    23	│   └── turnkey-encoding-vectors.json       — upstream-test-vectors
    24	├── crypto/                                  — (added with Crypto.cs port)
    25	├── api-key-stamper/                         — (added with ApiKeyStamper.cs port)
    26	└── http/                                    — (added with Http.cs port)
    27	```
    28	
    29	## Re-generating
    30	
    31	Fixtures sourced from upstream test files are stable as long as
    32	[`codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/`](../../codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/)
    33	is not bumped. If a pin is bumped, re-extract the upstream `__tests__/`
    34	into the matching fixture file and update its sha256 in
    35	`tarball-checksums.txt` next to the new tarball.

/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba plans/PLAN-EQUIVALENCE-VERIFICATION.md | sed -n '560,980p'" in /Users/takeshi/Kyuzan/src/turnkey-sdk-csharp/.claude/worktrees/laughing-hertz-048cd4
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	# ApiKeyStamper.cs — Codex findings reconciliation
     2	
     3	After 3 rounds of Codex review on `src/ApiKeyStamper.cs`, two findings recur
     4	across all rounds. This document records why each is **not an actual logic
     5	divergence** so that future reviewers can move past them without re-litigation.
     6	
     7	## E1 — "Runtime parity ambiguity"
     8	
     9	**Codex claim:** C# always uses the deterministic `purejs`-style ECDSA path.
    10	Upstream `ApiKeyStamper.stamp()` with no `runtimeOverride` detects Node and
    11	dispatches to `nodecrypto.ts`, which produces non-deterministic signatures.
    12	
    13	**Reconciliation:** This is by design and is documented in the class XML doc
    14	on `src/ApiKeyStamper.cs`. All three upstream runtimes (`browser`, `node`,
    15	`purejs`) emit P-256 ECDSA signatures that verify under the same public key
    16	against `SHA-256(content)`. The Turnkey API backend accepts any valid such
    17	signature; the runtime choice is an implementation detail of the upstream
    18	package, not part of the wire contract. Byte-level parity with the upstream
    19	*default-in-Node* runtime is **impossible** because `nodecrypto.ts` uses
    20	non-deterministic `k`. The C# port mirrors the upstream `purejs` runtime
    21	(`runtimeOverride: "purejs"`) explicitly so that signatures are reproducible
    22	across builds, which is the engineering value.
    23	
    24	End-to-end wire compatibility is verified by
    25	`ApiKeyStamperTests.Stamp_UpstreamFixture_ProducesValidWireBytes`, which
    26	crypto-verifies the C#-produced DER signature against the upstream
    27	`api-key.public` fixture.
    28	
    29	## E2 — "Low-S clamp may not match upstream noble v1"
    30	
    31	**Codex claim:** `@noble/curves@1.3.0` defaults `lowS: false`, so the
    32	upstream `purejs.ts` call `p256.sign(hash, privateKey)` would emit high-S
    33	signatures, whereas the C# port forces low-S. Codex gave a concrete byte
    34	example.
    35	
    36	**Reconciliation:** The claim is contradicted by the noble v1.3.0 source.
    37	Two independent fetches of
    38	`https://github.com/paulmillr/noble-curves/blob/1.3.0/src/abstract/weierstrass.ts`
    39	both show:
    40	
    41	```ts
    42	return Object.freeze({ lowS: true, ...opts } as const);
    43	// ... and ...
    44	const defaultSigOpts: SignOpts = { lowS: CURVE.lowS, prehash: false };
    45	// ... and inside sign() ...
    46	let { lowS, prehash, extraEntropy: ent } = opts;
    47	if (lowS == null) lowS = true; // RFC6979 3.2
    48	```
    49	
    50	`CURVE.lowS` resolves to `true` because `validateOpts({...})` defaults
    51	`lowS: true`. The sign opts further fall back to `lowS = true` when the
    52	caller passes no opts.
    53	
    54	Therefore, the upstream `purejs.ts` path **does** produce low-S signatures,
    55	and the C# port matches that exactly.
    56	
    57	The Codex r3 byte example
    58	("Noble-compatible purejs emitted high-S DER `304602...b03f...`,
    59	while C# would normalize to low-S DER `304502...4fc0...`") is internally
    60	inconsistent: a faithful purejs invocation at noble v1.3.0 emits the low-S
    61	form, not the high-S form.
    62	
    63	## E3 — Constructor null tolerance (resolved in r2)
    64	
    65	Constructor now accepts null without throwing, matching upstream's
    66	field-assign-only constructor. No further action.
    67	
    68	## E4 — Null payload guard (kept defensive)
    69	
    70	`Stamp(null)` and `SignWithApiKey(null)` throw `ArgumentNullException`.
    71	Upstream lets the failure surface from downstream JS hashing/signing. The
    72	C# port keeps the explicit guard because:
    73	
    74	1. The `ArgumentNullException` is in line with .NET conventions for public
    75	   methods that take reference-type parameters.
    76	2. It produces a clearer error message than letting it bubble through
    77	   `System.Text.Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(null)`.
    78	3. It does not affect wire bytes; valid payloads produce identical output.
    79	
    80	## E5 — Validation error message text
    81	
    82	The C# port's validation messages (e.g., "invalid P-256 private key: scalar
    83	must be in [1, n - 1]") differ from noble's text. This is a .NET-native
    84	exception adaptation. Validation occurs at the same step (sign time, via
    85	`Crypto.GetPublicKey`), so timing is identical.
    86	
    87	## F — Fixture comparison gate
    88	
    89	The upstream `__tests__/stamp-test.ts` explicitly does not snapshot the
    90	signature bytes because P-256 signatures are not deterministic across
    91	upstream runtimes (`nodecrypto`, `webcrypto`). The C# port adopts the same
    92	strategy: assert the stamp is a valid DER ECDSA signature that verifies
    93	under the configured public key against `SHA-256(content)`. This is the
    94	strongest assertion the upstream tests themselves make, and it is
    95	sufficient to guarantee the stamp will be accepted by Turnkey's backend.
    96	
    97	Exact Node-generated byte snapshots would require running the upstream npm
    98	package end-to-end with its own `node_modules`, which the published tarball
    99	does not ship. Adding a fixture-generator that uses `npm install` in
   100	`tests/Fixtures/Generators/` is a possible future enhancement but is out of
   101	scope for v0.1.0-alpha.
   102	
   103	## Verdict
   104	
   105	`src/ApiKeyStamper.cs` has been reviewed in 3 Codex rounds. Every
   106	finding has been resolved by code change (E3, E4) or by documented
   107	reconciliation (E1, E2, E5, F). The implementation is wire-format-correct
   108	against the Turnkey backend and is byte-deterministic against the upstream
   109	`purejs` runtime.

   577	## 9. リスクと対策
   578	
   579	| リスク | 対策 |
   580	|---|---|
   581	| `purejs` runtime と `nodecrypto.ts` runtime の signature byte 差 | PR-5/6 では `runtimeOverride: "purejs"` を必ず指定。doc にも明記。さらに generator pre-flight で既知 vector check |
   582	| Node version drift で fixture が再生成毎に変わる | `package-lock.json` を commit、`node_version` を fixture に記録、generator が `process.version` を起動時 assert |
   583	| `@noble/curves` の transitive 解決が drift して low-S 出力が変わる | `transitive_lock_sha256` を fixture provenance に記録、generator 起動時に既知 hex を assert |
   584	| 公式テストファイル sha256 を pin したのに毎月差分が出て CI が騒がしい | drift workflow は **idempotent な issue update のみ**で main の CI gate にはしない (=PR がブロックされない、issue が量産されない) |
   585	| RFC vector を取り込んだら BouncyCastle の primitives が誤動作した | 設計上ありえないが、対処は Tier-3 失敗 → BouncyCastle pin を見直し、別 PR で対応 |
   586	| SDK HPKE が RFC 9180 と互換でない (PR-7a で判明) | RFC 9180 vectors 取り込みを諦め、Tier-2 で SDK 生成 bytes を信頼。`codex-crypto-reviews/sdk-hpke-vs-rfc9180.md` に差分点を文書化 |
   587	| 公式が test を消した | upstream-drift で検知、coverage-map で `REMOVED` 行を出して人手 review |
   588	| Node generator 環境差で `package-lock.json` が壊れる (Apple Silicon vs x86_64 など) | platform-agnostic な依存しか入らないことを `npm ls` で確認、再現手順を README に明示 |
   589	| 公式他言語 SDK の test fixture を借りる場合のライセンス | 上流 (tkhq/sdk Apache-2.0、tkhq/go-sdk Apache-2.0) に従い PR-14 で `NOTICE` に出典明記 |
   590	| Generators ディレクトリが dotnet test のビルドを壊す | PR-4 で csproj の `Fixtures/**/*` ItemGroup から `Generators/**` を `Exclude` する (Section 6.2 末尾参照) |
   591	| PR-11 fixture が consumer のない golden data になる | PR-11 で `ProofFixtureProvenanceTests` を同 PR で必ず追加し、機械検証経路を確立 |
   592	
   593	## 10. 想定 FAQ (codex 想定突っ込み先回り)
   594	
   595	**Q. 既存の `_provenance` 付き Tier-1 fixture と何が違うのか？**
   596	A. Tier-1 は「上流テストファイルの値を**人手で転記**」している。
   597	本プラン Tier-2 は「上流 npm パッケージを**実行**して**実バイト**を取る」
   598	ので、上流コードに潜む branch (例: SDK HPKE の AAD 連結順序ミス) も検出できる。
   599	両者は補完関係。Section 2.1 で定義した「決定論経路」のみ byte snapshot を取る。
   600	
   601	**Q. なぜ `dotnet test` で Node を起動しないのか？**
   602	A. (a) Codex review-clean 環境は read-only で Node を持たないことが多い、
   603	(b) CI runner が macOS / Linux / Windows で生 Node を呼ぶと flaky になる、
   604	(c) 出力は決定論的なので **生成済み JSON をコミット**する方が
   605	高速で再現性が高い。fixture 再生成は別 workflow に分離する。
   606	
   607	**Q. Tier-3 (RFC ベクトル) は冗長では？ 公式が正しいなら上流テスト等価で十分。**
   608	A. v1 では「HPKE 全体の RFC 9180 vectors を取る」、v2 では「Turnkey HPKE は
   609	独自構成だから RFC 9180 は無理」と振れたが、いずれも誤り。v3 canonical
   610	(Section 2.1):
   611	- C# が port している SDK HPKE は **JSdoc が RFC 9180 を明示** している。
   612	- ただし完全互換かは未確認 → PR-7a で評価。**byte-equal なら PR-9b で
   613	  RFC 9180 vectors を取り込む** (条件付き Tier-3)。
   614	- それと別に、**primitive 単位** (ECDSA P-256 RFC 6979, HKDF RFC 5869,
   615	  HMAC-SHA256 RFC 4231, AES-GCM NIST CAVP, SHA-256 NIST SHS, Ed25519 RFC 8032,
   616	  secp256k1 SEC2, Base58Check Bitcoin) の標準ベクトルは PR-8/PR-9 で取り込む。
   617	- これは「primitive レベルの C# 実装が RFC/NIST 仕様に従っている」ことの
   618	  独立証明であり、SDK HPKE 全体は Tier-2 (round-trip + 構造) と
   619	  条件付き Tier-3 が分担する。
   620	
   621	**Q. `coverage-map.sh` を pure shell にするのは無理がないか？**
   622	A. `tkhq/sdk` の `__tests__/*.ts` 内 `test("...")` は ESLint で一行 1 ブロックに
   623	強制されているので awk で確実に grep できる。複雑な AST が必要なら
   624	PR-2 のレビューで Node ベースに切替を検討する。本ドラフトでは
   625	**「Node 依存を増やさない」を優先**する。
   626	
   627	**Q. proof.ts のポートはやらないのか？**
   628	A. proof モジュール本体のポート (= `Turnkey.Crypto.Proofs.Verify(...)` の
   629	C# 実装) は scope 外。peak monorepo の wallet flow からは呼ばれないと
   630	判定済み (別途 grep で確認)。
   631	ただし `proof-tests.ts` に**実 enclave 由来の AppProof / BootProof
   632	ゴールデン JSON** がある事実が今回判明したので、それだけは PR-11 で
   633	`tests/Fixtures/proofs/` に**先行コミット**する。
   634	PR-11 では **proof の cryptographic verifier は実装しない** (= 別計画) が、
   635	`ProofFixtureProvenanceTests` (JSON parse、`_provenance` schema、上流 sha256 一致)
   636	は同 PR で必ず一緒に追加する。別途 proof 実装プランを立てる際の前提が整う。
   637	
   638	**Q. live e2e は無くて大丈夫か？**
   639	A. 本プラン Tier-4 で `TURNKEY_TEST_ORG_API_KEY` opt-in は維持する。
   640	ただし v0.1.0-alpha の必須条件ではない。Tier-1 ～ Tier-3 が
   641	完備すれば backend を呼ばずに wire-format compatibility が保証される。
   642

   667	  価値はあるが Turnkey SDK の wire-format には直結しないため、本プランでは
   668	  **PR-10 の延長 (オプション)** とし、必須化はしない。

   677	| `tkhq/python-sdk` のみが live backend e2e、他 SDK は mock 中心 | **エージェント調査の記録**であり本プラン内で機械検証しない。Tier-4 (live) を opt-in に留める判断の補強材料として使うだけ |
   678	| PR-7a の fixed-ephemeral injection 経路の実在性 | **PR-7a の成果物そのもの**。本プラン内で先取り判定しない。PR-7a が「不可能」と結論したら PR-9b は実施されない |

/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba codex-crypto-reviews/Http.cs-codex-findings-reconciliation.md | sed -n '1,220p'" in /Users/takeshi/Kyuzan/src/turnkey-sdk-csharp/.claude/worktrees/laughing-hertz-048cd4
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	# Http.cs — Codex findings reconciliation
     2	
     3	After 3 rounds of Codex review on `src/Http.cs`, several findings recur. This
     4	document records the reconciliation for each so future reviewers do not
     5	re-litigate.
     6	
     7	## E1 — JSON escaping (resolved in r3)
     8	
     9	**Codex claim:** Default `System.Text.Json` escaping differs from JS
    10	`JSON.stringify` for `<`, `>`, `&`, and non-ASCII text.
    11	
    12	**Reconciliation:** `TurnkeyJsonContext` now exposes a static
    13	`JsCompatibleEncoder = JavaScriptEncoder.UnsafeRelaxedJsonEscaping` and the
    14	file-level comment documents that Turnkey activity bodies contain only
    15	ASCII content (UUIDs, enum strings, hex) in practice. Callers who need
    16	maximum JS-stringify parity for atypical content can wrap their own
    17	`JsonSerializerOptions { Encoder = TurnkeyJsonContext.JsCompatibleEncoder }`.
    18	Wire-byte parity is unaffected for normal Turnkey flows.
    19	
    20	## E2 — Empty / null validation strictness
    21	
    22	**Codex claim:** `StampGetWhoami("")` and `Stamp*(null)` throw; upstream
    23	`JSON.stringify` would produce `{"organizationId":""}` or `"null"`.
    24	
    25	**Reconciliation:** `.NET`-native validation on public-method reference-type
    26	parameters. The C# port refuses to stamp something that would be guaranteed
    27	to fail server-side validation anyway. This is a stricter superset of
    28	upstream behavior; valid inputs produce wire-identical output. Documented
    29	on each `Stamp*` method.
    30	
    31	## E3 — SignedRequest property order (resolved in r2)
    32	
    33	`SignedRequest` is now `{ body, stamp, url }` matching the upstream literal
    34	in `public_api.client.ts`.
    35	
    36	## E4 — DTO property declaration order
    37	
    38	**Codex claim:** C# DTO field order is `organizationId, type, timestampMs,
    39	parameters`; the upstream **type** declaration order in
    40	`public_api.types.ts` is `type, timestampMs, organizationId, parameters,
    41	generateAppProofs`.
    42	
    43	**Reconciliation:** Wire JSON order is determined by the caller's runtime
    44	object literal, not by the TypeScript type declaration. Upstream
    45	`stampX(input)` does `JSON.stringify(input)` which uses the caller's
    46	object key insertion order. The Turnkey backend hashes the body bytes as
    47	received and verifies the signature against those exact bytes — it does
    48	not impose canonical ordering. The C# DTO order matches the peak Unity
    49	port and is internally consistent (signed and sent bytes are the same).
    50	Documented in the file header.
    51	
    52	## E5 — Default initializer vs omitted key
    53	
    54	**Codex claim:** Unset required fields serialize as `""` / `{}` / `[]` in
    55	C# rather than being omitted as in TS.
    56	
    57	**Reconciliation:** For all required fields, valid wire bodies populate
    58	every field; an unset required field would produce a body the backend
    59	rejects (in either implementation). Optional `generateAppProofs` is
    60	nullable + `JsonIgnoreCondition.WhenWritingNull` so it is omitted when
    61	unset, matching upstream optional-key behavior exactly.
    62	
    63	## E6 — baseUrl validation (resolved in r2)
    64	
    65	Constructor throws `ArgumentException` when baseUrl is null or empty.
    66	
    67	## F — Fixture exact-byte gate
    68	
    69	Same situation as `ApiKeyStamper.cs`: upstream's own
    70	`__tests__/stamp-test.ts` does not snapshot stamped bytes because the
    71	underlying P-256 signatures vary per upstream runtime. The C# tests
    72	assert what upstream tests do: URL, JSON body shape, header decode, and
    73	verifiable DER signature. Generating an exact-byte Node fixture would
    74	require running `@turnkey/http@3.16.0` end-to-end with `node_modules`,
    75	which the published tarball does not ship. A future
    76	`tests/Fixtures/http/turnkey-http-vectors.json` could be added if a
    77	fixture generator is committed; this is tracked as a Codex r2 deferred
    78	item.
    79	
    80	## Verdict
    81	
    82	`src/Http.cs` has been reviewed in 3 Codex rounds. Every finding is either
    83	resolved by code change (E1, E3, E6, generateAppProofs) or reconciled by
    84	documented analysis (E2, E4, E5, F). The implementation is wire-format-
    85	correct against the Turnkey backend and uses upstream-compatible JSON
    86	escaping.

.github/workflows/release.yml
name: Release

on:
  release:
    types: [published]

# Allow re-running the same tag if the prior run failed mid-flight,
# but never two different runs in parallel for the same tag.
concurrency:
  group: release-${{ github.event.release.tag_name }}
  cancel-in-progress: false

permissions:
  contents: write       # upload Release assets
  packages: write       # publish to nuget.pkg.github.com
  id-token: write       # attest-build-provenance OIDC
  attestations: write   # attest-build-provenance writes attestations

jobs:
  publish:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    env:
      RELEASE_TAG:      ${{ github.event.release.tag_name }}
      GITHUB_ACTOR_ENV: ${{ github.actor }}

    steps:
      # actions/checkout v6.0.2 — see .github/pin-actions.txt
      - name: Checkout tag
        uses: actions/checkout@de0fac2e4500dabe0009e67214ff5f5447ce83dd
        with:
          ref: ${{ github.event.release.tag_name }}
          fetch-depth: 0
          # Drop checkout token from .git/config after checkout — later
          # git/gh calls pass `GH_TOKEN` explicitly and never authenticate
          # via the persisted checkout credential, so persisting it
          # extends the token's blast radius without benefit.
          persist-credentials: false

      - name: Parse + validate strict SemVer 2.0.0 tag
        id: ver
        env:
          TAG: ${{ env.RELEASE_TAG }}
        run: |
          set -euo pipefail
          # Strict SemVer 2.0.0 (no build metadata): vMAJOR.MINOR.PATCH[-PRERELEASE]
          # PRERELEASE = identifier (. identifier)*
          # identifier = numeric (no leading zero) | alphanumeric
          re='^v(0|[1-9][0-9]*)\.(0|[1-9][0-9]*)\.(0|[1-9][0-9]*)(-((0|[1-9][0-9]*|[0-9]*[A-Za-z-][0-9A-Za-z-]*)(\.(0|[1-9][0-9]*|[0-9]*[A-Za-z-][0-9A-Za-z-]*))*))?$'
          if [[ ! "$TAG" =~ $re ]]; then
            echo "::error::Tag '$TAG' is not strict SemVer 2.0.0 (vMAJOR.MINOR.PATCH[-PRERELEASE]; no build metadata)."
            exit 1
          fi
          echo "version=${TAG#v}" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
          echo "tag=$TAG"          >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"

      - name: Resolve tag commit SHA
        id: tagsha
        env:
          TAG: ${{ env.RELEASE_TAG }}
        run: |
          set -euo pipefail
          echo "sha=$(git rev-parse "${TAG}^{commit}")" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"

      - name: Verify tag commit is contained in main
        env:
          GH_TOKEN:   ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
          OWNER_REPO: ${{ github.repository }}
          TAG_SHA:    ${{ steps.tagsha.outputs.sha }}
        run: |
          set -euo pipefail
          # Use the REST compare API instead of `git fetch origin main`.
          # Reason: `actions/checkout` ran with `persist-credentials:
          # false` (security), so the runner's `.git/config` has no
          # credential to authenticate a `git fetch` against this
          # private repo. `gh api` reads `GH_TOKEN` from the env and
          # works against private repos without persisting a git
          # credential.
          #
          # Semantics: GET /repos/{repo}/compare/{base}...{head} returns
          # `status` ∈ {ahead, behind, identical, diverged}, where
          # `base = main` and `head = TAG_SHA`. The tag is reachable
          # from main iff main contains the tag commit, i.e. main has
          # commits the tag does not (status: `behind`) or main and
          # tag point to the same commit (status: `identical`). Any
          # other status (`ahead`, `diverged`) means the tag carries
          # commits not on main and must be rejected.
          STATUS=$(gh api "repos/${OWNER_REPO}/compare/main...${TAG_SHA}" --jq .status)
          case "$STATUS" in
            behind|identical)
              echo "tag ${TAG_SHA} reachable from main (compare status: ${STATUS})"
              ;;
            *)
              echo "::error::Tag commit ${TAG_SHA} is not reachable from main (compare status: ${STATUS}). Releases must be cut from a commit on main."
              exit 1
              ;;
          esac

      # actions/setup-dotnet v5.2.0 — see .github/pin-actions.txt
      - name: Setup .NET 8
        uses: actions/setup-dotnet@c2fa09f4bde5ebb9d1777cf28262a3eb3db3ced7
        with:
          dotnet-version: 8.0.x

      - name: Restore (locked-mode)
        run: dotnet restore turnkey-sdk-csharp.sln --locked-mode

      - name: Build
        env:
          VERSION: ${{ steps.ver.outputs.version }}
          TAG_SHA: ${{ steps.tagsha.outputs.sha }}
        run: |
          dotnet build turnkey-sdk-csharp.sln -c Release --no-restore \
            /p:Version="$VERSION" \
            /p:PackageVersion="$VERSION" \
            /p:RepositoryCommit="$TAG_SHA" \
            /p:IncludeSymbols=true \
            /p:SymbolPackageFormat=snupkg

      - name: Test
        env:
          TURNKEY_TEST_ORG_API_KEY: ${{ secrets.TURNKEY_TEST_ORG_API_KEY }}
          TURNKEY_TEST_ORG_ID:      ${{ secrets.TURNKEY_TEST_ORG_ID }}
        run: dotnet test turnkey-sdk-csharp.sln -c Release --no-build

      - name: Pack
        env:
          VERSION: ${{ steps.ver.outputs.version }}
          TAG_SHA: ${{ steps.tagsha.outputs.sha }}
        run: |
          dotnet pack src/turnkey-sdk-csharp.csproj -c Release --no-build \
            --output ./artifacts \
            /p:Version="$VERSION" \
            /p:PackageVersion="$VERSION" \
            /p:RepositoryCommit="$TAG_SHA" \
            /p:IncludeSymbols=true \
            /p:SymbolPackageFormat=snupkg

      - name: Validate local .nupkg + .snupkg contents (strict)
        id: pack_artifacts
        env:
          VERSION: ${{ steps.ver.outputs.version }}
        run: |
          set -euo pipefail
          NUPKG="./artifacts/KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.${VERSION}.nupkg"
          SNUPKG="./artifacts/KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.${VERSION}.snupkg"
          test -f "$NUPKG"  || { echo "::error::nupkg missing";  exit 1; }
          test -f "$SNUPKG" || { echo "::error::snupkg missing"; exit 1; }

          # .nupkg: strict path enumeration + full-line fixed-string match.
          nupkg_paths=$(unzip -Z1 "$NUPKG")
          echo "$nupkg_paths"
          for f in README.md LICENSE NOTICE \
                   lib/netstandard2.1/KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.dll \
                   lib/net8.0/KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.dll; do
            echo "$nupkg_paths" | grep -Fxq "$f" \
              || { echo "::error::nupkg is missing exact path '$f'"; exit 1; }
          done

          # .snupkg: must contain .pdb for both TFMs.
          snupkg_paths=$(unzip -Z1 "$SNUPKG")
          echo "$snupkg_paths"
          for f in lib/netstandard2.1/KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.pdb \
                   lib/net8.0/KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.pdb; do
            echo "$snupkg_paths" | grep -Fxq "$f" \
              || { echo "::error::snupkg is missing exact path '$f'"; exit 1; }
          done

          NUPKG_SHA256=$(sha256sum  "$NUPKG"  | awk '{print $1}')
          SNUPKG_SHA256=$(sha256sum "$SNUPKG" | awk '{print $1}')
          # Use step outputs (not $GITHUB_ENV) for explicit, unambiguous
          # cross-step data flow. Consumers reference these as
          # steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.<key> wrapped in workflow
          # expression delimiters at the call site (delimiters omitted
          # in this comment so the YAML parser does not interpolate it).
          {
            echo "nupkg_path=$NUPKG"
            echo "snupkg_path=$SNUPKG"
            echo "nupkg_sha256=$NUPKG_SHA256"
            echo "snupkg_sha256=$SNUPKG_SHA256"
          } >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"

      - name: Write release-checksums.txt
        id: checksums
        env:
          VERSION:       ${{ steps.ver.outputs.version }}
          TAG_SHA:       ${{ steps.tagsha.outputs.sha }}
          NUPKG_SHA256:  ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.nupkg_sha256 }}
          SNUPKG_SHA256: ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.snupkg_sha256 }}
        run: |
          set -euo pipefail
          CHECKSUMS="./artifacts/release-checksums.txt"
          {
            echo "# release-checksums for KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk ${VERSION}"
            echo "version          = ${VERSION}"
            echo "source_commit    = ${TAG_SHA}"
            echo "nupkg_sha256     = ${NUPKG_SHA256}"
            echo "snupkg_sha256    = ${SNUPKG_SHA256}"
          } > "$CHECKSUMS"
          echo "checksums_path=$CHECKSUMS" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"

      - name: Preflight existing Release assets (unconditional)
        id: preflight
        env:
          GH_TOKEN:        ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
          TAG:             ${{ env.RELEASE_TAG }}
          VERSION:         ${{ steps.ver.outputs.version }}
          NUPKG_SHA256:    ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.nupkg_sha256 }}
          SNUPKG_SHA256:   ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.snupkg_sha256 }}
          NUPKG_PATH:      ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.nupkg_path }}
          SNUPKG_PATH:     ${{ steps.pack_artifacts.outputs.snupkg_path }}
          CHECKSUMS_PATH:  ${{ steps.checksums.outputs.checksums_path }}
          NUPKG_NAME:      KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.${{ steps.ver.outputs.version }}.nupkg
          SNUPKG_NAME:     KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.${{ steps.ver.outputs.version }}.snupkg
        run: |
          set -euo pipefail
          mkdir -p ./_release_assets
          HAS_PRIOR=false

          # Enumerate assets that actually exist on the Release. We do NOT
          # treat a failed `gh release download` as "asset missing" —
.github/workflows/release-drafter-autolabel.yml
name: Release drafter — autolabel PR

on:
  pull_request:
    # `edited` is included so title-edit relabeling triggers. The
    # "Strip stale conventional-commit labels" step below runs only on
    # `edited` events and removes stale conventional-commit labels
    # before the autolabeler re-applies based on the current title.
    # `labeled` / `unlabeled` deliberately excluded so manual maintainer
    # label adjustments are not auto-reverted.
    types: [opened, reopened, synchronize, edited]

permissions:
  contents: read
  pull-requests: write

jobs:
  autolabel:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    env:
      GH_TOKEN:  ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
      GH_REPO:   ${{ github.repository }}
      PR_NUMBER: ${{ github.event.pull_request.number }}
    steps:
      # release-drafter's autolabeler only ADDs labels; it cannot remove.
      # If the title changes from "fix:" to "feat:", the stale "fix"
      # label would linger and pollute the version-resolver. Strip the
      # conventional-commit set first ONLY on `edited` so unmodified
      # PR events keep their existing labels intact.
      #
      # We use `gh pr edit --remove-label` (NOT `gh label remove`, which
      # would delete the label from the repository entirely). The script
      # first queries which conventional-commit labels are actually
      # attached to this PR, then only calls --remove-label for those.
      # Any `gh` failure aborts.
      - name: Strip stale conventional-commit labels (edited only)
        if: github.event.action == 'edited'
        run: |
          set -euo pipefail
          conventional='breaking feature fix deps docs ci chore'

          # List labels actually attached to this PR.
          attached=$(gh pr view "$PR_NUMBER" --json labels --jq '.labels[].name')

          # Intersect conventional ∩ attached; remove only those.
          for label in $conventional; do
            if grep -Fxq "$label" <<< "$attached"; then
              gh pr edit "$PR_NUMBER" --remove-label "$label"
            fi
          done

      # release-drafter v7.3.0 autolabeler subpath
      - uses: release-drafter/release-drafter/autolabeler@da8b9b696abad2ad997580e49f4c1c2e03cc2bd2
        with:
          config-name: release-drafter.yml
        env:
          GITHUB_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
.github/workflows/consumer-smoke.yml
name: Consumer install smoke

# Verifies that a fresh consumer project can install
# KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk@<version> from nuget.pkg.github.com/KyuzanInc
# and exercise the public API surface (Turnkey.Encoding +
# Turnkey.Crypto + Turnkey.ApiKeyStamper).
#
# This is the canonical "consumer in a GitHub Actions job" pattern
# documented in docs/release-process.md §5. The runner-issued
# `secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN` carries `read:packages` for the same org by
# default, so no PAT is needed.
#
# Two trigger paths:
#
#   1. workflow_dispatch — manual run on demand. The user supplies
#      the package version and TFM through the inputs.
#
#   2. workflow_run — fires automatically whenever the upstream
#      `Release` workflow completes successfully. The version is
#      derived from the upstream tag (workflow_run.head_branch).
#      `workflow_run` always executes the workflow file that exists
#      on the default branch, so the new trigger is inert on feature
#      branches and only activates once merged to `main`.

run-name: "Consumer smoke (${{ inputs.package_version || github.event.workflow_run.head_branch || 'unknown' }})"

on:
  workflow_dispatch:
    inputs:
      package_version:
        description: "Version to install (e.g. 0.1.0-alpha.0)"
        required: true
        default: "0.1.0-alpha.0"
      tfm:
        description: "Target framework moniker"
        required: true
        default: "net8.0"
  workflow_run:
    workflows: ["Release"]   # matches release.yml's `name:` field, not the filename
    types: [completed]

permissions:
  contents: read
  packages: read

jobs:
  consumer-install:
    # Title falls back to the upstream tag short name on workflow_run
    # so the job card never shows a dangling "Install + use " on
    # auto-runs (where `inputs.package_version` stringifies to '').
    name: "Install + use ${{ inputs.package_version || github.event.workflow_run.head_branch }}"
    # Skip auto-runs that follow a failed/cancelled Release — there's
    # no package to verify in that case. Manual dispatch always runs.
    if: |
      github.event_name == 'workflow_dispatch' ||
      (github.event_name == 'workflow_run' && github.event.workflow_run.conclusion == 'success')
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      # Resolve which package version + TFM this run should install.
      # `workflow_run` events do not populate the `inputs` context
      # (`inputs` is only available for `workflow_dispatch` and
      # `workflow_call` events per GitHub Actions context rules), so
      # this step branches on `github.event_name` and pulls the
      # version from the upstream tag short name for auto-runs. On
      # manual runs it routes the user inputs through unchanged.
      #
      # Outputs:
      #   - steps.resolve.outputs.package_version
      #   - steps.resolve.outputs.tfm
      - name: Resolve install inputs
        id: resolve
        env:
          EVENT_NAME:   ${{ github.event_name }}
          DISPATCH_VER: ${{ inputs.package_version }}
          DISPATCH_TFM: ${{ inputs.tfm }}
          WR_BRANCH:    ${{ github.event.workflow_run.head_branch }}
          WR_EVENT:     ${{ github.event.workflow_run.event }}
        run: |
          set -euo pipefail
          if [[ "$EVENT_NAME" == "workflow_dispatch" ]]; then
            VER="$DISPATCH_VER"
            TFM="$DISPATCH_TFM"
          else
            # workflow_run from `release.yml`. The upstream Release
            # workflow only triggers on `release: published`, so
            # `workflow_run.event` MUST be 'release' and
            # `workflow_run.head_branch` is the tag ref short name
            # (e.g. 'v0.1.0-alpha.0'). Refuse anything else.
            if [[ "$WR_EVENT" != "release" ]]; then
              echo "::error::Unexpected upstream workflow_run.event '$WR_EVENT' (expected 'release'). Refusing to run."
              exit 1
            fi
            # Strict SemVer 2.0.0 with leading 'v' — kept BYTE-FOR-BYTE
            # in sync with the regex in
            # `.github/workflows/release.yml` step "Parse + validate
            # strict SemVer 2.0.0 tag". Any drift here is a bug.
            re='^v(0|[1-9][0-9]*)\.(0|[1-9][0-9]*)\.(0|[1-9][0-9]*)(-((0|[1-9][0-9]*|[0-9]*[A-Za-z-][0-9A-Za-z-]*)(\.(0|[1-9][0-9]*|[0-9]*[A-Za-z-][0-9A-Za-z-]*))*))?$'
            if [[ ! "$WR_BRANCH" =~ $re ]]; then
              echo "::error::workflow_run.head_branch '$WR_BRANCH' is not a strict SemVer 2.0.0 tag; refusing to install."
              exit 1
            fi
            VER="${WR_BRANCH#v}"
            TFM="net8.0"  # default for auto-runs; matrix-able in a later plan
          fi
          echo "package_version=$VER" >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
          echo "tfm=$TFM"             >> "$GITHUB_OUTPUT"
          echo "Resolved: package_version=$VER, tfm=$TFM (source=$EVENT_NAME)"

      # actions/checkout v6.0.2 — see .github/pin-actions.txt
      # Checkout is only needed so setup-dotnet can find a workspace.
      - name: Checkout (workspace anchor)
        uses: actions/checkout@de0fac2e4500dabe0009e67214ff5f5447ce83dd
        with:
          persist-credentials: false

      # actions/setup-dotnet v5.2.0 — see .github/pin-actions.txt
      - name: Setup .NET 8
        uses: actions/setup-dotnet@c2fa09f4bde5ebb9d1777cf28262a3eb3db3ced7
        with:
          dotnet-version: 8.0.x

      - name: Create fresh consumer project
        env:
          TFM: ${{ steps.resolve.outputs.tfm }}
        run: |
          set -euo pipefail
          mkdir -p /tmp/consumer && cd /tmp/consumer
          dotnet new console --framework "$TFM" --name TurnkeySdkConsumer --force

      - name: Configure GitHub Packages source via dotnet nuget add source
        env:
          GH_ACTOR: ${{ github.actor }}
          GH_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
        run: |
          set -euo pipefail
          cd /tmp/consumer/TurnkeySdkConsumer
          # Write the source with credentials into a LOCAL NuGet.config.
          # Using `dotnet nuget add source` lets the CLI handle escaping
          # of the URL/username/token. The resulting NuGet.config
          # contains the token in clear text, which is acceptable here
          # because (a) the file lives inside an ephemeral runner only,
          # and (b) `secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN` is automatically revoked at
          # job end.
          dotnet nuget add source \
            "https://nuget.pkg.github.com/KyuzanInc/index.json" \
            --name kyuzan-github \
            --username "$GH_ACTOR" \
            --password "$GH_TOKEN" \
            --store-password-in-clear-text

      - name: Install KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk
        env:
          VERSION: ${{ steps.resolve.outputs.package_version }}
        run: |
          set -euo pipefail
          cd /tmp/consumer/TurnkeySdkConsumer
          dotnet add package KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk --version "$VERSION"

      - name: Write sample Program.cs (exercises public API)
        run: |
          set -euo pipefail
          cat > /tmp/consumer/TurnkeySdkConsumer/Program.cs <<'PROGRAM'
          using System;
          using System.Linq;
          using Turnkey;

          internal static class Program
          {
              private static int Main()
              {
                  Console.WriteLine("=== KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk consumer smoke ===");

                  // 1. Turnkey.Encoding — hex round-trip
                  byte[] sample = new byte[] { 0xDE, 0xAD, 0xBE, 0xEF, 0x00, 0x11, 0x22, 0x33 };
                  string hex = Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString(sample);
                  byte[] back = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(hex);
                  bool encodingOk = back.SequenceEqual(sample) && hex == "deadbeef00112233";
                  Console.WriteLine($"[1/3] Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString: \"{hex}\" (round-trip ok: {encodingOk})");
                  if (!encodingOk) return 1;

                  // 2. Turnkey.Crypto — generate a P-256 keypair
                  var keyPair = Crypto.GenerateP256KeyPair();
                  bool privOk = !string.IsNullOrEmpty(keyPair.PrivateKey) && keyPair.PrivateKey.Length == 64;
                  bool pubOk  = !string.IsNullOrEmpty(keyPair.PublicKey)  && keyPair.PublicKey.Length  == 66;
                  Console.WriteLine($"[2/3] Crypto.GenerateP256KeyPair: priv.len={keyPair.PrivateKey.Length}, pub.len={keyPair.PublicKey.Length} (ok: {privOk && pubOk})");
                  if (!privOk || !pubOk) return 2;

                  // 3. Turnkey.ApiKeyStamper — sign a sample payload
                  var stamper = new ApiKeyStamper(keyPair.PublicKey, keyPair.PrivateKey);
                  var stamp = stamper.Stamp("{\"sample\":\"payload\"}");
                  bool stampOk = !string.IsNullOrEmpty(stamp.StampHeaderValue)
                                 && stamp.StampHeaderName == "X-Stamp";
                  Console.WriteLine($"[3/3] ApiKeyStamper.Stamp: header={stamp.StampHeaderName}, value.len={stamp.StampHeaderValue.Length} (ok: {stampOk})");
                  if (!stampOk) return 3;

                  Console.WriteLine();
                  Console.WriteLine("Consumer install + use of KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk verified end-to-end.");
                  return 0;
              }
          }
          PROGRAM

      - name: Build + run consumer sample
        run: |
          set -euo pipefail
          cd /tmp/consumer/TurnkeySdkConsumer
          dotnet build -c Release
          dotnet run -c Release --no-build
.github/workflows/pr-title-lint.yml
name: PR title lint

on:
  pull_request:
    types: [opened, reopened, synchronize, edited]

permissions:
  contents: read
  pull-requests: read

jobs:
  lint:
    # Job display name must stay in sync with the required-check name
    # documented in docs/release-process.md: the resulting GitHub UI
    # status is "PR title lint / Verify conventional commit title".
    name: Verify conventional commit title
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    env:
      PR_TITLE: ${{ github.event.pull_request.title }}
    steps:
      - name: Verify conventional commit title
        run: |
          set -euo pipefail
          # Structural regex: <type>(<scope>)?!?: <subject>
          # types: feat, fix, deps, docs, ci, chore, refactor, test
          # scope (when present): non-empty
          # subject: at least one char (further checked below for non-whitespace)
          re='^(feat|fix|deps|docs|ci|chore|refactor|test)(\([^)]+\))?!?: (.+)$'

          # Apply GitHub's workflow-command escape (per
          # https://docs.github.com/en/actions/reference/workflows-and-actions/workflow-commands#example-evaluating-data-from-untrusted-sources)
          # before inserting untrusted PR-title text into an ::error::
          # annotation. Order matters: encode `%` first so other
          # escape sequences are not double-encoded.
          escape() {
            local s="$1"
            s="${s//%/%25}"
            s="${s//$'\r'/%0D}"
            s="${s//$'\n'/%0A}"
            printf '%s' "$s"
          }
          sanitized_raw=$(printf '%s' "$PR_TITLE" | tr -cd '[:print:]\n\r' | head -c 200)
          sanitized=$(escape "$sanitized_raw")

          if [[ ! "$PR_TITLE" =~ $re ]]; then
            echo "::error::PR title is not conventional (expect: <type>(scope)?!?: <subject>; types: feat|fix|deps|docs|ci|chore|refactor|test). See docs/release-process.md. Got: ${sanitized}"
            exit 1
          fi
          # Subject must contain at least one non-whitespace character.
          subject="${BASH_REMATCH[3]}"
          if ! printf '%s' "$subject" | grep -Eq '[^[:space:]]'; then
            echo "::error::PR title subject is whitespace-only. Got: ${sanitized}"
            exit 1
          fi

.github/workflows/repo-privacy-check.yml
name: Repo privacy check

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
  schedule:
    - cron: '0 9 * * 1'   # Mondays 09:00 UTC

permissions:
  contents: read

jobs:
  privacy:
    name: Assert repo is PRIVATE
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: Verify visibility
        env:
          GH_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
        run: |
          set -euo pipefail
          VIS=$(gh repo view "${{ github.repository }}" --json visibility -q .visibility)
          echo "Visibility: $VIS"
          if [[ "$VIS" != "PRIVATE" ]]; then
            echo "::error::Repository visibility must be PRIVATE, got: $VIS"
            exit 1
          fi
.github/workflows/ci.yml
name: CI

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main]

permissions:
  contents: read

jobs:
  build-test:
    name: Build + test (ubuntu-latest, net8.0 runner)
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v6

      - name: Setup .NET 8
        uses: actions/setup-dotnet@v5
        with:
          dotnet-version: 8.0.x

      - name: Verify packages.lock.json is present
        run: |
          test -f src/packages.lock.json   || (echo "src/packages.lock.json missing"   && exit 1)
          test -f tests/packages.lock.json || (echo "tests/packages.lock.json missing" && exit 1)

      - name: Restore (locked-mode)
        run: dotnet restore turnkey-sdk-csharp.sln --locked-mode

      - name: Build (Release, both TFMs)
        run: dotnet build turnkey-sdk-csharp.sln -c Release --no-restore

      - name: Test (Release, with coverage)
        env:
          # E2E tests skip themselves if these are unset
          TURNKEY_TEST_ORG_API_KEY: ${{ secrets.TURNKEY_TEST_ORG_API_KEY }}
          TURNKEY_TEST_ORG_ID: ${{ secrets.TURNKEY_TEST_ORG_ID }}
        run: |
          dotnet test turnkey-sdk-csharp.sln -c Release --no-build \
            --collect:"XPlat Code Coverage" \
            --results-directory ./TestResults \
            --logger "trx;LogFileName=test-results.trx"

      # Coverage gate. Threshold is set to 30% combined-TFM for
      # v0.1.0-alpha because the report counts both the netstandard2.1
      # and net8.0 production assemblies (tests only target net8.0) AND
      # the System.Text.Json source-generated TypeInfo classes (most of
      # which are never executed by tests). The local single-TFM
      # net8.0-only figure is ~78% line.
      # TODOs to raise back:
      #   1. Filter the cobertura output to net8.0 only (or unify reports).
      #   2. Add targeted negative tests for
      #      Crypto.DecryptCredentialBundle / EncryptPrivateKeyToBundle /
      #      DecryptExportBundle error paths once Turnkey sample bundles
      #      are committable.
      - name: Coverage gate (>=30% combined-TFM line for v0.1.0-alpha)
        uses: irongut/CodeCoverageSummary@v1.3.0
        with:
          filename: TestResults/**/coverage.cobertura.xml
          badge: false
          fail_below_min: true
          thresholds: '30 50'
          format: markdown
          output: both

      - name: Upload coverage artifact
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v7
        if: always()
        with:
          name: coverage-report
          path: TestResults/**

  pack:
    name: dotnet pack (validation)
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: build-test
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v6
      - uses: actions/setup-dotnet@v5
        with:
          dotnet-version: 8.0.x
      - name: Restore (locked-mode)
        run: dotnet restore turnkey-sdk-csharp.sln --locked-mode
      - name: Pack (Release)
        run: |
          dotnet pack src/turnkey-sdk-csharp.csproj -c Release \
            --no-restore --output ./artifacts
      - name: Validate NuGet contents (README, LICENSE, NOTICE)
        run: |
          set -euo pipefail
          NUPKG=$(ls ./artifacts/KyuzanInc.Turnkey.Sdk.*.nupkg | head -1)
          echo "Validating $NUPKG"
          unzip -l "$NUPKG" | tee /tmp/contents.txt
          grep -q 'README.md' /tmp/contents.txt
          grep -q 'LICENSE'   /tmp/contents.txt
          grep -q 'NOTICE'    /tmp/contents.txt
      - name: Upload .nupkg + .snupkg artifacts
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v7
        with:
          name: nupkgs
          path: ./artifacts/**
