    72	/**
    73	 * Get PublicKey function
    74	 * Derives public key from Uint8Array or hexstring private key
    75	 *
    76	 * @param {Uint8Array | string} privateKey - The Uint8Array or hexstring representation of a compressed private key.
    77	 * @param {boolean} isCompressed - Specifies whether to return a compressed or uncompressed public key. Defaults to true.
    78	 * @returns {Uint8Array} - The public key in Uin8Array representation.
    79	 */
    80	export const getPublicKey = (
    81	  privateKey: Uint8Array | string,
    82	  isCompressed: boolean = true,
    83	): Uint8Array => {
    84	  return p256.getPublicKey(privateKey, isCompressed);

    87	/**
    88	 * HPKE Encrypt Function
    89	 * Encrypts data using Hybrid Public Key Encryption (HPKE) standard https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/rfc9180/.
    90	 *
    91	 * @param {HpkeEncryptParams} params - The encryption parameters including plain text, encapsulated key, and sender private key.
    92	 * @returns {Uint8Array} - The encrypted data.
    93	 */
    94	
    95	export const hpkeEncrypt = ({
    96	  plainTextBuf,
    97	  targetKeyBuf,
    98	}: HpkeEncryptParams): Uint8Array => {
    99	  try {
   100	    // Standard HPKE Mode (Ephemeral Key Pair)
   101	    const ephemeralKeyPair = generateP256KeyPair();
   102	    const senderPrivBuf = uint8ArrayFromHexString(ephemeralKeyPair.privateKey);
   103	    const senderPubBuf = uint8ArrayFromHexString(
   104	      ephemeralKeyPair.publicKeyUncompressed,
   105	    );
   106	
   107	    const aad = buildAdditionalAssociatedData(senderPubBuf, targetKeyBuf);
   108	
   109	    // Step 1: Generate Shared Secret
   110	    const ss = deriveSS(targetKeyBuf, uint8ArrayToHexString(senderPrivBuf!));
   111	
   112	    // Step 2: Generate the KEM context
   113	    const kemContext = getKemContext(
   114	      senderPubBuf,
   115	      uint8ArrayToHexString(targetKeyBuf),
   116	    );
   117	
   118	    // Step 3: Build the HKDF inputs for key derivation
   119	    let ikm = buildLabeledIkm(LABEL_EAE_PRK, ss, SUITE_ID_1);
   120	    let info = buildLabeledInfo(
   121	      LABEL_SHARED_SECRET,
   122	      kemContext,
   123	      SUITE_ID_1,
   124	      32,
   125	    );
   126	    const sharedSecret = extractAndExpand(new Uint8Array([]), ikm, info, 32);
   127	
   128	    // Step 4: Derive the AES key
   129	    ikm = buildLabeledIkm(LABEL_SECRET, new Uint8Array([]), SUITE_ID_2);
   130	    info = AES_KEY_INFO;
   131	    const key = extractAndExpand(sharedSecret, ikm, info, 32);
   132	
   133	    // Step 5: Derive the initialization vector
   134	    info = IV_INFO;
   135	    const iv = extractAndExpand(sharedSecret, ikm, info, 12);
   136	
   137	    // Step 6: Encrypt the data using AES-GCM
   138	    const encryptedData = aesGcmEncrypt(plainTextBuf, key, iv, aad);
   139	
   140	    // Step 7: Concatenate the encapsulated key and the encrypted data for output
   141	    const compressedSenderBuf = compressRawPublicKey(senderPubBuf);
   142	    const result = new Uint8Array(
   143	      compressedSenderBuf.length + encryptedData.length,
   144	    );
   145	    result.set(compressedSenderBuf, 0);
   146	    result.set(encryptedData, compressedSenderBuf.length);
   147	
   148	    return result;
   149	  } catch (error) {
   150	    throw new Error(`Unable to perform hpkeEncrypt: ${error}`);
   151	  }
   152	};
   153	
   154	/**
   155	 * HPKE Encrypt Function
   156	 * Encrypts data using Authenticated ,Hybrid Public Key Encryption (HPKE) standard https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/rfc9180/.
   157	 *
   158	 * @param {HpkeAuthEncryptParams} params - The encryption parameters including plain text, encapsulated key, and sender private key.

   181	    );

   189	      32,
   190	    );
   191	    const sharedSecret = extractAndExpand(new Uint8Array([]), ikm, info, 32);
   192	
   193	    // Step 4: Derive the AES key
   194	    ikm = buildLabeledIkm(LABEL_SECRET, new Uint8Array([]), SUITE_ID_2);
   195	    info = AES_KEY_INFO;
   196	    const key = extractAndExpand(sharedSecret, ikm, info, 32);
   197	
   198	    // Step 5: Derive the initialization vector
   199	    info = IV_INFO;
   200	    const iv = extractAndExpand(sharedSecret, ikm, info, 12);
   201	
   202	    // Step 6: Encrypt the data using AES-GCM
   203	    const encryptedData = aesGcmEncrypt(plainTextBuf, key, iv, aad);
   204

   206	    const compressedSenderBuf = compressRawPublicKey(senderPubBuf);
   207	    const result = new Uint8Array(

   209	    );
   210	    result.set(compressedSenderBuf, 0);
   211	    result.set(encryptedData, compressedSenderBuf.length);
   212	    return result;
   213	  } catch (error) {
   214	    throw new Error(`Unable to perform hpkeEncrypt: ${error}`);
   215	  }
   216	};
   217	
   218	/**
   219	 * Encrypt a message to a quorum key. Algorithm originally implemented in qos here: https://github.com/tkhq/qos/blob/ae01904c756107f850aea42000137ef124df3fe4/src/qos_p256/src/encrypt.rs#L123
   220	 * Returns a borsh serialized encrypted Envelope which is the nonce + ephemeralSenderPublicKey + encryptedMessage
   221	 * This function creates an ephemeral key, creates a shared secret with the recipient targetPublicKeyUncompressed
   222	 * creates additional associated data which follows the form: sender_public||sender_public_len||receiver_public||receiver_public_len
   223	 * encrypts using aes-gcm-256 with a SHA-512 HMAC over the QOS_ENCRYPTION_HMAC_MESSAGE literally: "qos_encryption_hmac_message"
   224	 * inserts and returns the necessary information in a borsh serialized envelope as described above
   225	 * This encryption function is meant to be used with this decryption function in QOS: https://github.com/tkhq/qos/blob/ae01904c756107f850aea42000137ef124df3fe4/src/qos_p256/src/encrypt.rs#L52
   226	 *
   227	 * @param {Uint8Array} targetPublicKeyUncompressed - The P256 uncompressed public key to encrypt the message to
   228	 * @param {Uint8Array} message - The message to encrypt to targetPublicKeyUncompressed
   229	 * @returns {Uint8Array} - A borsh serialized envelope containing the nonce + ephemeralSenderPublicKey + encrypted message
   230	 */
   231	export const quorumKeyEncrypt = async (
   232	  targetPublicKeyUncompressed: Uint8Array,
   233	  message: Uint8Array,
   234	): Promise<Uint8Array> => {
   235	  // generate an ephemeral keypair for this encryption operation
   236	  const ephemeralKeyPair = generateP256KeyPair();
   237	  const ephemeralSenderPublic = ephemeralKeyPair.publicKeyUncompressed;
   238	
   239	  // create a shared secret AES-GCM key with the SHA-512 HMAC
   240	  let cipher = await createQuorumKeyEncryptCipher(
   241	    uint8ArrayFromHexString(ephemeralSenderPublic),
   242	    uint8ArrayFromHexString(ephemeralKeyPair.privateKey),
   243	    targetPublicKeyUncompressed,
   244	  );
   245	
   246	  // generate a nonce
   247	  const nonce = new Uint8Array(QUORUM_ENCRYPT_NONCE_LENGTH_BYTES);
   248	  crypto.getRandomValues(nonce);
   249	
   250	  // create the additional data in the form of sender_public||sender_public_len||receiver_public||receiver_public_len taken from QOS here: https://github.com/tkhq/qos/blob/ae01904c756107f850aea42000137ef124df3fe4/src/qos_p256/src/encrypt.rs#L298
   251	  const aad = createAdditionalAssociatedData(
   252	    uint8ArrayFromHexString(ephemeralSenderPublic),
   253	    targetPublicKeyUncompressed,
   254	  );
   255	
   256	  // algorithm specifications for AES-GCM
   257	  const alg: AesGcmParams = {
   258	    name: "AES-GCM",
   259	    iv: nonce,
   260	    tagLength: 128,
   261	    additionalData: aad,
   262	  };
   263	
   264	  // encrypt the message with the shared secret
   265	  const encryptedMessageBuf = await crypto.subtle.encrypt(alg, cipher, message);
   266	
   267	  // create the envelope
   268	  let envelope: Envelope = {
   269	    nonce: nonce,
   270	    ephemeralSenderPublic: uint8ArrayFromHexString(ephemeralSenderPublic),
   271	    encryptedMessage: new Uint8Array(encryptedMessageBuf),
   272	  };
   273	
   274	  // borsh serialize the envelope
   275	  return borsh.serialize(EnvelopeSchema, envelope);
   276	};
   277	
   278	/**
   279	 * Format HPKE Buffer Function
   280	 * Returns a JSON string of an encrypted bundle, separating out the cipher text and the sender public key

     1	import { p256 } from "@noble/curves/p256";
     2	import { createHash } from "sha256-uint8array";
     3	import { uint8ArrayToHexString } from "@turnkey/encoding";
     4	
     5	export const signWithApiKey = async (input: {
     6	  content: string;
     7	  publicKey: string;
     8	  privateKey: string;
     9	}): Promise<string> => {
    10	  const publicKey = p256.getPublicKey(input.privateKey, true);
    11	
    12	  // Public key in the usual 02 or 03 + 64 hex digits
    13	  const publicKeyString = uint8ArrayToHexString(publicKey);
    14	
    15	  if (publicKeyString != input.publicKey) {
    16	    throw new Error(
    17	      `Bad API key. Expected to get public key ${input.publicKey}, got ${publicKeyString}`,
    18	    );
    19	  }
    20	
    21	  const hash = createHash().update(input.content).digest();
    22	  const signature = p256.sign(hash, input.privateKey);
    23	  return signature.toDERHex();
    24	};
     1	/// <reference lib="dom" />
     2	import { stringToBase64urlString } from "@turnkey/encoding";
     3	
     4	// Header name for an API key stamp
     5	const stampHeaderName = "X-Stamp";
     6	
     7	export type Runtime = "browser" | "node" | "purejs";
     8	
     9	export type TApiKeyStamperConfig = {
    10	  apiPublicKey: string;
    11	  apiPrivateKey: string;
    12	  runtimeOverride?: Runtime | undefined;
    13	};
    14	
    15	// `window.document` ensures that we're in a browser context
    16	// and `crypto.subtle` ensures that it supports the web crypto APIs
    17	// Inspired by https://github.com/flexdinesh/browser-or-node/blob/master/src/index.ts
    18	const isCryptoEnabledBrowser: boolean =
    19	  typeof window !== "undefined" &&
    20	  typeof window.document !== "undefined" &&
    21	  typeof crypto !== "undefined" &&
    22	  typeof crypto.subtle !== "undefined";
    23	
    24	// We check `process.versions.node`
    25	// Taken from https://github.com/flexdinesh/browser-or-node/blob/master/src/index.ts
    26	const isNode: boolean =
    27	  typeof process !== "undefined" &&
    28	  process.versions != null &&
    29	  process.versions.node != null;
    30	
    31	const detectRuntime = (): Runtime => {
    32	  if (isCryptoEnabledBrowser) {
    33	    return "browser";
    34	  }
    35	
    36	  if (isNode) {
    37	    return "node";
    38	  }
    39	
    40	  // If we don't have NodeJS or web crypto at our disposal, default to pure JS implementation
    41	  // This is the case for old browsers and react native environments
    42	  return "purejs";
    43	};
    44	
    45	/**
    46	 * Signature function abstracting the differences between NodeJS and web environments for signing with API keys.
    47	 */
    48	export const signWithApiKey = async (
    49	  input: {
    50	    content: string;
    51	    publicKey: string;
    52	    privateKey: string;
    53	  },
    54	  runtimeOverride?: Runtime | undefined,
    55	): Promise<string> => {
    56	  const runtime = runtimeOverride ?? detectRuntime();
    57	
    58	  switch (runtime) {
    59	    case "browser":
    60	      return (await import("./webcrypto")).signWithApiKey(input);
    61	    case "node":
    62	      return (await import("./nodecrypto")).signWithApiKey(input);
    63	    case "purejs":
    64	      return (await import("./purejs")).signWithApiKey(input);
    65	    default:
    66	      throw new Error(`Unsupported runtime: ${runtime}`);
    67	  }
    68	};
    69	
    70	/**
    71	 * Stamper to use with `@turnkey/http`'s `TurnkeyClient`
    72	 */
    73	export class ApiKeyStamper {
    74	  apiPublicKey: string;
    75	  apiPrivateKey: string;
    76	  runtimeOverride?: Runtime | undefined;
    77	
    78	  constructor(config: TApiKeyStamperConfig) {
    79	    this.apiPublicKey = config.apiPublicKey;
    80	    this.apiPrivateKey = config.apiPrivateKey;
    81	    this.runtimeOverride = config.runtimeOverride;
    82	  }
    83	
    84	  async stamp(payload: string) {
    85	    const signature = await signWithApiKey(
    86	      {
    87	        publicKey: this.apiPublicKey,
    88	        privateKey: this.apiPrivateKey,
    89	        content: payload,
    90	      },
    91	      this.runtimeOverride,
    92	    );
    93	
    94	    const stamp = {
    95	      publicKey: this.apiPublicKey,
    96	      scheme: "SIGNATURE_SCHEME_TK_API_P256",
    97	      signature,
    98	    };
    99	
   100	    return {
   101	      stampHeaderName,
   102	      stampHeaderValue: stringToBase64urlString(JSON.stringify(stamp)),
   103	    };
   104	  }
   105	}
   106	
   107	export { pointDecode } from "./tink/elliptic_curves";

    24

    26

    28	    content,
    29	    privateKey,

    31	  });
    32

    36	      content,
    37	      pemPublicKey,

    39	    }),
    40	  ).toBe(true);

    45	      content: "something else that wasn't stamped",

    47	      signature: signature,
    48	    });
    49	  }).toThrow();
    50	});
    51

    56	])("sign with openssl generated key pairs: $name", async ({ impl: stamp }) => {

    63

    66	          return String.fromCharCode(Math.floor(Math.random() * 65536));
    67	        }).join("");

    70	          content,

   301	/**
   302	 * HPKE Decrypt Function
   303	 * Decrypts data using Hybrid Public Key Encryption (HPKE) standard https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/rfc9180/.
   304	 *
   305	 * @param {HpkeDecryptParams} params - The decryption parameters including ciphertext, encapsulated key, and receiver private key.
   306	 * @returns {Uint8Array} - The decrypted data.
   307	 */
   308	export const hpkeDecrypt = ({
   309	  ciphertextBuf,
   310	  encappedKeyBuf,
   311	  receiverPriv,
   312	}: HpkeDecryptParams): Uint8Array => {
   313	  try {
   314	    let ikm: Uint8Array;
   315	    let info: Uint8Array;
   316	    const receiverPubBuf = getPublicKey(
   317	      uint8ArrayFromHexString(receiverPriv),
   318	      false,
   319	    );
   320	    const aad = buildAdditionalAssociatedData(encappedKeyBuf, receiverPubBuf); // Eventually we want users to be able to pass in aad as optional
   321	
   322	    // Step 1: Generate Shared Secret
   323	    const ss = deriveSS(encappedKeyBuf, receiverPriv);
   324	
   325	    // Step 2: Generate the KEM context
   326	    const kemContext = getKemContext(
   327	      encappedKeyBuf,
   328	      uint8ArrayToHexString(receiverPubBuf),
   329	    );
   330	
   331	    // Step 3: Build the HKDF inputs for key derivation
   332	    ikm = buildLabeledIkm(LABEL_EAE_PRK, ss, SUITE_ID_1);
   333	    info = buildLabeledInfo(LABEL_SHARED_SECRET, kemContext, SUITE_ID_1, 32);
   334	    const sharedSecret = extractAndExpand(new Uint8Array([]), ikm, info, 32);
   335	
   336	    // Step 4: Derive the AES key
   337	    ikm = buildLabeledIkm(LABEL_SECRET, new Uint8Array([]), SUITE_ID_2);
   338	    info = AES_KEY_INFO;
   339	    const key = extractAndExpand(sharedSecret, ikm, info, 32);
   340	
   341	    // Step 5: Derive the initialization vector
   342	    info = IV_INFO;
   343	    const iv = extractAndExpand(sharedSecret, ikm, info, 12);
   344	
   345	    // Step 6: Decrypt the data using AES-GCM
   346	    const decryptedData = aesGcmDecrypt(ciphertextBuf, key, iv, aad);
   347	    return decryptedData;
   348	  } catch (error) {
   349	    throw new Error(`Unable to perform hpkeDecrypt: ${error} `);
   350	  }
   351	};
   352	
   353	/**
   354	 * Generate a P-256 key pair. Contains the hexed privateKey, publicKey, and Uncompressed publicKey
   355	 *
   356	 * @returns {KeyPair} - The generated key pair.
   357	 */
   358	export const generateP256KeyPair = (): KeyPair => {
   359	  const privateKey = randomBytes(32);
   360	  const publicKey = getPublicKey(privateKey, true);
   361	  const publicKeyUncompressed = uint8ArrayToHexString(
   362	    uncompressRawPublicKey(publicKey),
   363	  );
   364	  return {
   365	    privateKey: uint8ArrayToHexString(privateKey),
   366	    publicKey: uint8ArrayToHexString(publicKey),
   367	    publicKeyUncompressed,
   368	  };
   369	};
   370	
   371	/**
   372	 * Create additional associated data (AAD) for AES-GCM decryption.
   373	 *
   374	 * @param {Uint8Array} senderPubBuf
   375	 * @param {Uint8Array} receiverPubBuf
   376	 * @return {Uint8Array} - The resulting concatenation of sender and receiver pubkeys.
   377	 */
   378	export const buildAdditionalAssociatedData = (
   379	  senderPubBuf: Uint8Array,
   380	  receiverPubBuf: Uint8Array,
   381	): Uint8Array => {
   382	  return new Uint8Array([
   383	    ...Array.from(senderPubBuf),
   384	    ...Array.from(receiverPubBuf),
   385	  ]);
   386	};
   387	
   388	/**
   389	 * Accepts a private key Uint8Array in the PKCS8 format, and returns the encapsulated private key.
   390	 *
   391	 * @param {Uint8Array} privateKey - A PKCS#8 private key structured with the key data at a specific position. The actual key starts at byte 36 and is 32 bytes long.
   392	 * @return {Uint8Array} - The private key.
   393	 */
   394	export const extractPrivateKeyFromPKCS8Bytes = (
   395	  privateKey: Uint8Array,
   396	): Uint8Array => {
   397	  return privateKey.slice(36, 36 + 32);
   398	};
   399	
   400	/**
   401	 * Accepts a public key Uint8Array, and returns a Uint8Array with the compressed version of the public key.
   402	 *
   403	 * @param {Uint8Array} rawPublicKey - The raw public key.
   404	 * @return {Uint8Array} – The compressed public key.
   405	 */
   406	export const compressRawPublicKey = (rawPublicKey: Uint8Array): Uint8Array => {
   407	  const len = rawPublicKey.byteLength;
   408	
   409	  // Drop the y coordinate
   410	  // Uncompressed key is in the form 0x04||x||y
   411	  // `len >>> 1` is a more concise way to write `floor(len/2)`
   412	  var compressedBytes = rawPublicKey.slice(0, (1 + len) >>> 1);
   413	
   414	  // Encode the parity of `y` in first bit
   415	  // `BYTE & 0x01` tests for parity and returns 0x00 when even, or 0x01 when odd
   416	  // Then `0x02 | <parity test result>` yields either 0x02 (even case) or 0x03 (odd).
   417	  compressedBytes[0] = 0x02 | (rawPublicKey[len - 1]! & 0x01);
   418	  return compressedBytes;
   419	};
   420	
   421	/**
   422	 * Accepts a public key array buffer, and returns a buffer with the uncompressed version of the public key
   423	 * @param {Uint8Array} rawPublicKey - The public key.
   424	 * @return {Uint8Array} - The uncompressed public key.
   425	 */
   426	export const uncompressRawPublicKey = (
   427	  rawPublicKey: Uint8Array,
   428	  curve: Curve = "CURVE_P256",
   429	): Uint8Array => {
   430	  if (rawPublicKey.length !== 33) {
   431	    throw new Error("failed to uncompress raw public key: invalid length");
   432	  }
   433	
   434	  if (!(rawPublicKey[0] === 2 || rawPublicKey[0] === 3)) {
   435	    throw new Error("failed to uncompress raw public key: invalid prefix");
   436	  }
   437	
   438	  // point[0] must be 2 (false) or 3 (true).
   439	  // this maps to the initial "02" or "03" prefix
   440	  const lsb = rawPublicKey[0] === 3;
   441	  const x = BigInt("0x" + uint8ArrayToHexString(rawPublicKey.subarray(1)));
   442	
   443	  let p: bigint, a: bigint, b: bigint;
   444	  if (curve === "CURVE_P256") {
   445	    // p-256 domain parameters
   446	    // https://nvlpubs.nist.gov/nistpubs/FIPS/NIST.FIPS.186-4.pdf (Appendix D).
   447	    p = BigInt(
   448	      "115792089210356248762697446949407573530086143415290314195533631308867097853951",
   449	    );
   450	    b = BigInt(
   451	      "0x5ac635d8aa3a93e7b3ebbd55769886bc651d06b0cc53b0f63bce3c3e27d2604b",
   452	    );
   453	    a = p - BigInt(3);
   454	  } else {
   455	    // secp256k1 domain parameters
   456	    // https://www.secg.org/sec2-v2.pdf (Section 2.4.1).
   457	    p = BigInt(
   458	      "0xfffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffffefffffc2f",
   459	    );
   460	    a = BigInt(0);
   461	    b = BigInt(7);
   462	  }
   463	
   464	  // Now compute y based on x
   465	  const rhs = ((x * x + a) * x + b) % p;
   466	  let y = modSqrt(rhs, p);
   467	  if (lsb !== testBit(y, 0)) {
   468	    y = (p - y) % p;
   469	  }
   470	
   471	  if (x < BigInt(0) || x >= p) {
   472	    throw new Error("x is out of range");
   473	  }
   474	
   475	  if (y < BigInt(0) || y >= p) {
   476	    throw new Error("y is out of range");
   477	  }
   478	
   479	  var uncompressedHexString = "04" + bigIntToHex(x, 64) + bigIntToHex(y, 64);
   480	  return uint8ArrayFromHexString(uncompressedHexString);
   481	};
   482	
   483	/**
   484	 * Build labeled Initial Key Material (IKM).
   485	 *
   486	 * @param {Uint8Array} label - The label to use.
   487	 * @param {Uint8Array} ikm - The input key material.
   488	 * @param {Uint8Array} suiteId - The suite identifier.
   489	 * @returns {Uint8Array} - The labeled IKM.
   490	 */
   491	const buildLabeledIkm = (
   492	  label: Uint8Array,
   493	  ikm: Uint8Array,
   494	  suiteId: Uint8Array,
   495	): Uint8Array => {
   496	  const combinedLength =
   497	    HPKE_VERSION.length + suiteId.length + label.length + ikm.length;
   498	  const ret = new Uint8Array(combinedLength);
   499	  let offset = 0;
   500	
   501	  ret.set(HPKE_VERSION, offset);
   502	  offset += HPKE_VERSION.length;
   503	
   504	  ret.set(suiteId, offset);
   505	  offset += suiteId.length;
   506	
   507	  ret.set(label, offset);
   508	  offset += label.length;
   509	
   510	  ret.set(ikm, offset);
   511	
   512	  return ret;
   513	};
   514	
   515	/**
   516	 * Build labeled info for HKDF operations.
   517	 *
   518	 * @param {Uint8Array} label - The label to use.
   519	 * @param {Uint8Array} info - Additional information.
   520	 * @param {Uint8Array} suiteId - The suite identifier.
   521	 * @param {number} len - The output length.
   522	 * @returns {Uint8Array} - The labeled info.
   523	 */
   524	const buildLabeledInfo = (
   525	  label: Uint8Array,
   526	  info: Uint8Array,
   527	  suiteId: Uint8Array,
   528	  len: number,
   529	): Uint8Array => {
   530	  const suiteIdStartIndex = 9; // first two are reserved for length bytes (unused in this case), the next 7 are for the HPKE_VERSION, then the suiteId starts at 9
   531	  const ret = new Uint8Array(
   532	    suiteIdStartIndex + suiteId.byteLength + label.byteLength + info.byteLength,
   533	  );
   534	  ret.set(new Uint8Array([0, len]), 0); // this isn’t an error, we’re starting at index 2 because the first two bytes should be 0. See <https://github.com/dajiaji/hpke-js/blob/1e7fb1372fbcdb6d06bf2f4fa27ff676329d633e/src/kdfs/hkdf.ts#L41> for reference.
   535	  ret.set(HPKE_VERSION, 2);
   536	  ret.set(suiteId, suiteIdStartIndex);
   537	  ret.set(label, suiteIdStartIndex + suiteId.byteLength);
   538	  ret.set(info, suiteIdStartIndex + suiteId.byteLength + label.byteLength);
   539	  return ret;
   540	};
   541	
   542	/**
   543	 * Perform HKDF extract and expand operations.
   544	 */
   545	const extractAndExpand = (
   546	  sharedSecret: Uint8Array,
   547	  ikm: Uint8Array,
   548	  info: Uint8Array,
   549	  len: number,
   550	): Uint8Array => {
   551	  const prk = hkdf.extract(sha256, ikm, sharedSecret);
   552	  const resp = hkdf.expand(sha256, prk, info, len);
   553	  return new Uint8Array(resp);
   554	};
   555	
   556	/**
   557	 * Derive the Diffie-Hellman shared secret using ECDH.
   558	 */
   559	const deriveSS = (encappedKeyBuf: Uint8Array, priv: string): Uint8Array => {
   560	  const ss = p256.getSharedSecret(
   561	    uint8ArrayFromHexString(priv),
   562	    encappedKeyBuf,
   563	  );
   564	  return ss.slice(1);
   565	};
   566	
   567	/**
   568	 * Encrypt data using AES-GCM.
   569	 */
   570	const aesGcmEncrypt = (
   571	  plainTextData: Uint8Array,
   572	  key: Uint8Array,
   573	  iv: Uint8Array,
   574	  aad?: Uint8Array,
   575	): Uint8Array => {
   576	  const aes = gcm(key, iv, aad);
   577	  const data = aes.encrypt(plainTextData);
   578	  return data;
   579	};
   580	
   581	/**
   582	 * Decrypt data using AES-GCM.
   583	 */
   584	const aesGcmDecrypt = (
   585	  encryptedData: Uint8Array,
   586	  key: Uint8Array,
   587	  iv: Uint8Array,
   588	  aad?: Uint8Array,
   589	): Uint8Array => {
   590	  const aes = gcm(key, iv, aad);
   591	  const data = aes.decrypt(encryptedData);
   592	  return data;
   593	};
   594	
   595	/**
   596	 * Generate a Key Encapsulation Mechanism (KEM) context.
   597	 */
   598	const getKemContext = (
   599	  encappedKeyBuf: Uint8Array,
   600	  publicKey: string,
   601	): Uint8Array => {
   602	  const encappedKeyArray = new Uint8Array(encappedKeyBuf);
   603	  const publicKeyArray = uint8ArrayFromHexString(publicKey);
   604	
   605	  const kemContext = new Uint8Array(
   606	    encappedKeyArray.length + publicKeyArray.length,
   607	  );
   608	  kemContext.set(encappedKeyArray);
   609	  kemContext.set(publicKeyArray, encappedKeyArray.length);
   610	
   611	  return kemContext;
   612	};
   613	
   614	/**
   615	 * Convert a BigInt to a hexadecimal string of a specific length.
   616	 */
   617	const bigIntToHex = (num: bigint, length: number): string => {
   618	  const hexString = num.toString(16);
   619	  if (hexString.length > length) {
   620	    throw new Error(
   621	      `number cannot fit in a hex string of ${length} characters`,
   622	    );
   623	  }
   624	  return hexString.padStart(length, "0");
   625	};
   626	
   627	/**
   628	 * Converts an ASN.1 DER-encoded ECDSA signature to the raw format used for verification.
   629	 *
   630	 * @param {string} derSignature - The DER-encoded signature.
   631	 * @returns {Uint8Array} - The raw signature.
   632	 */
   633	export const fromDerSignature = (derSignature: string): Uint8Array => {
   634	  const derSignatureBuf = uint8ArrayFromHexString(derSignature);
   635	
   636	  // Check minimum length
   637	  if (derSignatureBuf.length < 2) {
   638	    throw new Error(
   639	      "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: insufficient length",
   640	    );
   641	  }
   642	
   643	  // Check SEQUENCE tag (0x30 at first byte)
   644	  if (derSignatureBuf[0] !== 0x30) {
   645	    throw new Error(
   646	      "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: invalid format (missing SEQUENCE tag)",
   647	    );
   648	  }
   649	
   650	  // Check second byte, start of length field
   651	  let index = 1;
   652	  const lengthByte = derSignatureBuf[index]!;
   653	  if (lengthByte <= 0x7f) {
   654	    // Short form: single byte length
   655	
   656	    // directly take the consumed value as length and check against buffer
   657	    // buffer length: initial header bytes + claimed remaining length
   658	    if (derSignatureBuf.length < 1 + 1 + lengthByte) {
   659	      throw new Error(
   660	        "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: inconsistent message length header",
   661	      );
   662	    }
   663	
   664	    // continue parsing
   665	    index += 1;
   666	  } else {
   667	    // Multi-byte DER length header
   668	    // Invalid DER values: lengthByte 0x80 and 0xff
   669	    // Valid DER values: lengthByte > 0x80, < 0xff
   670	    //
   671	    // We do not expect signature data in the Long form notation
   672	    // -> reject all such inputs
   673	    //
   674	    // More complex parsing for longer signature sequences can be implemented once needed
   675	    throw new Error(
   676	      "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: unexpectedly large or invalid signature length",
   677	    );
   678	  }
   679	
   680	  // Parse 'r' and check for integer tag (0x02)
   681	  if (derSignatureBuf[index] !== 0x02) {
   682	    throw new Error(
   683	      "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: invalid tag for r",
   684	    );
   685	  }
   686	
   687	  index++; // Move past the INTEGER tag
   688	  const rLength = derSignatureBuf[index]!;
   689	
   690	  // Allow up to 32 data bytes + 1 byte 0-padding prefix
   691	  if (rLength > 33) {
   692	    throw new Error(
   693	      "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: unexpected length for r",
   694	    );
   695	  }
   696	
   697	  index++; // Move past the length byte
   698	  const r = derSignatureBuf.slice(index, index + rLength);
   699	  index += rLength; // Move to the start of s
   700	
   701	  // Parse 's' and check for integer tag (0x02)
   702	  if (derSignatureBuf[index] !== 0x02) {
   703	    throw new Error(
   704	      "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: invalid tag for s",
   705	    );
   706	  }
   707	
   708	  index++; // Move past the INTEGER tag
   709	  const sLength = derSignatureBuf[index]!;
   710	
   711	  // Allow up to 32 data bytes + 1 byte 0-padding prefix
   712	  if (sLength > 33) {
   713	    throw new Error(
   714	      "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: unexpected length for s",
   715	    );
   716	  }
   717	
   718	  index++; // Move past the length byte
   719	  const s = derSignatureBuf.slice(index, index + sLength);
   720	
   721	  // Normalize 'r' and 's' to 32 bytes each
   722	  const rPadded = normalizePadding(r, 32);
   723	  const sPadded = normalizePadding(s, 32);
   724	
   725	  // Concatenate and return the raw signature
   726	  return new Uint8Array([...rPadded, ...sPadded]);
   727	};
   728	
   729	/**
   730	 * Converts a raw ECDSA signature to DER-encoded format.
   731	 *
   732	 * This function takes a raw ECDSA signature, which is a concatenation of two 32-byte integers (r and s),
   733	 * and converts it into the DER-encoded format. DER (Distinguished Encoding Rules) is a binary encoding
   734	 * for data structures described by ASN.1.
   735	 *
   736	 * @param {string} rawSignature - The raw signature in hexadecimal string format.
   737	 * @returns {string} - The DER-encoded signature in hexadecimal string format.
   738	 *
   739	 * @throws {Error} - Throws an error if the input signature is invalid or if the encoding process fails.
   740	 *
   741	 * @example
   742	 * // Example usage:
   743	 * const rawSignature = "0x487cdb8a88f2f4044b701cbb116075c4cabe5fe4657a6358b395c0aab70694db3453a8057e442bd1aff0ecabe8a82c831f0edd7f2158b7c1feb3de9b1f20309b1c";
   744	 * const derSignature = toDerSignature(rawSignature);
   745	 * console.log(derSignature); // Outputs the DER-encoded signature as a hex string
   746	 * // "30440220487cdb8a88f2f4044b701cbb116075c4cabe5fe4657a6358b395c0aab70694db02203453a8057e442bd1aff0ecabe8a82c831f0edd7f2158b7c1feb3de9b1f20309b"
   747	 */
   748	export const toDerSignature = (rawSignature: string) => {
   749	  const rawSignatureBuf = uint8ArrayFromHexString(rawSignature);
   750	
   751	  // Split raw signature into r and s, each 32 bytes
   752	  const r = rawSignatureBuf.slice(0, 32);
   753	  const s = rawSignatureBuf.slice(32, 64);
   754	
   755	  // Helper function to encode an integer with DER structure
   756	  const encodeDerInteger = (integer?: Uint8Array): Uint8Array => {
   757	    // Check if integer is defined and has at least one byte
   758	    if (
   759	      integer === undefined ||
   760	      integer.length === 0 ||
   761	      integer[0] === undefined
   762	    ) {
   763	      throw new Error("Invalid integer: input is undefined or empty.");
   764	    }
   765	
   766	    // Add a leading zero if the integer's most significant byte is >= 0x80
   767	    const needsPadding = integer[0] & 0x80;
   768	    const paddedInteger = needsPadding
   769	      ? new Uint8Array([0x00, ...integer])
   770	      : integer;
   771	
   772	    // Prepend the integer tag (0x02) and length
   773	    return new Uint8Array([0x02, paddedInteger.length, ...paddedInteger]);
   774	  };
   775	
   776	  // DER encode r and s
   777	  const rEncoded = encodeDerInteger(r);
   778	  const sEncoded = encodeDerInteger(s);
   779	
   780	  // Combine as a DER sequence: 0x30, total length, rEncoded, sEncoded
   781	  const derSignature = new Uint8Array([
   782	    0x30,
   783	    rEncoded.length + sEncoded.length,
   784	    ...rEncoded,
   785	    ...sEncoded,
   786	  ]);
   787	
   788	  return uint8ArrayToHexString(derSignature);
   789	};
   790	
   791	/**
   792	 * Create a shared AES-GCM secret with the quorum key encryption SHA-512 HMAC
   793	 *
   794	 * This function takes an ephemeral Sender public key generated for each encryption operation
   795	 * the corresponding ephemeral private key, and the target public key uncompressed
   796	 * for data structures described by ASN.1.
   797	 *
   798	 * @param {Uint8Array} ephemeralSenderPublic - The ephemeral public key used to create the preImage
   799	 * @param {Uint8Array} ephemeralSenderPrivate - The ephemeral private key to create the shared secret with
   800	 * @param {Uint8Array} targetPublicKeyUncompressed - The public key to create the shared secret with and encrypt the message to
   801	 * @returns {Promise<CryptoKey>} - A shared secret AES-GCM key between ephemeralSenderPrivate and the targetPublicKeyUncompressed
   802	 */
   803	async function createQuorumKeyEncryptCipher(
   804	  ephemeralSenderPublic: Uint8Array,
   805	  ephemeralSenderPrivate: Uint8Array,
   806	  targetPublicKeyUncompressed: Uint8Array,
   807	): Promise<CryptoKey> {
   808	  // create the shared secret between ephemeralSenderPrivate and targetPublicKeyUncompressed
   809	  const sharedSecretUncompressed = p256.getSharedSecret(
   810	    ephemeralSenderPrivate,
   811	    targetPublicKeyUncompressed,
   812	    false,
   813	  );
   814	  const sharedSecret = sharedSecretUncompressed.slice(1, 33);
   815	
   816	  // create the preImage as defined in qos here: https://github.com/tkhq/qos/blob/ae01904c756107f850aea42000137ef124df3fe4/src/qos_p256/src/encrypt.rs#L273-L282
   817	  let preImage = new Uint8Array(
   818	    ephemeralSenderPublic.length +
   819	      targetPublicKeyUncompressed.length +
   820	      sharedSecret.length,
   821	  );
   822	  preImage.set(ephemeralSenderPublic, 0);
   823	  preImage.set(targetPublicKeyUncompressed, ephemeralSenderPublic.length);
   824	  preImage.set(
   825	    sharedSecret,
   826	    ephemeralSenderPublic.length + targetPublicKeyUncompressed.length,
   827	  );
   828	
   829	  // create the HMAC key and create an HMAC using QOS_ENCRYPTION_HMAC_MESSAGE
   830	  const hmacKey = await crypto.subtle.importKey(
   831	    "raw",
   832	    preImage,
   833	    {
   834	      name: "HMAC",
   835	      hash: "SHA-512",
   836	    },
   837	    false,
   838	    ["sign"],
   839	  );
   840	  const mac = new Uint8Array(
   841	    await crypto.subtle.sign("HMAC", hmacKey, QOS_ENCRYPTION_HMAC_MESSAGE),
   842	  );
   843	
   844	  // Use the first 32 bytes as the AES-GCM key
   845	  const aesKeyRaw = mac.slice(0, 32);
   846	
   847	  return crypto.subtle.importKey(
   848	    "raw",
   849	    aesKeyRaw,
   850	    {
   851	      name: "AES-GCM",
   852	    },
   853	    false,
   854	    ["encrypt"],
   855	  );
   856	}
   857	
   858	/// Helper function to create the additional associated data (AAD). The data is
   859	/// of the form `sender_public||sender_public_len||receiver_public||receiver_public_len`.
   860	/// This is taken from QOS here: https://github.com/tkhq/qos/blob/ae01904c756107f850aea42000137ef124df3fe4/src/qos_p256/src/encrypt.rs#L298
   861	///
   862	/// Note that we append the length to each field as per NIST specs here: <https://nvlpubs.nist.gov/nistpubs/SpecialPublications/NIST.SP.800-56Ar3.pdf/>. See section 5.8.2.
   863	function createAdditionalAssociatedData(
   864	  ephemeralSenderPublic: Uint8Array,
   865	  receiverPublic: Uint8Array,
   866	): Uint8Array {
   867	  // get the length of the sending and receiver public keys
   868	  const ephemeralSenderLength = ephemeralSenderPublic.length;
   869	  const receiverPublicLength = receiverPublic.length;
   870	
   871	  // ensure the lengths are under 1 byte
   872	  if (ephemeralSenderLength > 255 || receiverPublicLength > 255)
   873	    throw new Error("AAD len fields are 1 byte");
   874	
   875	  // allocate an array the size of both keys + 1 byte for their length
   876	  const aad = new Uint8Array(
   877	    ephemeralSenderLength + 1 + receiverPublicLength + 1,
   878	  );
   879	
   880	  // keep track of the offset within the array

 succeeded in 120ms:

   128	        /// <c>"CURVE_P256" | "CURVE_SECP256K1"</c> exposed by

   395	
   396	        /// <summary>
   397	        /// HPKE-Base mode decrypt (P-256 / HKDF-SHA256 / AES-128-GCM).
   398	        /// Equivalent to upstream <c>crypto.ts hpkeDecrypt</c>.
   399	        /// </summary>
   400	        /// <exception cref="InvalidOperationException">
   401	        /// Wraps any underlying decryption failure with the upstream
   402	        /// message <c>"Unable to perform hpkeDecrypt: ..."</c>.
   403	        /// </exception>
   404	        public static byte[] HpkeDecrypt(HpkeDecryptParams parameters)
   405	        {
   406	            try
   407	            {
   408	                if (parameters == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters));
   409	                var ciphertextBuf = parameters.CiphertextBuf
   410	                                    ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters.CiphertextBuf));
   411	                var encappedKeyBuf = parameters.EncappedKeyBuf
   412	                                     ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters.EncappedKeyBuf));
   413	                var receiverPriv = parameters.ReceiverPriv
   414	                                   ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters.ReceiverPriv));
   415	
   416	                var receiverPrivBytes = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(receiverPriv);
   417	                var receiverPubBuf = GetPublicKey(receiverPrivBytes, false);
   418	
   419	                var aad = BuildAdditionalAssociatedData(encappedKeyBuf, receiverPubBuf);
   420	                var ss = DeriveSS(encappedKeyBuf, receiverPriv);
   421	                var kemContext = GetKemContext(encappedKeyBuf, Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString(receiverPubBuf));
   422	
   423	                var ikm = BuildLabeledIkm(Constants.LABEL_EAE_PRK, ss, Constants.SUITE_ID_1);
   424	                var info = BuildLabeledInfo(Constants.LABEL_SHARED_SECRET, kemContext, Constants.SUITE_ID_1, 32);
   425	                var sharedSecret = ExtractAndExpand(Array.Empty<byte>(), ikm, info, 32);
   426	
   427	                ikm = BuildLabeledIkm(Constants.LABEL_SECRET, Array.Empty<byte>(), Constants.SUITE_ID_2);
   428	                info = Constants.AES_KEY_INFO;
   429	                var key = ExtractAndExpand(sharedSecret, ikm, info, 32);
   430	
   431	                info = Constants.IV_INFO;
   432	                var iv = ExtractAndExpand(sharedSecret, ikm, info, 12);
   433	
   434	                return AesGcmDecrypt(ciphertextBuf, key, iv, aad);
   435	            }
   436	            catch (Exception error)
   437	            {
   438	                throw new InvalidOperationException(
   439	                    "Unable to perform hpkeDecrypt: " + error.Message + " ", error);
   440	            }
   441	        }
   442	
   443	        /// <summary>
   444	        /// HPKE-Base mode encrypt (P-256 / HKDF-SHA256 / AES-128-GCM).
   445	        /// Equivalent to upstream <c>crypto.ts hpkeEncrypt</c>.
   446	        /// </summary>
   447	        /// <returns>
   448	        /// The byte concatenation
   449	        /// <c>compressed(senderPub) || ciphertext</c>, ready to feed to
   450	        /// <see cref="FormatHpkeBuf"/> or <see cref="DecryptCredentialBundle"/>.
   451	        /// </returns>
   452	        /// <exception cref="InvalidOperationException">
   453	        /// Wraps any underlying failure with the upstream message
   454	        /// <c>"Unable to perform hpkeEncrypt: ..."</c>.
   455	        /// </exception>
   456	        public static byte[] HpkeEncrypt(HpkeEncryptParams parameters)
   457	        {
   458	            try
   459	            {
   460	                if (parameters == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters));
   461	                var plainTextBuf = parameters.PlainTextBuf
   462	                                   ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters.PlainTextBuf));
   463	                var targetKeyBuf = parameters.TargetKeyBuf
   464	                                   ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters.TargetKeyBuf));
   465	
   466	                var ephemeralKeyPair = GenerateP256KeyPair();
   467	                var senderPrivBuf = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(ephemeralKeyPair.PrivateKey);
   468	                var senderPubBuf = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(ephemeralKeyPair.PublicKeyUncompressed);
   469	
   470	                var aad = BuildAdditionalAssociatedData(senderPubBuf, targetKeyBuf);
   471	                var ss = DeriveSS(targetKeyBuf, Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString(senderPrivBuf));
   472	                var kemContext = GetKemContext(senderPubBuf, Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString(targetKeyBuf));
   473	
   474	                var ikm = BuildLabeledIkm(Constants.LABEL_EAE_PRK, ss, Constants.SUITE_ID_1);
   475	                var info = BuildLabeledInfo(Constants.LABEL_SHARED_SECRET, kemContext, Constants.SUITE_ID_1, 32);
   476	                var sharedSecret = ExtractAndExpand(Array.Empty<byte>(), ikm, info, 32);
   477	
   478	                ikm = BuildLabeledIkm(Constants.LABEL_SECRET, Array.Empty<byte>(), Constants.SUITE_ID_2);
   479	                info = Constants.AES_KEY_INFO;
   480	                var key = ExtractAndExpand(sharedSecret, ikm, info, 32);
   481	
   482	                info = Constants.IV_INFO;
   483	                var iv = ExtractAndExpand(sharedSecret, ikm, info, 12);
   484	
   485	                var encryptedData = AesGcmEncrypt(plainTextBuf, key, iv, aad);
   486	                var compressedSenderBuf = CompressRawPublicKey(senderPubBuf);
   487	                return Encoding.ConcatUint8Arrays(compressedSenderBuf, encryptedData);
   488	            }
   489	            catch (Exception error)
   490	            {
   780	        /// </summary>
   781	        public static string DecryptExportBundle(DecryptExportBundleParams parameters)
   782	        {
   783	            if (parameters == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters));
   784	            if (parameters.ExportBundle == null)
   785	                throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(parameters.ExportBundle));
   786	
   787	            // Upstream order, exactly:
   788	            //   1. enter try
   789	            //   2. JSON.parse(exportBundle)
   790	            //   3. verifyEnclaveSignature(...)
   791	            //   4. parse signed data, check organizationId, encappedPublic
   792	            //   5. hpkeDecrypt
   793	            //   6. format output (SOLANA / mnemonic / hex)
   794	            //   catch -> "Error decrypting bundle: ..."
   795	            try
   796	            {
   797	                using var bundleDoc = JsonDocument.Parse(parameters.ExportBundle);
   798	                var parsedExportBundle = bundleDoc.RootElement;
   799	
   800	                string? enclaveQuorumPublic = GetStringOrNull(parsedExportBundle, "enclaveQuorumPublic");
   801	                string? dataSignature = GetStringOrNull(parsedExportBundle, "dataSignature");
   802	                string? dataHex = GetStringOrNull(parsedExportBundle, "data");
   803	
   804	                bool verified = VerifyEnclaveSignature(
   805	                    enclaveQuorumPublic,
   806	                    dataSignature,
   807	                    dataHex,
   808	                    parameters.DangerouslyOverrideSignerPublicKey);
   809	                if (!verified)
   810	                {
   811	                    throw new InvalidOperationException(
   812	                        "failed to verify enclave signature: " + parameters.ExportBundle);
   813	                }
   814	
   815	                var signedDataBytes = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(dataHex!);
   816	                using var signedDoc = JsonDocument.Parse(System.Text.Encoding.UTF8.GetString(signedDataBytes));
   817	                var signedData = signedDoc.RootElement;
   818	
   819	                string? bundleOrgId = GetStringOrNull(signedData, "organizationId");
   820	                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(bundleOrgId)
   821	                    || !string.Equals(bundleOrgId, parameters.OrganizationId, StringComparison.Ordinal))
   822	                {
   823	                    throw new InvalidOperationException(
   824	                        "organization id does not match expected value. Expected: " + parameters.OrganizationId
   825	                        + ". Found: " + bundleOrgId + ".");
   826	                }
   827	
   828	                string? encappedPublic = GetStringOrNull(signedData, "encappedPublic");
   829	                if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(encappedPublic))
   830	                {
   831	                    throw new InvalidOperationException("missing \"encappedPublic\" in bundle signed data");
   832	                }
   833	                string? ciphertextStr = GetStringOrNull(signedData, "ciphertext");
   834	
   835	                var encappedKeyBuf = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(encappedPublic!);
   836	                var ciphertextBuf = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(ciphertextStr!);
   837	
   838	                var decryptedData = HpkeDecrypt(new HpkeDecryptParams
   839	                {
   840	                    CiphertextBuf = ciphertextBuf,
   841	                    EncappedKeyBuf = encappedKeyBuf,
   842	                    ReceiverPriv = parameters.EmbeddedKey,
   843	                });
   844	
   845	                if (string.Equals(parameters.KeyFormat, "SOLANA", StringComparison.Ordinal)
   846	                    && !parameters.ReturnMnemonic)
   847	                {
   848	                    if (decryptedData.Length != 32)
   849	                    {
   850	                        throw new InvalidOperationException(
   851	                            "invalid private key length. Expected 32 bytes. Got " + decryptedData.Length + ".");
   852	                    }
   853	                    // Derive Ed25519 public key from the 32-byte seed via BouncyCastle.
   854	                    var ed25519PrivKey = new Ed25519PrivateKeyParameters(decryptedData, 0);
   855	                    var publicKeyBytes = ed25519PrivKey.GeneratePublicKey().GetEncoded();
   856	                    if (publicKeyBytes.Length != 32)
   857	                    {
   858	                        throw new InvalidOperationException(
   859	                            "invalid public key length. Expected 32 bytes. Got " + publicKeyBytes.Length + ".");
   860	                    }
   861	                    var concatenated = new byte[64];
   862	                    Array.Copy(decryptedData, 0, concatenated, 0, 32);
   863	                    Array.Copy(publicKeyBytes, 0, concatenated, 32, 32);
   864	                    return Encoding.Base58Encode(concatenated);
   865	                }
   866	
   867	                var decryptedHex = Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString(decryptedData);
   868	                return parameters.ReturnMnemonic ? Encoding.HexToAscii(decryptedHex) : decryptedHex;
   869	            }
   870	            catch (Exception error)

   146	        /// <summary>
   147	        /// Mirror of upstream <c>purejs.ts signWithApiKey</c>. Verifies that
   148	        /// the configured public key matches the one derived from the
   149	        /// configured private key, then SHA-256-hashes the payload and signs
   150	        /// it with deterministic ECDSA (RFC 6979 + low-S) returning the
   151	        /// DER-encoded signature as a hex string.
   152	        /// </summary>
   153	        public string SignWithApiKey(string content)
   154	        {
   155	            if (content == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(content));
   156	
   157	            // Upstream `purejs.ts`:
   158	            //   const publicKey = p256.getPublicKey(input.privateKey, true);
   159	            //   const publicKeyString = uint8ArrayToHexString(publicKey);
   160	            //   if (publicKeyString != input.publicKey) throw new Error(...);
   161	            //
   162	            // Crypto.GetPublicKey enforces the noble invariants (exact 32-byte
   163	            // private key, scalar in [1, n - 1]) before deriving the public
   164	            // key. Per the upstream pattern this validation happens at sign
   165	            // time, not at constructor time.
   166	            byte[] derivedPublicKeyBytes = Crypto.GetPublicKey(_apiPrivateKey, isCompressed: true);
   167	            string derivedPublicKey = Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString(derivedPublicKeyBytes);
   168	            if (!string.Equals(derivedPublicKey, _apiPublicKey, StringComparison.Ordinal))
   169	            {
   170	                throw new InvalidOperationException(
   171	                    "Bad API key. Expected to get public key " + _apiPublicKey
   172	                    + ", got " + derivedPublicKey);
   173	            }
   174	
   175	            // Upstream:
   176	            //   const hash = createHash().update(input.content).digest();   // SHA-256
   177	            //   const signature = p256.sign(hash, input.privateKey);        // RFC 6979 + lowS
   178	            //   return signature.toDERHex();
   179	            var curve = ECNamedCurveTable.GetByName(CryptoConstants.CURVE_NAME);
   180	            var domainParams = new ECDomainParameters(curve.Curve, curve.G, curve.N, curve.H, curve.GetSeed());
   181	            var privateKeyBytes = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(_apiPrivateKey);
   182	            var privateKeyScalar = new BigInteger(1, privateKeyBytes);
   183	
   184	            byte[] payloadBytes = System.Text.Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(content);
   185	
   186	            var digest = DigestUtilities.GetDigest("SHA-256");
   187	            digest.BlockUpdate(payloadBytes, 0, payloadBytes.Length);
   188	            var hash = new byte[digest.GetDigestSize()];
   189	            digest.DoFinal(hash, 0);
   190	
   191	            var hmacCalculator = new HMacDsaKCalculator(DigestUtilities.GetDigest("SHA-256"));
   192	            var signer = new ECDsaSigner(hmacCalculator);
   193	            signer.Init(true, new ECPrivateKeyParameters(privateKeyScalar, domainParams));
   194	
   195	            BigInteger[] signature = signer.GenerateSignature(hash);
   196	            BigInteger r = signature[0];
   197	            BigInteger s = signature[1];
   198	
   199	            // Low-S normalization. @turnkey/api-key-stamper@0.5.0 depends on
   200	            // @noble/curves@^1.3.0, and noble v1.3.0
   201	            // (src/abstract/weierstrass.ts) defaults to lowS=true:
   202	            //   let { lowS, prehash, extraEntropy: ent } = opts;
   203	            //   if (lowS == null) lowS = true; // RFC6979 3.2
   204	            // The upstream purejs.ts call `p256.sign(hash, privateKey)` passes
   205	            // no opts, so the runtime emits low-S signatures. We reproduce
   206	            // that here by clamping s into (0, n/2].
   207	            BigInteger halfN = domainParams.N.ShiftRight(1);
   208	            if (s.CompareTo(halfN) > 0)
   209	            {
   210	                s = domainParams.N.Subtract(s);
   211	            }
   212	
   213	            return EncodeDerSignatureHex(r, s);
   214	        }
   215	
   216	        /// <summary>
   217	        /// Encode the <c>(r, s)</c> pair as a DER ASN.1 SEQUENCE of two
   218	        /// INTEGERs, then hex-encode the result.
   219	        /// Equivalent to noble's <c>signature.toDERHex()</c>.
   220	        /// </summary>
   221	        private static string EncodeDerSignatureHex(BigInteger r, BigInteger s)
   222	        {
   223	            byte[] rBytes = r.ToByteArrayUnsigned();
   224	            byte[] sBytes = s.ToByteArrayUnsigned();
   225	
   226	            bool rNeedsPadding = rBytes.Length > 0 && (rBytes[0] & 0x80) != 0;
   227	            bool sNeedsPadding = sBytes.Length > 0 && (sBytes[0] & 0x80) != 0;
   228	            int rLen = rBytes.Length + (rNeedsPadding ? 1 : 0);
   229	            int sLen = sBytes.Length + (sNeedsPadding ? 1 : 0);
   230	
   231	            int contentLen = 2 + rLen + 2 + sLen; // (INTEGER tag + length) * 2 + r + s
   232	
   233	            using (var ms = new MemoryStream())
   234	            {
   235	                ms.WriteByte(0x30); // SEQUENCE
   236	
   237	                if (contentLen >= 128)
   238	                {
   239	                    // Long-form length (1 octet count). For ECDSA P-256
   240	                    // signatures the total length never exceeds 0x7f in

     1	'use strict';
     2	
     3	var encoding = require('@turnkey/encoding');
     4	var elliptic_curves = require('./tink/elliptic_curves.js');
     5	
     6	/// <reference lib="dom" />
     7	// Header name for an API key stamp
     8	const stampHeaderName = "X-Stamp";
     9	// `window.document` ensures that we're in a browser context
    10	// and `crypto.subtle` ensures that it supports the web crypto APIs
    11	// Inspired by https://github.com/flexdinesh/browser-or-node/blob/master/src/index.ts
    12	const isCryptoEnabledBrowser = typeof window !== "undefined" &&
    13	    typeof window.document !== "undefined" &&
    14	    typeof crypto !== "undefined" &&
    15	    typeof crypto.subtle !== "undefined";
    16	// We check `process.versions.node`
    17	// Taken from https://github.com/flexdinesh/browser-or-node/blob/master/src/index.ts
    18	const isNode = typeof process !== "undefined" &&
    19	    process.versions != null &&
    20	    process.versions.node != null;
    21	const detectRuntime = () => {
    22	    if (isCryptoEnabledBrowser) {
    23	        return "browser";
    24	    }
    25	    if (isNode) {
    26	        return "node";
    27	    }
    28	    // If we don't have NodeJS or web crypto at our disposal, default to pure JS implementation
    29	    // This is the case for old browsers and react native environments
    30	    return "purejs";
    31	};
    32	/**
    33	 * Signature function abstracting the differences between NodeJS and web environments for signing with API keys.
    34	 */
    35	const signWithApiKey = async (input, runtimeOverride) => {
    36	    const runtime = runtimeOverride ?? detectRuntime();
    37	    switch (runtime) {
    38	        case "browser":
    39	            return (await Promise.resolve().then(function () { return require('./webcrypto.js'); })).signWithApiKey(input);
    40	        case "node":
    41	            return (await Promise.resolve().then(function () { return require('./nodecrypto.js'); })).signWithApiKey(input);
    42	        case "purejs":
    43	            return (await Promise.resolve().then(function () { return require('./purejs.js'); })).signWithApiKey(input);
    44	        default:
    45	            throw new Error(`Unsupported runtime: ${runtime}`);
    46	    }
    47	};
    48	/**
    49	 * Stamper to use with `@turnkey/http`'s `TurnkeyClient`
    50	 */
    51	class ApiKeyStamper {
    52	    constructor(config) {
    53	        this.apiPublicKey = config.apiPublicKey;
    54	        this.apiPrivateKey = config.apiPrivateKey;
    55	        this.runtimeOverride = config.runtimeOverride;
    56	    }
    57	    async stamp(payload) {
    58	        const signature = await signWithApiKey({
    59	            publicKey: this.apiPublicKey,
    60	            privateKey: this.apiPrivateKey,
    61	            content: payload,
    62	        }, this.runtimeOverride);
    63	        const stamp = {
    64	            publicKey: this.apiPublicKey,
    65	            scheme: "SIGNATURE_SCHEME_TK_API_P256",
    66	            signature,
    67	        };
    68	        return {
    69	            stampHeaderName,
    70	            stampHeaderValue: encoding.stringToBase64urlString(JSON.stringify(stamp)),
    71	        };
    72	    }
    73	}
    74	
    75	exports.pointDecode = elliptic_curves.pointDecode;
    76	exports.ApiKeyStamper = ApiKeyStamper;
    77	exports.signWithApiKey = signWithApiKey;

     1	// This is a temporary shim for bs58check@4.0.0
     2	//
     3	// See: https://github.com/bitcoinjs/bs58check/issues/47
     4	//
     5	// bs58check v4.0.0 uses ESM with only a default export, which causes compatibility
     6	// issues with Metro (React Native). When importing the package using
     7	// `import bs58check from 'bs58check'`, Metro applies multiple levels of wrapping,
     8	// resulting in a structure like `{ default: { default: { encode, decode, ... } } }`.
     9	//
    10	// This shim unwraps the exports until it reaches the object that contains `.decode`,
    11	// `.encode`, and `.decodeUnsafe`, allowing consistent usage across platforms.
    12	//
    13	// We can remove this shim once bs58check publishes a version that properly re-exports
    14	// named methods from its ESM build
    15	
    16	import * as raw from "bs58check";
    17	
    18	type Bs58Check = {
    19	  encode(payload: Uint8Array | number[]): string;
    20	  decode(str: string): Uint8Array;
    21	  decodeUnsafe(str: string): Uint8Array | undefined;
    22	};
    23	
    24	function unwrap(obj: any): any {
    25	  let cur = obj;
    26	  while (
    27	    cur &&
    28	    !(cur.encode && cur.decode && cur.decodeUnsafe) &&
    29	    cur.default
    30	  ) {
    31	    cur = cur.default;
    32	  }
    33	  return cur;
    34	}
    35	
    36	export const bs58check = unwrap(raw) as Bs58Check;

     7	    ".": {

     1	// CryptoTests.cs — xunit tests for src/Crypto.cs.
     2	//
     3	// Vector sources:
     4	//   - HKDF RFC 5869 test cases A.1..A.3 (the SHA-256 cases)
     5	//   - NIST P-256 known points (G and 2G) for GetPublicKey
     6	//   - Compress/UncompressRawPublicKey roundtrip
     7	//   - HpkeEncrypt/HpkeDecrypt roundtrip (deterministic round-trip)
     8	//   - VerifySessionJwtSignature negative cases
     9	//
    10	// Tests that require a Turnkey-signed bundle (DecryptCredentialBundle,
    11	// EncryptPrivateKeyToBundle, DecryptExportBundle against PRODUCTION_SIGNER)
    12	// are not unit-testable without a real Turnkey signing key. They are
    13	// implicitly exercised by the HPKE roundtrip (the inner HPKE step is
    14	// identical) and by the E2E whoami flow once credentials are present.
    15	
    16	using System;
    17	using System.Text;
    18	using FluentAssertions;
    19	using Org.BouncyCastle.Math;
    20	using Xunit;
    21	
    22	namespace Turnkey.Tests
    23	{
    24	    public class CryptoTests
    25	    {
    26	        // ============================================================
    27	        // Math.ModSqrt — Tonelli-Shanks
    28	        // ============================================================
    29	
    30	        [Fact]
    31	        public void ModSqrt_SmallPrime_HappyPath()
    32	        {
    33	            // 4 = 2^2 mod 7, ModSqrt(4, 7) should be 2 or 5 (-2 mod 7).
    34	            var p = new BigInteger("7");
    35	            var x = new BigInteger("4");
    36	            var root = Crypto.Math.ModSqrt(x, p);
    37	            (root.Equals(new BigInteger("2")) || root.Equals(new BigInteger("5")))
    38	                .Should().BeTrue($"got {root}");
    39	        }
    40	
    41	        [Fact]
    42	        public void ModSqrt_NonResidue_Throws()
    43	        {
    44	            // 3 is a non-residue mod 7.
    45	            var p = new BigInteger("7");
    46	            var x = new BigInteger("3");
    47	            Action act = () => Crypto.Math.ModSqrt(x, p);
    48	            act.Should().Throw<InvalidOperationException>()
    49	               .WithMessage("could not find a modular square root");
    50	        }
    51	
    52	        [Fact]
    53	        public void ModSqrt_NonPositiveP_Throws()
    54	        {
    55	            var p = new BigInteger("0");
    56	            var x = new BigInteger("1");
    57	            Action act = () => Crypto.Math.ModSqrt(x, p);
    58	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>()
    59	               .WithMessage("p must be positive");
    60	        }
    61	
    62	        [Fact]
    63	        public void ModSqrt_NegativeX_Throws()
    64	        {
    65	            // Upstream JS BigInt % keeps the sign of the dividend, so a
    66	            // negative x stays negative through "base = x % p" and then
    67	            // fails the squareRoot check. Mirror that.
    68	            var p = new BigInteger("7");
    69	            var x = new BigInteger("-4");
    70	            Action act = () => Crypto.Math.ModSqrt(x, p);
    71	            act.Should().Throw<InvalidOperationException>()
    72	               .WithMessage("could not find a modular square root");
    73	        }
    74	
    75	        [Fact]
    76	        public void ModSqrt_P256Prime_Works()
    77	        {
    78	            // P-256 prime. Pick any quadratic residue: 4 = 2^2.
    79	            var p = new BigInteger(CryptoConstants.P256_P);
    80	            var x = new BigInteger("4");
    81	            var root = Crypto.Math.ModSqrt(x, p);
    82	            root.Multiply(root).Mod(p).Equals(x).Should().BeTrue();
    83	        }
    84

    88	
    89	        // RFC 5869 Test Case 1 (Basic test case with SHA-256)
    90	        [Fact]
    91	        public void Hkdf_Rfc5869_A1()
    92	        {
    93	            byte[] ikm = HexToBytes("0b0b0b0b0b0b0b0b0b0b0b0b0b0b0b0b0b0b0b0b0b0b");
    94	            byte[] salt = HexToBytes("000102030405060708090a0b0c");
    95	            byte[] info = HexToBytes("f0f1f2f3f4f5f6f7f8f9");
    96	            int L = 42;
    97	
    98	            byte[] prk = Crypto.Hkdf.Extract(salt, ikm);
    99	            byte[] okm = Crypto.Hkdf.Expand(prk, info, L);
   100	
   101	            BytesToHex(prk).Should().Be(
   102	                "077709362c2e32df0ddc3f0dc47bba6390b6c73bb50f9c3122ec844ad7c2b3e5");
   103	            BytesToHex(okm).Should().Be(
   104	                "3cb25f25faacd57a90434f64d0362f2a"
   105	                + "2d2d0a90cf1a5a4c5db02d56ecc4c5bf"
   106	                + "34007208d5b887185865");
   107	        }
   108	
   109	        // RFC 5869 Test Case 2 (Test with SHA-256 and longer inputs/outputs)
   110	        [Fact]
   111	        public void Hkdf_Rfc5869_A2()
   112	        {
   113	            byte[] ikm = HexToBytes(
   114	                "000102030405060708090a0b0c0d0e0f"
   115	                + "101112131415161718191a1b1c1d1e1f"

   131	            int L = 82;

   138	            BytesToHex(okm).Should().Be(

   143	                + "cc30c58179ec3e87c14c01d5c1f3434f"

   186	        {

   188	            byte[] prkA = Crypto.Hkdf.Extract(null!, ikm);
   189	            byte[] prkB = Crypto.Hkdf.Extract(new byte[32], ikm); // RFC default
   190	            prkA.Should().Equal(prkB);

   194	        // CompressRawPublicKey / UncompressRawPublicKey
   195	        // ============================================================
   196	
   197	        [Fact]
   198	        public void CompressUncompress_Roundtrip_RandomKeys()
   199	        {
   200	            for (int i = 0; i < 8; i++)
   201	            {
   202	                var kp = Crypto.GenerateP256KeyPair();
   203	                byte[] uncompressed = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(kp.PublicKeyUncompressed);
   204	                byte[] compressed = Crypto.CompressRawPublicKey(uncompressed);
   205	                compressed.Should().HaveCount(33);
   206	                compressed[0].Should().BeOneOf((byte)0x02, (byte)0x03);
   207	
   208	                byte[] recovered = Crypto.UncompressRawPublicKey(compressed);
   209	                recovered.Should().Equal(uncompressed);
   210	            }
   211	        }
   212	
   213	        [Fact]
   214	        public void CompressRawPublicKey_Permissive_OnAnyLength()
   215	        {
   216	            // Upstream behavior: slice + LSB-flip regardless of input shape.
   217	            // For a 65-byte uncompressed key we produce a 33-byte compressed key.
   218	            // For other lengths we produce a different-length output that
   219	            // upstream would also produce. Confirm we no longer throw on
   220	            // malformed input.
   221	            var raw = new byte[64];
   222	            raw[0] = 0x04;
   223	            raw[63] = 0x01;
   224	            Action act = () => Crypto.CompressRawPublicKey(raw);
   225	            act.Should().NotThrow();
   226	        }
   227	
   228	        [Fact]
   229	        public void UncompressRawPublicKey_BadPrefix_Throws()
   230	        {
   231	            var compressed = new byte[33];
   232	            compressed[0] = 0x05;
   233	            Action act = () => Crypto.UncompressRawPublicKey(compressed);
   234	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>()
   235	               .WithMessage("failed to uncompress raw public key: invalid prefix");
   236	        }
   237	
   238	        [Fact]
   239	        public void UncompressRawPublicKey_WrongLength_Throws()
   240	        {
   241	            var compressed = new byte[32];
   242	            compressed[0] = 0x02;
   243	            Action act = () => Crypto.UncompressRawPublicKey(compressed);
   244	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>()
   245	               .WithMessage("failed to uncompress raw public key: invalid length");
   246	        }

   252	        [Fact]
   253	        public void GenerateP256KeyPair_LengthsAreCorrect()
   254	        {
   255	            var kp = Crypto.GenerateP256KeyPair();
   256	            kp.PrivateKey.Should().HaveLength(64);          // 32 bytes hex
   257	            kp.PublicKey.Should().HaveLength(66);            // 33 bytes hex
   258	            kp.PublicKeyUncompressed.Should().HaveLength(130); // 65 bytes hex
   259	            kp.PublicKey.Should().MatchRegex("^0[23][0-9a-f]{64}$");
   260	            kp.PublicKeyUncompressed.Should().StartWith("04");
   261	        }
   262	
   263	        [Fact]
   264	        public void GetPublicKey_FromPrivateKey_ProducesCompressedByDefault()
   265	        {
   266	            var kp = Crypto.GenerateP256KeyPair();
   267	            byte[] priv = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(kp.PrivateKey);
   268	            byte[] pub = Crypto.GetPublicKey(priv); // isCompressed default true
   269	            pub.Should().HaveCount(33);
   270	            Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString(pub).Should().Be(kp.PublicKey);
   271	        }
   272	
   273	        [Fact]
   274	        public void GetPublicKey_Uncompressed_MatchesGenerator()
   275	        {
   276	            var kp = Crypto.GenerateP256KeyPair();
   277	            byte[] priv = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(kp.PrivateKey);
   278	            byte[] uncompressed = Crypto.GetPublicKey(priv, isCompressed: false);
   279	            Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString(uncompressed).Should().Be(kp.PublicKeyUncompressed);
   280	        }
   281	
   282	        [Fact]
   283	        public void GetPublicKey_HexStringOverload_MatchesByteOverload()
   284	        {
   285	            var kp = Crypto.GenerateP256KeyPair();
   286	            byte[] viaBytes = Crypto.GetPublicKey(Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(kp.PrivateKey));
   287	            byte[] viaHex = Crypto.GetPublicKey(kp.PrivateKey);
   288	            viaBytes.Should().Equal(viaHex);
   289	        }

   320	        // ============================================================
   321	        // HPKE roundtrip
   322	        // ============================================================
   323	
   324	        [Fact]
   325	        public void Hpke_EncryptThenDecrypt_RoundTripsArbitraryPayload()
   326	        {
   327	            // Receiver key pair.
   328	            var recv = Crypto.GenerateP256KeyPair();
   329	            byte[] recvPubUncompressed = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(recv.PublicKeyUncompressed);
   330	
   331	            byte[] payload = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(
   332	                "deadbeefcafebabe1234567890abcdef00112233445566778899aabbccddeeff");
   333	
   334	            byte[] encrypted = Crypto.HpkeEncrypt(new Crypto.HpkeEncryptParams
   335	            {
   336	                PlainTextBuf = payload,
   337	                TargetKeyBuf = recvPubUncompressed,
   338	            });
   339	
   340	            // encrypted = compressed(senderPub) || ciphertext (33 + N bytes)
   341	            encrypted.Length.Should().BeGreaterThan(33);
   342	
   343	            // Split, uncompress the sender's compressed point, then decrypt.
   344	            var compressedSender = new byte[33];
   345	            Array.Copy(encrypted, 0, compressedSender, 0, 33);
   346	            var ciphertext = new byte[encrypted.Length - 33];
   347	            Array.Copy(encrypted, 33, ciphertext, 0, ciphertext.Length);
   348	
   349	            byte[] encapped = Crypto.UncompressRawPublicKey(compressedSender);
   350	
   351	            byte[] decrypted = Crypto.HpkeDecrypt(new Crypto.HpkeDecryptParams
   352	            {
   353	                CiphertextBuf = ciphertext,
   354	                EncappedKeyBuf = encapped,
   355	                ReceiverPriv = recv.PrivateKey,
   356	            });
   357	
   358	            decrypted.Should().Equal(payload);
   359	        }
   360	
   361	        [Fact]
   362	        public void Hpke_EncryptThenDecrypt_EmptyPayload()
   363	        {
   364	            var recv = Crypto.GenerateP256KeyPair();
   365	            byte[] recvPubUncompressed = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(recv.PublicKeyUncompressed);
   366	
   367	            byte[] encrypted = Crypto.HpkeEncrypt(new Crypto.HpkeEncryptParams
   368	            {
   369	                PlainTextBuf = Array.Empty<byte>(),
   370	                TargetKeyBuf = recvPubUncompressed,
   371	            });
   372	
   373	            var compressedSender = new byte[33];
   374	            Array.Copy(encrypted, 0, compressedSender, 0, 33);
   375	            var ciphertext = new byte[encrypted.Length - 33];
   376	            Array.Copy(encrypted, 33, ciphertext, 0, ciphertext.Length);
   377	
   378	            byte[] decrypted = Crypto.HpkeDecrypt(new Crypto.HpkeDecryptParams
   379	            {
   380	                CiphertextBuf = ciphertext,
   381	                EncappedKeyBuf = Crypto.UncompressRawPublicKey(compressedSender),
   382	                ReceiverPriv = recv.PrivateKey,
   383	            });
   384	            decrypted.Should().BeEmpty();
   385	        }
   386	
   387	        [Fact]
   388	        public void Hpke_DecryptWithWrongKey_Throws()
   389	        {
   390	            var recv = Crypto.GenerateP256KeyPair();
   391	            var attacker = Crypto.GenerateP256KeyPair();
   392	            byte[] recvPubUncompressed = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(recv.PublicKeyUncompressed);
   393	
   394	            byte[] encrypted = Crypto.HpkeEncrypt(new Crypto.HpkeEncryptParams
   395	            {
   396	                PlainTextBuf = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString("aabbcc"),
   397	                TargetKeyBuf = recvPubUncompressed,
   398	            });
   399	
   400	            var compressedSender = new byte[33];
   401	            Array.Copy(encrypted, 0, compressedSender, 0, 33);
   402	            var ciphertext = new byte[encrypted.Length - 33];
   403	            Array.Copy(encrypted, 33, ciphertext, 0, ciphertext.Length);
   404	
   405	            Action act = () => Crypto.HpkeDecrypt(new Crypto.HpkeDecryptParams
   406	            {
   407	                CiphertextBuf = ciphertext,
   408	                EncappedKeyBuf = Crypto.UncompressRawPublicKey(compressedSender),
   409	                ReceiverPriv = attacker.PrivateKey,
   410	            });
   411	            act.Should().Throw<Exception>();
   412	        }

   426	
   427	        [Fact]
   428	        public void FormatHpkeBuf_ReturnsExpectedJson()
   429	        {
   430	            // Use a real HpkeEncrypt output so the bytes are valid.
   431	            var recv = Crypto.GenerateP256KeyPair();
   432	            byte[] recvPubUncompressed = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(recv.PublicKeyUncompressed);
   433	
   434	            byte[] encrypted = Crypto.HpkeEncrypt(new Crypto.HpkeEncryptParams
   435	            {
   436	                PlainTextBuf = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString("1234"),
   437	                TargetKeyBuf = recvPubUncompressed,
   438	            });
   439	
   440	            string json = Crypto.FormatHpkeBuf(encrypted);
   441	
   442	            // Shape contains exactly two keys in upstream order.
   443	            json.Should().StartWith("{\"encappedPublic\":\"04");
   444	            json.Should().Contain("\"ciphertext\":\"");
   445	            json.Should().EndWith("\"}");
   446	        }
   447	
   448	        [Fact]
   449	        public void FormatHpkeBuf_TooSmall_Throws()
   450	        {
   451	            // Upstream passes the slice to uncompressRawPublicKey which
   452	            // throws "failed to uncompress raw public key: invalid length"
   453	            // when the buffer is shorter than 33 bytes.
   454	            Action act = () => Crypto.FormatHpkeBuf(new byte[10]);
   455	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>()
   456	               .WithMessage("failed to uncompress raw public key: invalid length");
   457	        }
   458	
   459	        // ============================================================
   460	        // VerifySessionJwtSignature negative paths
   461	        // ============================================================
   462	
   463	        [Fact]
   464	        public void VerifySessionJwtSignature_Empty_Throws()
   465	        {
   466	            // Upstream: throws "invalid JWT: need 3 parts" when signature part is missing.
   467	            Action act = () => Crypto.VerifySessionJwtSignature(string.Empty);
   468	            act.Should().Throw<InvalidOperationException>()
   469	               .WithMessage("invalid JWT: need 3 parts");
   470	        }
   471	
   472	        [Fact]
   473	        public void VerifySessionJwtSignature_WrongPartCount_Throws()
   474	        {
   475	            Action act = () => Crypto.VerifySessionJwtSignature("just.two");
   476	            act.Should().Throw<InvalidOperationException>()
   477	               .WithMessage("invalid JWT: need 3 parts");
   478	        }
   479	
   480	        [Fact]
   481	        public void VerifySessionJwtSignature_BadSignatureLength_ReturnsFalse()
   482	        {
   483	            // 3 parts but the signature decodes to a non-64-byte buffer.
   484	            string jwt = "aGVhZGVy.cGF5bG9hZA.YWJj"; // last part decodes to "abc" (3 bytes)
   485	            Crypto.VerifySessionJwtSignature(jwt).Should().BeFalse();
   486	        }
   487	
   488	        [Fact]
   489	        public void VerifySessionJwtSignature_WellFormedButForgedSig_ReturnsFalse()
   490	        {
   491	            // 64-byte signature of all zeros — should fail verification.
   492	            string header = Encoding.Base64StringToBase64UrlEncodedString(
   493	                Convert.ToBase64String(System.Text.Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes("{\"alg\":\"ES256\"}")));
   494	            string payload = Encoding.Base64StringToBase64UrlEncodedString(
   495	                Convert.ToBase64String(System.Text.Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes("{\"sub\":\"x\"}")));
   496	            string sig = Encoding.Base64StringToBase64UrlEncodedString(
   497	                Convert.ToBase64String(new byte[64]));
   498	            string jwt = header + "." + payload + "." + sig;
   499	            Crypto.VerifySessionJwtSignature(jwt).Should().BeFalse();
   500	        }
   501	
   502	        // ============================================================
   503	        // Curve.Secp256k1 — UncompressRawPublicKey
   504	        // ============================================================
   505	
   506	        [Fact]
   507	        public void UncompressRawPublicKey_Secp256k1_Roundtrip()
   508	        {
   509	            // secp256k1 generator point compressed = 02 79be667e f9dcbbac 55a06295 ce870b07
   510	            //                                       029bfcdb 2dce28d9 59f2815b 16f81798
   511	            byte[] compressed = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(
   512	                "0279be667ef9dcbbac55a06295ce870b07029bfcdb2dce28d959f2815b16f81798");
   513	            byte[] uncompressed = Crypto.UncompressRawPublicKey(compressed, Crypto.Curve.Secp256k1);
   514	            uncompressed.Should().HaveCount(65);
   515	            uncompressed[0].Should().Be(0x04);
   516	            // Y coordinate of G must be even (prefix was 0x02).
   517	            (uncompressed[64] & 1).Should().Be(0);
   518	        }
   519	
   520	        // ============================================================
   521	        // Bundle helpers — including a real Turnkey-pinned vector
   522	        // ============================================================
   523	
   524	        [Fact]
   525	        public void DecryptCredentialBundle_UpstreamVector()
   526	        {
   527	            // From upstream tests/__tests__/crypto-test.ts:179-184
   528	            // (codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-crypto-2.8.8/ts-source/__tests__/crypto-test.ts)
   529	            const string credentialBundle =
   530	                "w99a5xV6A75TfoAUkZn869fVyDYvgVsKrawMALZXmrauZd8hEv66EkPU1Z42CUaHESQjcA5bqd8dynTGBMLWB9ewtXWPEVbZvocB4Tw2K1vQVp7uwjf";
   531	            const string embeddedKey =
   532	                "20fa65df11f24833790ae283fc9a0c215eecbbc589549767977994dc69d05a56";
   533	            const string expectedSenderPrivateKey =
   534	                "67ee05fc3bdf4161bc70701c221d8d77180294cefcfcea64ba83c4d4c732fcb9";
   535	
   536	            string decrypted = Crypto.DecryptCredentialBundle(credentialBundle, embeddedKey);
   537	            decrypted.Should().Be(expectedSenderPrivateKey);
   538	        }
   539	
   540	        [Fact]
   541	        public void UncompressRawPublicKey_UpstreamInvalidPrefixVector()
