   544	            byte[] invalidPrefix = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(
   545	                "77c6047f9441ed7d6d3045406e95c07cd85c778e4b8cef3ca7abac09b95c709ee5");
   546	            Action act = () => Crypto.UncompressRawPublicKey(invalidPrefix);
   547	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>()
   548	               .WithMessage("failed to uncompress raw public key: invalid prefix");
   549	        }
   550	
   551	        [Fact]
   552	        public void CompressRawPublicKey_EmptyInput_ReturnsEmpty()
   553	        {
   554	            // Upstream behavior: empty Uint8Array slice produces empty result.
   555	            Crypto.CompressRawPublicKey(Array.Empty<byte>()).Should().BeEmpty();
   556	        }
   557	
   558	        [Fact]
   559	        public void HpkeEncrypt_NullPlainTextBuf_Throws()
   560	        {
   561	            // Upstream throws when plainTextBuf is absent (wrapped via try/catch).
   562	            var recv = Crypto.GenerateP256KeyPair();
   563	            byte[] recvPubUncompressed = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(recv.PublicKeyUncompressed);
   564	            Action act = () => Crypto.HpkeEncrypt(new Crypto.HpkeEncryptParams
   565	            {
   566	                PlainTextBuf = null,
   567	                TargetKeyBuf = recvPubUncompressed,
   568	            });
   569	            act.Should().Throw<InvalidOperationException>()
   570	               .WithMessage("Unable to perform hpkeEncrypt:*");
   571	        }
   572	
   573	        [Fact]
   574	        public void DecryptCredentialBundle_BundleTooSmall_Throws()
   575	        {
   576	            // Base58Check of a small (<33 byte) payload should still decode (with valid checksum)
   577	            // but trigger the size guard. Use Base58Check encode so DecryptCredentialBundle's
   578	            // bs58check decode succeeds, then it should fail on the size check.
   579	            string tiny = Encoding.Base58CheckEncode(new byte[] { 0x01, 0x02, 0x03 });
   580	            Action act = () => Crypto.DecryptCredentialBundle(tiny, new string('1', 64));
   581	            act.Should().Throw<InvalidOperationException>()
   582	               .WithMessage("*Error decrypting bundle*");
   583	        }
   584	
   585	        [Fact]
   586	        public void DecryptCredentialBundle_RawBase58_Rejected()
   587	        {
   588	            // Upstream uses bs58check.decode exclusively. A plain base58 input
   589	            // (no checksum) must NOT be accepted.
   590	            string rawBs58 = Encoding.Base58Encode(new byte[40]);
   591	            Action act = () => Crypto.DecryptCredentialBundle(rawBs58, new string('1', 64));
   592	            act.Should().Throw<InvalidOperationException>();
   593	        }
   594	
   595	        [Fact]
   596	        public void EncryptPrivateKeyToBundle_MissingArgs_Throws()
   597	        {
   598	            Action act = () => Crypto.EncryptPrivateKeyToBundle(new Crypto.EncryptPrivateKeyToBundleParams());
   599	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>();
   600	        }
   601	
   602	        [Fact]
   603	        public void DecryptExportBundle_MissingArgs_Throws()
   604	        {
   605	            Action act = () => Crypto.DecryptExportBundle(new Crypto.DecryptExportBundleParams());
   606	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>();
   607	        }
   608	
   609	        // ============================================================
   610	        // Helpers
   611	        // ============================================================
   612	
   613	        private static byte[] HexToBytes(string hex)
   614	        {
   615	            return Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(hex);
   616	        }
   617	
   618	        private static string BytesToHex(byte[] bytes)
   619	        {
   620	            return Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString(bytes);
   621	        }

/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba tests/ApiKeyStamperTests.cs | sed -n '1,260p'; nl -ba tests/HttpTests.cs | sed -n '1,260p'; nl -ba tests/EncodingTests.cs | sed -n '1,360p'" in /Users/takeshi/Kyuzan/src/turnkey-sdk-csharp/.claude/worktrees/laughing-hertz-048cd4
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	// ApiKeyStamperTests.cs — xunit tests for src/ApiKeyStamper.cs.
     2	//
     3	// Vector sources:
     4	//   codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-api-key-stamper-0.5.0/ts-source/__fixtures__/api-key.{private,public}
     5	//   codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-api-key-stamper-0.5.0/ts-source/__tests__/stamp-test.ts
     6	//
     7	// P-256 ECDSA signatures are not deterministic across libraries (noble uses
     8	// RFC 6979; BouncyCastle's HMacDsaKCalculator also uses RFC 6979 with the
     9	// same digest, so for identical input + key + nonce-source the signature
    10	// is deterministic). Tests therefore assert:
    11	//   - the header name == "X-Stamp"
    12	//   - the base64url-decoded JSON has keys ["publicKey", "scheme", "signature"]
    13	//   - publicKey matches the configured key
    14	//   - scheme == "SIGNATURE_SCHEME_TK_API_P256"
    15	//   - the signature is a valid DER-encoded ECDSA signature over SHA-256(content)
    16	//     under the configured public key
    17	
    18	using System;
    19	using System.IO;
    20	using System.Text;
    21	using System.Text.Json;
    22	using FluentAssertions;
    23	using Org.BouncyCastle.Asn1;
    24	using Org.BouncyCastle.Asn1.X9;
    25	using Org.BouncyCastle.Crypto.Parameters;
    26	using Org.BouncyCastle.Math;
    27	using Org.BouncyCastle.Security;
    28	using Xunit;
    29	
    30	namespace Turnkey.Tests
    31	{
    32	    public class ApiKeyStamperTests
    33	    {
    34	        // From upstream __fixtures__/api-key.{private,public}
    35	        private const string FixturePrivateKey =
    36	            "487f361ddfd73440e707f4daa6775b376859e8a3c9f29b3bb694a12927c0213c";
    37	        private const string FixturePublicKey =
    38	            "02f739f8c77b32f4d5f13265861febd76e7a9c61a1140d296b8c16302508870316";
    39	
    40	        [Fact]
    41	        public void Constructor_DefersValidation()
    42	        {
    43	            // Upstream `new ApiKeyStamper({apiPublicKey, apiPrivateKey})` only
    44	            // assigns fields; validation happens at sign time. C# mirrors
    45	            // that, including null tolerance.
    46	            Action act = () => new ApiKeyStamper(FixturePublicKey, "abcd");
    47	            act.Should().NotThrow();
    48	            Action act2 = () => new ApiKeyStamper(null!, null!);
    49	            act2.Should().NotThrow();
    50	        }
    51	
    52	        [Fact]
    53	        public void SignWithApiKey_RejectsBadKeyLength()
    54	        {
    55	            // Validation now occurs in SignWithApiKey -> Crypto.GetPublicKey.
    56	            var stamper = new ApiKeyStamper(FixturePublicKey, "abcd");
    57	            Action act = () => stamper.SignWithApiKey("payload");
    58	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>()
    59	               .WithMessage("invalid P-256 private key: expected 32 bytes, got 2");
    60	        }
    61	
    62	        [Fact]
    63	        public void SignWithApiKey_RejectsZeroScalar()
    64	        {
    65	            string zero = new string('0', 64);
    66	            var stamper = new ApiKeyStamper(FixturePublicKey, zero);
    67	            Action act = () => stamper.SignWithApiKey("payload");
    68	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>()
    69	               .WithMessage("invalid P-256 private key: scalar must be in [1, n - 1]");
    70	        }
    71	
    72	        [Fact]
    73	        public void Stamp_UpstreamFixture_ProducesValidWireBytes()
    74	        {
    75	            // Matches upstream __tests__/stamp-test.ts:6-37
    76	            var stamper = new ApiKeyStamper(FixturePublicKey, FixturePrivateKey);
    77	            const string messageToSign = "hello from TKHQ!";
    78	
    79	            var result = stamper.Stamp(messageToSign);
    80	
    81	            result.StampHeaderName.Should().Be("X-Stamp");
    82	
    83	            // Decode base64url -> JSON -> object.
    84	            string decodedJson = Encoding.DecodeBase64UrlToString(result.StampHeaderValue);
    85	
    86	            using var doc = JsonDocument.Parse(decodedJson);
    87	            var root = doc.RootElement;
    88	
    89	            // Keys must be exactly publicKey, scheme, signature in this order.
    90	            int i = 0;
    91	            string[] expectedKeys = { "publicKey", "scheme", "signature" };
    92	            foreach (var prop in root.EnumerateObject())
    93	            {
    94	                prop.Name.Should().Be(expectedKeys[i++]);
    95	            }
    96	            i.Should().Be(3);
    97	
    98	            root.GetProperty("publicKey").GetString().Should().Be(FixturePublicKey);
    99	            root.GetProperty("scheme").GetString().Should().Be("SIGNATURE_SCHEME_TK_API_P256");
   100	
   101	            // Verify the DER ECDSA signature against SHA-256(content) under the
   102	            // public key. This is the wire-format gate: if the signature isn't
   103	            // verifiable against the configured P-256 key, the stamp would be
   104	            // rejected by Turnkey's backend.
   105	            string signatureHex = root.GetProperty("signature").GetString()!;
   106	            byte[] signatureBytes = HexToBytes(signatureHex);
   107	            AssertSignatureVerifies(FixturePublicKey, messageToSign, signatureBytes);
   108	        }
   109	
   110	        [Fact]
   111	        public void SignWithApiKey_ProducesDerHexThatVerifies()
   112	        {
   113	            var stamper = new ApiKeyStamper(FixturePublicKey, FixturePrivateKey);
   114	            const string content = "any payload we care to sign";
   115	            string sigHex = stamper.SignWithApiKey(content);
   116	
   117	            // Output is DER hex; even length, starts with 30 (SEQUENCE tag).
   118	            (sigHex.Length % 2).Should().Be(0);
   119	            sigHex.Substring(0, 2).Should().Be("30");
   120	
   121	            AssertSignatureVerifies(FixturePublicKey, content, HexToBytes(sigHex));
   122	        }
   123	
   124	        [Fact]
   125	        public void SignWithApiKey_DeterministicWithRfc6979()
   126	        {
   127	            // RFC 6979 + same key + same content + same SHA-256(content) +
   128	            // same low-S normalization => signature is bit-identical across
   129	            // invocations (HMacDsaKCalculator is deterministic).
   130	            var stamper = new ApiKeyStamper(FixturePublicKey, FixturePrivateKey);
   131	            string a = stamper.SignWithApiKey("the same content");
   132	            string b = stamper.SignWithApiKey("the same content");
   133	            a.Should().Be(b);
   134	        }
   135	
   136	        [Fact]
   137	        public void SignWithApiKey_LowSEnforced()
   138	        {
   139	            // For RFC 6979 + low-S: the s value's high bit (top byte) must be
   140	            // strictly less than (n / 2 + 1). Verify by parsing the DER and
   141	            // checking the s integer is in the lower half of [1, n-1].
   142	            var stamper = new ApiKeyStamper(FixturePublicKey, FixturePrivateKey);
   143	            for (int i = 0; i < 8; i++)
   144	            {
   145	                string sigHex = stamper.SignWithApiKey("content_" + i);
   146	                var (r, s) = ParseDerEcdsa(HexToBytes(sigHex));
   147	
   148	                var curve = ECNamedCurveTable.GetByName(CryptoConstants.CURVE_NAME);
   149	                var halfN = curve.N.ShiftRight(1);
   150	                s.CompareTo(halfN).Should().BeLessOrEqualTo(0,
   151	                    "low-S requires s to be in (0, n/2]");
   152	                r.SignValue.Should().BeGreaterThan(0);
   153	                s.SignValue.Should().BeGreaterThan(0);
   154	            }
   155	        }
   156	
   157	        [Fact]
   158	        public void SignWithApiKey_WrongPublicKey_Throws()
   159	        {
   160	            // Mismatched public key (any other valid P-256 compressed key).
   161	            var other = Crypto.GenerateP256KeyPair();
   162	            Action act = () =>
   163	            {
   164	                var stamper = new ApiKeyStamper(other.PublicKey, FixturePrivateKey);
   165	                stamper.SignWithApiKey("payload");
   166	            };
   167	            act.Should().Throw<InvalidOperationException>()
   168	               .WithMessage("Bad API key. Expected to get public key*");
   169	        }
   170	
   171	        [Fact]
   172	        public void Stamp_HeaderConstantsAndScheme()
   173	        {
   174	            ApiKeyStamper.StampHeaderName.Should().Be("X-Stamp");
   175	            ApiKeyStamper.SignatureScheme.Should().Be("SIGNATURE_SCHEME_TK_API_P256");
   176	        }
   177	
   178	        [Fact]
   179	        public void StampHeaderValue_IsAsciiUrlSafe()
   180	        {
   181	            var stamper = new ApiKeyStamper(FixturePublicKey, FixturePrivateKey);
   182	            var result = stamper.Stamp("hello");
   183	            // base64url alphabet: A-Z a-z 0-9 - _
   184	            foreach (char c in result.StampHeaderValue)
   185	            {
   186	                bool ok = (c >= 'A' && c <= 'Z')
   187	                          || (c >= 'a' && c <= 'z')
   188	                          || (c >= '0' && c <= '9')
   189	                          || c == '-' || c == '_';
   190	                ok.Should().BeTrue($"char '{c}' is not in base64url alphabet");
   191	            }
   192	        }
   193	
   194	        // ============================================================
   195	        // Helpers
   196	        // ============================================================
   197	
   198	        private static byte[] HexToBytes(string hex) => Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(hex);
   199	
   200	        private static void AssertSignatureVerifies(string compressedPubHex, string content, byte[] derSignature)
   201	        {
   202	            byte[] payloadBytes = System.Text.Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(content);
   203	
   204	            var digest = DigestUtilities.GetDigest("SHA-256");
   205	            digest.BlockUpdate(payloadBytes, 0, payloadBytes.Length);
   206	            var hash = new byte[digest.GetDigestSize()];
   207	            digest.DoFinal(hash, 0);
   208	
   209	            var curve = ECNamedCurveTable.GetByName(CryptoConstants.CURVE_NAME);
   210	            var domainParams = new ECDomainParameters(curve.Curve, curve.G, curve.N, curve.H, curve.GetSeed());
   211	
   212	            byte[] compressedPub = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(compressedPubHex);
   213	            var point = curve.Curve.DecodePoint(compressedPub);
   214	            var publicKey = new ECPublicKeyParameters(point, domainParams);
   215	
   216	            var signer = SignerUtilities.GetSigner("NONEwithECDSA");
   217	            signer.Init(false, publicKey);
   218	            signer.BlockUpdate(hash, 0, hash.Length);
   219	            signer.VerifySignature(derSignature).Should().BeTrue();
   220	        }
   221	
   222	        private static (BigInteger R, BigInteger S) ParseDerEcdsa(byte[] der)
   223	        {
   224	            using var ms = new MemoryStream(der);
   225	            using var reader = new Asn1InputStream(ms);
   226	            var seq = (DerSequence)reader.ReadObject();
   227	            var r = ((DerInteger)seq[0]).Value;
   228	            var s = ((DerInteger)seq[1]).Value;
   229	            return (r, s);
   230	        }
   231	    }
   232	}
     1	// HttpTests.cs — xunit tests for src/Http.cs.
     2	
     3	using System;
     4	using System.Text.Json;
     5	using FluentAssertions;
     6	using Xunit;
     7	
     8	namespace Turnkey.Tests
     9	{
    10	    public class HttpTests
    11	    {
    12	        // Upstream api-key-stamper@0.5.0 fixture, reused to drive Http here so
    13	        // that the stamped bodies verify under a known public key.
    14	        private const string FixturePrivateKey =
    15	            "487f361ddfd73440e707f4daa6775b376859e8a3c9f29b3bb694a12927c0213c";
    16	        private const string FixturePublicKey =
    17	            "02f739f8c77b32f4d5f13265861febd76e7a9c61a1140d296b8c16302508870316";
    18	
    19	        private static Http MakeClient() => Http.FromTargetPrivateKey(FixturePrivateKey);
    20	
    21	        [Fact]
    22	        public void FromTargetPrivateKey_RejectsEmpty()
    23	        {
    24	            Action act = () => Http.FromTargetPrivateKey("");
    25	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>();
    26	        }
    27	
    28	        [Fact]
    29	        public void FromTargetPrivateKey_RejectsInvalidHex()
    30	        {
    31	            Action act = () => Http.FromTargetPrivateKey("zz");
    32	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>()
    33	               .WithMessage("cannot create uint8array from invalid hex string*");
    34	        }
    35	
    36	        [Fact]
    37	        public void GetHttpClient_RejectsEmptyArgs()
    38	        {
    39	            Action a1 = () => Http.GetHttpClient("", "abc");
    40	            a1.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>();
    41	            Action a2 = () => Http.GetHttpClient("abc", "");
    42	            a2.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>();
    43	        }
    44	
    45	        [Fact]
    46	        public void StampGetWhoami_ProducesCorrectUrlAndBody()
    47	        {
    48	            var http = MakeClient();
    49	            var req = http.StampGetWhoami("00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000");
    50	
    51	            req.Url.Should().Be("https://api.turnkey.com/public/v1/query/whoami");
    52	            req.Body.Should().Be("{\"organizationId\":\"00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000\"}");
    53	            req.Stamp.StampHeaderName.Should().Be("X-Stamp");
    54	            req.Stamp.StampHeaderValue.Should().NotBeNullOrEmpty();
    55	        }
    56	
    57	        [Fact]
    58	        public void StampGetWhoami_EmptyOrg_Throws()
    59	        {
    60	            var http = MakeClient();
    61	            Action act = () => http.StampGetWhoami("");
    62	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>();
    63	        }
    64	
    65	        [Fact]
    66	        public void StampInitImportPrivateKey_ProducesCorrectUrlAndJson()
    67	        {
    68	            var http = MakeClient();
    69	            var body = new Http.InitImportPrivateKeyRequestBody
    70	            {
    71	                OrganizationId = "org-1",
    72	                Type = "ACTIVITY_TYPE_INIT_IMPORT_PRIVATE_KEY",
    73	                TimestampMs = "1729000000000",
    74	                Parameters = new Http.InitImportPrivateKeyParameters
    75	                {
    76	                    UserId = "user-1",
    77	                },
    78	            };
    79	
    80	            var req = http.StampInitImportPrivateKey(body);
    81	
    82	            req.Url.Should().Be("https://api.turnkey.com/public/v1/submit/init_import_private_key");
    83	
    84	            // Field order must be organizationId, type, timestampMs, parameters.
    85	            using var doc = JsonDocument.Parse(req.Body);
    86	            var keys = new System.Collections.Generic.List<string>();
    87	            foreach (var p in doc.RootElement.EnumerateObject())
    88	            {
    89	                keys.Add(p.Name);
    90	            }
    91	            keys.Should().ContainInOrder(new[] { "organizationId", "type", "timestampMs", "parameters" });
    92	
    93	            doc.RootElement.GetProperty("organizationId").GetString().Should().Be("org-1");
    94	            doc.RootElement.GetProperty("type").GetString().Should().Be("ACTIVITY_TYPE_INIT_IMPORT_PRIVATE_KEY");
    95	            doc.RootElement.GetProperty("timestampMs").GetString().Should().Be("1729000000000");
    96	            doc.RootElement.GetProperty("parameters").GetProperty("userId").GetString().Should().Be("user-1");
    97	        }
    98	
    99	        [Fact]
   100	        public void StampImportPrivateKey_ProducesArrayInBody()
   101	        {
   102	            var http = MakeClient();
   103	            var body = new Http.ImportPrivateKeyRequestBody
   104	            {
   105	                OrganizationId = "org-x",
   106	                Type = "ACTIVITY_TYPE_IMPORT_PRIVATE_KEY",
   107	                TimestampMs = "1729000000123",
   108	                Parameters = new Http.ImportPrivateKeyParameters
   109	                {
   110	                    UserId = "user-x",
   111	                    AddressFormats = new[] { "ADDRESS_FORMAT_ETHEREUM", "ADDRESS_FORMAT_SOLANA" },
   112	                    Curve = "CURVE_SECP256K1",
   113	                    EncryptedBundle = "{\"encappedPublic\":\"04...\",\"ciphertext\":\"ab\"}",
   114	                    PrivateKeyName = "my-key",
   115	                },
   116	            };
   117	
   118	            var req = http.StampImportPrivateKey(body);
   119	            req.Url.Should().Be("https://api.turnkey.com/public/v1/submit/import_private_key");
   120	
   121	            using var doc = JsonDocument.Parse(req.Body);
   122	            var parameters = doc.RootElement.GetProperty("parameters");
   123	            var formats = parameters.GetProperty("addressFormats");
   124	            formats.ValueKind.Should().Be(JsonValueKind.Array);
   125	            formats.GetArrayLength().Should().Be(2);
   126	            formats[0].GetString().Should().Be("ADDRESS_FORMAT_ETHEREUM");
   127	            formats[1].GetString().Should().Be("ADDRESS_FORMAT_SOLANA");
   128	            parameters.GetProperty("curve").GetString().Should().Be("CURVE_SECP256K1");
   129	        }
   130

   135	            var body = new Http.ExportPrivateKeyRequestBody
   136	            {

   149

   151	            var p = doc.RootElement.GetProperty("parameters");
   152	            p.GetProperty("privateKeyId").GetString().Should().Be("pk-1");
   153	            p.GetProperty("targetPublicKey").GetString().Should().Be(FixturePublicKey);
   154	        }

   156	        [Fact]
   157	        public void StampExportWalletAccount_ProducesCorrectShape()
   158	        {
   159	            var http = MakeClient();
   160	            var body = new Http.ExportWalletAccountRequestBody
   161	            {
   162	                OrganizationId = "org-z",
   163	                Type = "ACTIVITY_TYPE_EXPORT_WALLET_ACCOUNT",
   164	                TimestampMs = "2",
   165	                Parameters = new Http.ExportWalletAccountParameters
   166	                {
   167	                    Address = "0xabcdef",
   168	                    TargetPublicKey = FixturePublicKey,
   169	                },
   170	            };
   171	
   172	            var req = http.StampExportWalletAccount(body);
   173	            req.Url.Should().Be("https://api.turnkey.com/public/v1/submit/export_wallet_account");
   174	
   175	            using var doc = JsonDocument.Parse(req.Body);
   176	            var p = doc.RootElement.GetProperty("parameters");
   177	            p.GetProperty("address").GetString().Should().Be("0xabcdef");
   178	            p.GetProperty("targetPublicKey").GetString().Should().Be(FixturePublicKey);
   179	        }
   180	
   181	        [Fact]
   182	        public void Stamp_HeaderValueDecodesAndVerifies()
   183	        {
   184	            // End-to-end wire-format check: stamp a whoami request, decode the
   185	            // X-Stamp header, parse the JSON, and crypto-verify the DER
   186	            // signature over SHA-256(body) under the API public key.
   187	            var http = MakeClient();
   188	            var req = http.StampGetWhoami("org-id");
   189	
   190	            string decodedJson = Encoding.DecodeBase64UrlToString(req.Stamp.StampHeaderValue);
   191	            using var doc = JsonDocument.Parse(decodedJson);
   192	            var root = doc.RootElement;
   193	            root.GetProperty("publicKey").GetString().Should().Be(FixturePublicKey);
   194	            root.GetProperty("scheme").GetString().Should().Be("SIGNATURE_SCHEME_TK_API_P256");
   195	            string signatureHex = root.GetProperty("signature").GetString()!;
   196	            signatureHex.Should().StartWith("30"); // DER SEQUENCE
   197	
   198	            // Verify the signature against SHA-256(body) under the API public key.
   199	            byte[] bodyBytes = System.Text.Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(req.Body);
   200	            using var sha = System.Security.Cryptography.SHA256.Create();
   201	            byte[] digest = sha.ComputeHash(bodyBytes);
   202	
   203	            var curve = Org.BouncyCastle.Asn1.X9.ECNamedCurveTable.GetByName(CryptoConstants.CURVE_NAME);
   204	            var domain = new Org.BouncyCastle.Crypto.Parameters.ECDomainParameters(
   205	                curve.Curve, curve.G, curve.N, curve.H, curve.GetSeed());
   206	            byte[] pubBytes = Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(FixturePublicKey);
   207	            var publicKey = new Org.BouncyCastle.Crypto.Parameters.ECPublicKeyParameters(
   208	                curve.Curve.DecodePoint(pubBytes), domain);
   209	
   210	            var signer = Org.BouncyCastle.Security.SignerUtilities.GetSigner("NONEwithECDSA");
   211	            signer.Init(false, publicKey);
   212	            signer.BlockUpdate(digest, 0, digest.Length);
   213	            signer.VerifySignature(Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(signatureHex)).Should().BeTrue();
   214	        }
   215	
   216	        [Fact]
   217	        public void StampNullBody_Throws()
   218	        {
   219	            var http = MakeClient();
   220	            Action a1 = () => http.StampInitImportPrivateKey(null!);
   221	            a1.Should().Throw<ArgumentNullException>();
   222	            Action a2 = () => http.StampImportPrivateKey(null!);
   223	            a2.Should().Throw<ArgumentNullException>();
   224	            Action a3 = () => http.StampExportPrivateKey(null!);
   225	            a3.Should().Throw<ArgumentNullException>();
   226	            Action a4 = () => http.StampExportWalletAccount(null!);
   227	            a4.Should().Throw<ArgumentNullException>();
   228	        }
   229	    }
   230	}
     1	// EncodingTests.cs — xunit tests for src/Encoding.cs
     2	//
     3	// Vectors are derived from the upstream test file at:
     4	//   codex-crypto-reviews/upstream-snapshots/turnkey-encoding-0.6.0/ts-source/__tests__/index-test.ts
     5	//
     6	// Plus additional edge cases for leading-zero handling, base58check
     7	// roundtrip, and PointEncode round-trip.
     8	
     9	using System;
    10	using FluentAssertions;
    11	using Xunit;
    12	
    13	namespace Turnkey.Tests
    14	{
    15	    public class EncodingTests
    16	    {
    17	        // ========================================================
    18	        // hex
    19	        // ========================================================
    20	
    21	        [Fact]
    22	        public void Uint8ArrayToHexString_UpstreamVector()
    23	        {
    24	            // From index-test.ts test("uint8ArrayToHexString")
    25	            byte[] input =
    26	            {
    27	                82, 52, 208, 143, 250, 44, 129, 95, 48, 151, 184, 186, 132, 138, 40, 23,
    28	                46, 133, 190, 199, 136, 134, 232, 226, 1, 175, 204, 177, 102, 252, 84, 193,
    29	            };
    30	            const string expected =
    31	                "5234d08ffa2c815f3097b8ba848a28172e85bec78886e8e201afccb166fc54c1";
    32	
    33	            Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString(input).Should().Be(expected);
    34	        }
    35	
    36	        [Fact]
    37	        public void Uint8ArrayToHexString_EmptyArray_ReturnsEmpty()
    38	        {
    39	            Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString(Array.Empty<byte>()).Should().Be(string.Empty);
    40	        }
    41	
    42	        [Fact]
    43	        public void Uint8ArrayToHexString_Null_Throws()
    44	        {
    45	            Action act = () => Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString(null!);
    46	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentNullException>();
    47	        }
    48	
    49	        [Fact]
    50	        public void Uint8ArrayToHexString_LeadingZeros_Preserved()
    51	        {
    52	            byte[] input = { 0x00, 0x00, 0x01, 0x02 };
    53	            Encoding.Uint8ArrayToHexString(input).Should().Be("00000102");
    54	        }
    55	
    56	        [Fact]
    57	        public void Uint8ArrayFromHexString_UpstreamVector()
    58	        {
    59	            // From index-test.ts test("uint8ArrayFromHexString")
    60	            const string hex =
    61	                "5234d08dfa2c815f3097b8ba848a28172e85bec78886e8e201afccb166fc54c1";
    62	            byte[] expected =
    63	            {
    64	                82, 52, 208, 141, 250, 44, 129, 95, 48, 151, 184, 186, 132, 138, 40, 23,
    65	                46, 133, 190, 199, 136, 134, 232, 226, 1, 175, 204, 177, 102, 252, 84, 193,
    66	            };
    67	            Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(hex).Should().Equal(expected);
    68	        }
    69	
    70	        [Fact]
    71	        public void Uint8ArrayFromHexString_ShortAscii()
    72	        {
    73	            // From index-test.ts: "627566666572" -> [98,117,102,102,101,114] (ASCII "buffer")
    74	            byte[] expected = { 98, 117, 102, 102, 101, 114 };
    75	            Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString("627566666572").Should().Equal(expected);
    76	        }
    77	
    78	        [Theory]
    79	        [InlineData("")]    // empty
    80	        [InlineData("123")] // odd length
    81	        [InlineData("oops")] // bad chars
    82	        public void Uint8ArrayFromHexString_Invalid_Throws(string hex)
    83	        {
    84	            Action act = () => Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(hex);
    85	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>()
    86	               .WithMessage("cannot create uint8array from invalid hex string*");
    87	        }
    88	
    89	        [Fact]
    90	        public void Uint8ArrayFromHexString_WithLength_Pads()
    91	        {
    92	            // "01" with length 2 -> [0, 1]
    93	            Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString("01", 2).Should().Equal(new byte[] { 0, 1 });
    94	        }
    95	
    96	        [Fact]
    97	        public void Uint8ArrayFromHexString_WithoutLength_NoPadding()
    98	        {
    99	            Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString("01").Should().Equal(new byte[] { 1 });
   100	        }
   101	
   102	        [Fact]
   103	        public void Uint8ArrayFromHexString_TooShortGetsPadded()
   104	        {
   105	            // From upstream "TOO SHORT" case
   106	            const string hex =
   107	                "5234d08dfa2c815f3097b8ba848a28172e85bec78886e8e201afccb166fc";
   108	            byte[] expected =
   109	            {
   110	                0, 0, 82, 52, 208, 141, 250, 44, 129, 95, 48, 151, 184, 186, 132, 138,
   111	                40, 23, 46, 133, 190, 199, 136, 134, 232, 226, 1, 175, 204, 177, 102, 252,
   112	            };
   113	            Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(hex, 32).Should().Equal(expected);
   114	        }
   115	
   116	        [Fact]
   117	        public void Uint8ArrayFromHexString_TooLong_Throws()
   118	        {
   119	            // From upstream "TOO LONG" case: 34 bytes into length=32 buffer
   120	            const string hex =
   121	                "5234d08dfa2c815f3097b8ba848a28172e85bec78886e8e201afccb166fcfafbfcfd";
   122	            Action act = () => Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString(hex, 32);
   123	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>()
   124	               .WithMessage("hex value cannot fit in a buffer of 32 byte(s)");
   125	        }
   126	
   127	        [Fact]
   128	        public void Uint8ArrayFromHexString_OneByte_FitTwoByteRequest_Padding()
   129	        {
   130	            // Upstream: "0100" with length=1 throws "cannot fit in 1 byte(s)"
   131	            Action act = () => Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString("0100", 1);
   132	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>()
   133	               .WithMessage("hex value cannot fit in a buffer of 1 byte(s)");
   134	        }
   135	
   136	        [Fact]
   137	        public void HexToAscii_Roundtrip()
   138	        {
   139	            const string asciiHex = "627566666572";
   140	            Encoding.HexToAscii(asciiHex).Should().Be("buffer");
   141	        }
   142	
   143	        [Fact]
   144	        public void HexToAscii_OddLength_JsParity()
   145	        {
   146	            // JS: parseInt('f', 16) === 15, String.fromCharCode(15) === ''
   147	            Encoding.HexToAscii("f").Should().Be("");
   148	        }
   149	
   150	        [Fact]
   151	        public void HexToAscii_InvalidPair_EmitsNul()
   152	        {
   153	            // JS: parseInt('zz', 16) === NaN, String.fromCharCode(NaN) === ' '
   154	            Encoding.HexToAscii("zz").Should().Be(" ");
   155	        }
   156	
   157	        [Fact]
   158	        public void HexToAscii_JsParityWhitespace()
   159	        {
   160	            // JS: parseInt(' f', 16) === 15 -> String.fromCharCode(15) === '\u000F'
   161	            // (leading whitespace skipped per JS spec)
   162	            Encoding.HexToAscii(" f").Should().Be("\u000F");
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        [Fact]
   166	        public void HexToAscii_JsParitySign()
   167	        {
   168	            // JS: parseInt('+f', 16) === 15 -> '\u000F'
   169	            Encoding.HexToAscii("+f").Should().Be("\u000F");
   170	        }
   171	
   172	        [Fact]
   173	        public void HexToAscii_JsParityTabBeforeHex()
   174	        {
   175	            // JS: parseInt('\tA', 16) === 10 -> '\u000A' (LF)
   176	            Encoding.HexToAscii("\tA").Should().Be("\u000A");
   177	        }
   178	
   179	        [Fact]
   180	        public void Uint8ArrayFromHexString_LengthZero_TreatedAsOmitted()
   181	        {
   182	            // JS: `if (!length)` is true for 0; behavior is identical to omitted length.
   183	            Encoding.Uint8ArrayFromHexString("01", 0).Should().Equal(new byte[] { 1 });
   184	        }
   185	
   186	        [Fact]
   187	        public void NormalizePadding_AddsLeadingZeros()
   188	        {
   189	            byte[] input = { 0x01, 0x02 };
   190	            Encoding.NormalizePadding(input, 4).Should().Equal(new byte[] { 0, 0, 1, 2 });
   191	        }
   192	
   193	        [Fact]
   194	        public void NormalizePadding_StripsLeadingZeros()
   195	        {
   196	            byte[] input = { 0x00, 0x00, 0x01, 0x02 };
   197	            Encoding.NormalizePadding(input, 2).Should().Equal(new byte[] { 1, 2 });
   198	        }
   199	
   200	        [Fact]
   201	        public void NormalizePadding_StripWouldRemoveNonZero_Throws()
   202	        {
   203	            byte[] input = { 0x01, 0x02, 0x03, 0x04 };
   204	            Action act = () => Encoding.NormalizePadding(input, 2);
   205	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>()
   206	               .WithMessage("invalid number of starting zeroes*");
   207	        }
   208	
   209	        [Fact]
   210	        public void NormalizePadding_EqualLength_Identity()
   211	        {
   212	            byte[] input = { 0x01, 0x02 };
   213	            Encoding.NormalizePadding(input, 2).Should().Equal(input);
   214	        }
   215

   224	        }

   246	            Encoding.StringToBase64UrlString(input).Should().Be(expected);

   249	        [Fact]
   250	        public void StringToBase64UrlString_CodePointAbove255_Throws()
   251	        {
   252	            Action act = () => Encoding.StringToBase64UrlString("aĀb");
   253	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>()
   254	               .WithMessage("InvalidCharacterError: found code point greater than 255:256 at position 1");
   255	        }
   256	
   257	        [Fact]
   258	        public void Base64StringToBase64UrlEncodedString_UpstreamVectors()
   259	        {
   260	            Encoding.Base64StringToBase64UrlEncodedString("aGVsbG8gd29ybGQ=")
   261	                .Should().Be("aGVsbG8gd29ybGQ");
   262	            Encoding.Base64StringToBase64UrlEncodedString("U29tZSBzYW1wbGUgdGV4dA==")
   263	                .Should().Be("U29tZSBzYW1wbGUgdGV4dA");
   264	        }
   265	
   266	        [Fact]
   267	        public void HexStringToBase64Url_UpstreamVectors()
   268	        {
   269	            Encoding.HexStringToBase64Url("01").Should().Be("AQ");
   270	            Encoding.HexStringToBase64Url("01", 2).Should().Be("AAE");
   271	            Encoding.HexStringToBase64Url("ff").Should().Be("_w");
   272	            Encoding.HexStringToBase64Url("ff", 2).Should().Be("AP8");
   273	        }
   274	
   275	        [Fact]
   276	        public void HexStringToBase64Url_TooLong_Throws()
   277	        {
   278	            Action act = () => Encoding.HexStringToBase64Url("0100", 1);
   279	            act.Should().Throw<ArgumentException>()
   280	               .WithMessage("hex value cannot fit in a buffer of 1 byte(s)");
   281	        }
   282	
   283	        [Fact]
   284	        public void Base64UrlToBase64_RestoresPadding()
   285	        {
   286	            Encoding.Base64UrlToBase64("aGVsbG8gd29ybGQ").Should().Be("aGVsbG8gd29ybGQ=");
   287	            Encoding.Base64UrlToBase64("U29tZSBzYW1wbGUgdGV4dA").Should().Be("U29tZSBzYW1wbGUgdGV4dA==");
   288	            Encoding.Base64UrlToBase64("AQ").Should().Be("AQ==");
   289	        }
   290	
   291	        [Fact]
   292	        public void Base64UrlToBase64_NoChangeWhenAlreadyPadded()
   293	        {
   294	            // "AAAA" length 4, padding 0
   295	            Encoding.Base64UrlToBase64("AAAA").Should().Be("AAAA");
   296	        }
   297	
   298	        [Fact]
   299	        public void DecodeBase64UrlToString_Roundtrip()
   300	        {
   301	            Encoding.DecodeBase64UrlToString("aGVsbG8").Should().Be("hello");
   302	            // From upstream private-key encoding vector
   303	            const string b64url =
   304	                "NTIzNGQwOGRmYTJjODE1ZjMwOTdiOGJhODQ4YTI4MTcyZTg1YmVjNzg4ODZlOGUyMDFhZmNjYjE2NmZjNTRjMQ";
   305	            Encoding.DecodeBase64UrlToString(b64url).Should().Be(
   306	                "5234d08dfa2c815f3097b8ba848a28172e85bec78886e8e201afccb166fc54c1");
   307	        }
   308	
   309	        [Fact]
   310	        public void DecodeBase64UrlToString_StripsInvalidChars()
   311	        {
   312	            // JS atob silently strips chars not in [A-Za-z0-9+/=] before decoding.
   313	            // "aGVsbG8" decodes to "hello"; "a*GVsbG8" must too.
   314	            Encoding.DecodeBase64UrlToString("a*GVsbG8").Should().Be("hello");
   315	        }
   316	
   317	        [Fact]
   318	        public void DecodeBase64UrlToString_LengthMod4Is1_Throws()
   319	        {
   320	            // JS atob: throws when (filtered length) % 4 === 1.
   321	            // 5 chars from [A-Za-z0-9] (no = since base64 padding is +0/2/3),
   322	            // restoring base64 padding adds 3 '='s => total length 8 mod 4 = 0,
   323	            // so we need to confirm the post-padding check triggers.
   324	            // The upstream rule fires on the filtered (post-replace) length;
   325	            // construct an input that yields exactly mod-4==1 after restore.
   326	            // "a" base64url -> "a===" base64 -> filtered length stays 4. mod4=0.
   327	            // We must construct mod-4==1 *after* padding: e.g. "ab" -> "ab==" len 4 mod4=0.
   328	            // The only way to hit mod4==1 is if input strips to something like "a"
   329	            // before padding; Base64UrlToBase64("a") => "a===" mod4=0. So in practice
   330	            // the throw is unreachable via Base64UrlToBase64 input; we exercise the
   331	            // raw path with a manually crafted length-5 string.
   332	            // Use bytes with a leading '=' inside which atob treats as padding reset.
   333	            // Easiest: stamp the helper directly via a length that hits mod-4==1.
   334	            // The Base64UrlToBase64 sanitizer adds '=' until len % 4 == 0, so the
   335	            // only way to trip the throw is when an embedded '=' is followed by
   336	            // material that brings the total to a mod-4==1 residue. We skip the
   337	            // throw test here because the public API path cannot produce it; the
   338	            // throw is kept defensively to match upstream.
   339	            // Sanity check: trivial valid input still decodes.
   340	            Encoding.DecodeBase64UrlToString("AQ").Should().Be("");
   341	        }
   342	
   343	        // ========================================================
   344	        // PointEncode
   345	        // ========================================================
   346	
   347	        [Fact]
   348	        public void PointEncode_EvenY_PrefixIs02()
   349	        {
   350	            var raw = new byte[65];
   351	            raw[0] = 0x04;
   352	            for (int i = 1; i < 33; i++) raw[i] = 0xAA;
   353	            for (int i = 33; i < 65; i++) raw[i] = 0xBB;
   354	            raw[64] = 0xBE; // last byte even
   355	
   356	            var compressed = Encoding.PointEncode(raw);
   357	
   358	            compressed.Should().HaveCount(33);
   359	            compressed[0].Should().Be(0x02);
   360	            for (int i = 1; i < 33; i++) compressed[i].Should().Be(0xAA);

    30	describe("HPKE Encryption and Decryption", () => {
    31	  test("hpkeAuthEncrypt and hpkeDecrypt - end-to-end encryption and decryption", () => {
    32	    const senderKeyPair = generateP256KeyPair();
    33	    const receiverKeyPair = generateP256KeyPair();
    34	    const receiverPublicKeyUncompressed = uncompressRawPublicKey(
    35	      uint8ArrayFromHexString(receiverKeyPair.publicKey),
    36	    );
    37	
    38	    const textEncoder = new TextEncoder();
    39	    // Mock plaintext
    40	    const plainText = "Hello, this is a secure message!";
    41	    const plainTextBuf = textEncoder.encode(plainText);
    42	    // Encrypt
    43	    const encryptedDataBuf = hpkeAuthEncrypt({
    44	      plainTextBuf: plainTextBuf,
    45	      targetKeyBuf: receiverPublicKeyUncompressed,
    46	      senderPriv: senderKeyPair.privateKey,
    47	    });
    48	    const encryptedData = formatHpkeBuf(encryptedDataBuf);
    49	    // Extract the encapsulated key buffer and the ciphertext
    50	    const data = JSON.parse(encryptedData);
    51	    // Decrypt
    52	    const decryptedData = hpkeDecrypt({
    53	      ciphertextBuf: uint8ArrayFromHexString(data.ciphertext),
    54	      encappedKeyBuf: uint8ArrayFromHexString(data.encappedPublic),
    55	      receiverPriv: receiverKeyPair.privateKey,
    56	    });
    57	
    58	    // Convert decrypted data back to string
    59	    const decryptedText = new TextDecoder().decode(decryptedData);
    60	
    61	    // Expect the decrypted text to equal the original plaintext
    62	    expect(decryptedText).toEqual(plainText);
    63	  });
    64	});
    65	
    66	describe("HPKE Standard Encryption and Decryption", () => {
    67	  test("hpkeEncrypt and hpkeDecrypt - standard mode (ephemeral sender key)", async () => {
    68	    // Generate a receiver key pair
    69	    const receiverKeyPair = generateP256KeyPair();
    70	    const receiverPublicKeyUncompressed = uncompressRawPublicKey(
    71	      uint8ArrayFromHexString(receiverKeyPair.publicKey),
    72	    );
    73	
    74	    // Prepare the plaintext
    75	    const textEncoder = new TextEncoder();
    76	    const plainText =
    77	      "6ab33bd6e4bdc73017233da0554f9616fe10ede5c3ce001e81b321d5a74199b7";
    78	    const plainTextBuf = textEncoder.encode(plainText);
    79	
    80	    // Encrypt using standard mode (no sender private key provided)
    81	    const encryptedDataBuf = hpkeEncrypt({
    82	      plainTextBuf: plainTextBuf,
    83	      targetKeyBuf: receiverPublicKeyUncompressed,
    84	      // No senderPriv provided, so it will use an ephemeral key
    85	    });
    86	    const encryptedData = formatHpkeBuf(encryptedDataBuf);
    87	    // Parse the encrypted data
    88	    const data = JSON.parse(encryptedData);
    89	    // Decrypt the message
    90	    const decryptedData = hpkeDecrypt({
    91	      ciphertextBuf: uint8ArrayFromHexString(data.ciphertext),
    92	      encappedKeyBuf: uint8ArrayFromHexString(data.encappedPublic),
    93	      receiverPriv: receiverKeyPair.privateKey,
    94	    });
    95	
    96	    // Convert decrypted data back to string
    97	    const decryptedText = new TextDecoder().decode(decryptedData);
    98	
    99	    // Verify that the decrypted text matches the original plaintext
   100	    expect(decryptedText).toEqual(plainText);
   101	
   102	    // Additional checks to ensure standard mode behavior
   103	    const encappedPublicKey = uint8ArrayFromHexString(data.encappedPublic);
   104	    expect(encappedPublicKey.length).toBe(65); // Uncompressed public key length
   105	    expect(encappedPublicKey[0]).toBe(0x04); // Uncompressed public key prefix
   106	  });
   107	});

   199	  test("verifyRequestStamp", async () => {
   200	    const { publicKey: apiPublicKey, privateKey: apiPrivateKey } =
   201	      generateP256KeyPair();
   202	    const apiKeyStamper = new ApiKeyStamper({
   203	      apiPublicKey,
   204	      apiPrivateKey,
   205	    });
   206	
   207	    const turnkeyClient = new TurnkeyClient(
   208	      {
   209	        baseUrl: "https://api.turnkey.com",
   210	      },
   211	      apiKeyStamper,
   212	    );
   213	
   214	    const stampedRequest = await turnkeyClient.stampGetWhoami({
   215	      organizationId: "00000000-00000000-00000000-00000000",
   216	    });
   217	
   218	    const stampContents = stampedRequest.stamp.stampHeaderValue;
   219	    const decodedStampContents = atob(stampContents);
   220	    const parsedStampContents = JSON.parse(decodedStampContents);
   221	    const signature = parsedStampContents.signature;
   222	
   223	    const verified = await verifyStampSignature(
   224	      apiPublicKey,
   225	      signature,
   226	      stampedRequest.body,
   227	    );
   228	
   229	    expect(verified).toEqual(true);
   230	  });

   262	  describe("Valid DER signatures", () => {
   263	    test("should parse a simple DER signature with short-form length", () => {
   264	      // Create a signature with 32-byte r and s values
   265	      const rValue = new Array(32).fill(0x01);
   266	      const sValue = new Array(32).fill(0x02);
   267	      const totalLength = 2 + 32 + 2 + 32; // 2 bytes for each INTEGER header + values
   268	
   269	      const derHex = createDerSignature([totalLength], rValue, sValue);
   270	
   271	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(derHex)).not.toThrow();
   272	    });
   273	
   274	    test("should parse a DER signature with 33-byte integers (with leading zero)", () => {
   275	      // ECDSA signatures sometimes have leading zeros to ensure positive integers
   276	      const rValue = [0x00, ...new Array(32).fill(0x80)]; // Leading zero + high bit set
   277	      const sValue = [0x00, ...new Array(32).fill(0x90)];
   278	      const totalLength = 2 + 33 + 2 + 33;
   279	
   280	      const derHex = createDerSignature([totalLength], rValue, sValue);
   281	
   282	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(derHex)).not.toThrow();
   283	    });
   284	  });
   285	
   286	  describe("Invalid signatures - missing SEQUENCE tag", () => {
   287	    test("should reject signatures without SEQUENCE tag (0x30)", () => {
   288	      const invalidHex = bytesToHex([
   289	        0x31, // Wrong tag (should be 0x30)
   290	        0x44, // Length of SEQUENCE
   291	        0x02,
   292	        0x20,
   293	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x01), // r
   294	        0x02,
   295	        0x20,
   296	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x02), // s
   297	      ]);
   298	
   299	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(invalidHex)).toThrow(
   300	        "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: invalid format (missing SEQUENCE tag)",
   301	      );
   302	    });
   303	
   304	    test("should reject empty signatures", () => {
   305	      expect(() => fromDerSignature("")).toThrow(
   306	        "cannot create uint8array from invalid hex string",
   307	      );
   308	    });
   309	
   310	    test("should reject signatures that are too short", () => {
   311	      const shortHex = bytesToHex([0x30]); // Only SEQUENCE tag, no length
   312	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(shortHex)).toThrow(
   313	        "failed to convert DER-encoded signature: insufficient length",
   314	      );
   315	    });
   316	  });
   317	
   318	  describe("Invalid signatures - length field issues", () => {
   319	    test("should reject signatures with unsupported length encoding (0x80-0xFE range)", () => {
   320	      const unsupportedLengthHex = bytesToHex([
   321	        0x30, // SEQUENCE tag
   322	        0x81, // Length encoding value that we do not want to support
   323	        0x44, // Length value
   324	        // ... rest of signature would follow
   325	      ]);
   326	
   327	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(unsupportedLengthHex)).toThrow(
   328	        /large or invalid signature length/,
   329	      );
   330	    });
   331	
   332	    test("should handle edge case of maximum short-form length (0x7F)", () => {
   333	      // This would be a very large signature chunk with trailing data, but valid short-form
   334	      const rValue = new Array(32).fill(0x01);
   335	      const sValue = new Array(32).fill(0x02);
   336	
   337	      const derHex = bytesToHex([
   338	        0x30, // SEQUENCE tag
   339	        0x7f, // Maximum short-form length of SEQUENCE
   340	        0x02, // INTEGER tag
   341	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   342	        ...rValue, // r (34 bytes total for INTEGER including header)
   343	        0x02, // INTEGER tag
   344	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   345	        ...sValue, // s (34 bytes total for INTEGER including header)
   346	        ...new Array(0x7f - 68).fill(0x00), // Padding to reach 0x7F total length
   347	      ]);
   348	
   349	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(derHex)).not.toThrow();
   350	    });
   351	
   352	    test("should reject signatures with invalid r length", () => {
   353	      const invalidRTagHex = bytesToHex([
   354	        0x30, // SEQUENCE tag
   355	        0x44, // length of SEQUENCE
   356	        0x02, // Correct tag for r
   357	        0x22, // length of INTEGER // invalid -- should be 32 or 33
   358	        ...new Array(34).fill(0x01), // r
   359	        0x02, // Correct tag for s
   360	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   361	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x02), // s
   362	      ]);
   363	
   364	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(invalidRTagHex)).toThrow(
   365	        /unexpected length for r/,
   366	      );
   367	    });
   368	
   369	    test("should reject signatures with invalid s length", () => {
   370	      const invalidRTagHex = bytesToHex([
   371	        0x30, // SEQUENCE tag
   372	        0x44, // length of SEQUENCE
   373	        0x02, // Correct tag for r
   374	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   375	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x01), // r
   376	        0x02, // Correct tag for s
   377	        0x22, // length of INTEGER // invalid -- should be 32 or 33
   378	        ...new Array(34).fill(0x02), // s
   379	      ]);
   380	
   381	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(invalidRTagHex)).toThrow(
   382	        /unexpected length for s/,
   383	      );
   384	    });
   385	
   386	    test("should reject signatures with invalid, non-padding r bytes", () => {
   387	      const invalidRTagHex = bytesToHex([
   388	        0x30, // SEQUENCE tag
   389	        0x44, // length of SEQUENCE
   390	        0x02, // Correct tag for r
   391	        0x21, // length of INTEGER // 33 -- this is valid
   392	        ...new Array(33).fill(0x01), // r -- this is invalid, as the first byte in a 33 byte sequence is a non-padding byte
   393	        0x02, // Correct tag for s
   394	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   395	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x02), // s
   396	      ]);
   397	
   398	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(invalidRTagHex)).toThrow(
   399	        /invalid number of starting zeroes/,
   400	      );
   401	    });
   402	
   403	    test("should reject signatures with invalid, non-padding s bytes", () => {
   404	      const invalidRTagHex = bytesToHex([
   405	        0x30, // SEQUENCE tag
   406	        0x44, // length of SEQUENCE
   407	        0x02, // Correct tag for r
   408	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   409	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x01), // r
   410	        0x02, // Correct tag for s
   411	        0x21, // length of INTEGER // 33 -- this is valid
   412	        ...new Array(33).fill(0x02), // s -- this is invalid, as the first byte in a 33 byte sequence is a non-padding byte
   413	      ]);
   414	
   415	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(invalidRTagHex)).toThrow(
   416	        /invalid number of starting zeroes/,
   417	      );
   418	    });
   419	  });
   420	
   421	  describe("Invalid signatures - INTEGER parsing", () => {
   422	    test("should reject signatures with invalid r INTEGER tag", () => {
   423	      const invalidRTagHex = bytesToHex([
   424	        0x30, // SEQUENCE tag
   425	        0x44, // length of SEQUENCE
   426	        0x03, // WRONG tag for r (0x03 instead of 0x02)
   427	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   428	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x01), // r
   429	        0x02, // Correct tag for s
   430	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   431	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x02), // s
   432	      ]);
   433	
   434	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(invalidRTagHex)).toThrow(
   435	        /invalid tag for r/,
   436	      );
   437	    });
   438	
   439	    test("should reject signatures with invalid s INTEGER tag", () => {
   440	      const invalidSTagHex = bytesToHex([
   441	        0x30, // SEQUENCE tag
   442	        0x44, // length of SEQUENCE
   443	        0x02, // Correct tag for r
   444	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   445	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x01), // r
   446	        0x03, // WRONG tag for s (0x03 instead of 0x02)
   447	        0x20, // length of INTEGER
   448	        ...new Array(32).fill(0x02), // s
   449	      ]);
   450	
   451	      expect(() => fromDerSignature(invalidSTagHex)).toThrow(
   452	        /invalid tag for s/,
   453	      );
   454	    });
   455	  });
   456	});
   457	
   458	describe("Session JWT signature", () => {
   459	  test("verifies the provided JWT against its public key", async () => {
   460	    const jwt =
   461	      "eyJhbGciOiJFUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9." +
   462	      "eyJleHAiOjE3NDg4NzY4MzcsInB1YmxpY19rZXkiOiIwMzk5ZmUyYWNlNjIwOGFmMGFkZjg0OGY0NGJjNDgyMTBiNTk0YjdlNjllY2Q5MWVjOTY4ZmQ3NWIzYmI0NDgzMzYiLCJzZXNzaW9uX3R5cGUiOiJTRVNTSU9OX1RZUEVfUkVBRF9XUklURSIsInVzZXJfaWQiOiI2OTEyYjgxOS1mNGRmLTQwZjQtYTE5Mi0yMGVlNDMwOTA5NzQiLCJvcmdhbml6YXRpb25faWQiOiJjNzVlY2IwNy1jODRhLTRkZDUtOTMyYy01MzlkZmFmYzY4NjQifQ." +
   463	      "y6LPW1jlTwc9jFcvCwKJoKfleL_vHnGUr5tRVdMFUCnHvDspSPZ3DWK85tf1znCCBFQ6MYaFOl-1FLb0KcFxqQ";
   464	
   465	    const ok = await verifySessionJwtSignature(jwt);
   466	    expect(ok).toBe(true);
   467	  });
   468	});
   469	
   470	// Helper function to create hex strings from byte arrays
   471	const bytesToHex = (bytes: number[]): string => {
   472	  return bytes.map((b) => b.toString(16).padStart(2, "0")).join("");
   473	};
   474	
   475	// Helper function to create a basic DER signature structure
   476	const createDerSignature = (
   477	  sequenceLength: number[],
   478	  rValue: number[],
   479	  sValue: number[],
   480	): string => {
   481	  const rLength = rValue.length;
   482	  const sLength = sValue.length;
   483	
   484	  return bytesToHex([
   485	    0x30, // SEQUENCE tag
   486	    ...sequenceLength, // Sequence length (can be multiple bytes)
   487	    0x02, // INTEGER tag for r
   488	    rLength, // r length (assuming single byte for simplicity)
   489	    ...rValue,
   490	    0x02, // INTEGER tag for s
   491	    sLength, // s length (assuming single byte for simplicity)
   492	    ...sValue,
   493	  ]);
   494	};

   272	});
   273	
   274	test("typecheck only: `withAsyncPolling` only works with mutations that return an activity", () => {
   275	  // Legit ones
   276	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.createApiKeys });
   277	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.createInvitations });
   278	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.createPolicy });
   279	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.createPrivateKeys });
   280	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.deleteApiKeys });
   281	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.deleteInvitation });
   282	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.deletePolicy });
   283	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.signRawPayload });
   284	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.signTransaction });
   285	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.getActivity });
   286	
   287	  // Invalid ones
   288	  // @ts-expect-error
   289	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.postGetOrganization });
   290	  // @ts-expect-error
   291	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.postGetPolicy });
   292	  // @ts-expect-error
   293	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.postGetUser });
   294	  // @ts-expect-error
   295	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.postGetActivities });
   296	  // @ts-expect-error
   297	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.postGetPolicies });
   298	  // @ts-expect-error
   299	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.postGetPrivateKeys });
   300	  // @ts-expect-error
   301	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.postGetUsers });
   302	  // @ts-expect-error
   303	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.postGetWhoami });
   304	  // @ts-expect-error
   305	  withAsyncPolling({ request: TurnkeyApi.postGetPrivateKey });
   306	});

    62	
    63	  test("should verify valid app proof signatures", () => {
    64	    expect(verifyAppProofSignature(testAppProof1)).toBeUndefined();
    65	    expect(verifyAppProofSignature(testAppProof2)).toBeUndefined();
    66	  });
    67	
    68	  test("should verify correct app proof / boot proof combos", async () => {
    69	    await expect(
    70	      verify(testAppProof1, testBootProof1),
    71	    ).resolves.toBeUndefined();
    72	    await expect(
    73	      verify(testAppProof2, testBootProof2),
    74	    ).resolves.toBeUndefined();
    75	  });
    76	
    77	  test("should NOT verify with malformed app proofs", () => {
    78	    let malformedAppProof2 = { ...testAppProof2 };
    79	
    80	    // Wrong publicKey - should cause signature verification failure
    81	    malformedAppProof2.publicKey = testAppProof1.publicKey;
    82	    expect(() => verifyAppProofSignature(malformedAppProof2)).toThrow(
    83	      "Signature verification failed",
    84	    );
    85	    malformedAppProof2.publicKey = testAppProof2.publicKey;
    86	
    87	    // Wrong proofPayload - should cause signature verification failure
    88	    malformedAppProof2.proofPayload = testAppProof1.proofPayload;
    89	    expect(() => verifyAppProofSignature(malformedAppProof2)).toThrow(
    90	      "Signature verification failed",
    91	    );
    92	    malformedAppProof2.proofPayload = testAppProof2.proofPayload;
    93	
    94	    // Wrong signature - should cause signature verification failure
    95	    malformedAppProof2.signature = testAppProof1.signature;
    96	    expect(() => verifyAppProofSignature(malformedAppProof2)).toThrow(
    97	      "Signature verification failed",
    98	    );
    99	  });
   100	
   101	  test("should NOT verify with malformed boot proofs", async () => {
   102	    let malformedBootProof2 = { ...testBootProof2 };
   103	
   104	    // Wrong ephemeral key - should cause ephemeral key mismatch
   105	    malformedBootProof2.ephemeralPublicKeyHex =
   106	      testBootProof1.ephemeralPublicKeyHex;
   107	    await expect(verify(testAppProof2, malformedBootProof2)).rejects.toThrow(
   108	      "Ephemeral pub keys from app proof:",
   109	    );
   110	    malformedBootProof2.ephemeralPublicKeyHex =
   111	      testBootProof2.ephemeralPublicKeyHex;
   112	
   113	    // Wrong awsAttestationDocB64 - causes ephemeral key mistmatch error because the boot proofs have the same qos manifest, so the user data check doesn't fail
   114	    malformedBootProof2.awsAttestationDocB64 =
   115	      testBootProof1.awsAttestationDocB64;
   116	    await expect(verify(testAppProof2, malformedBootProof2)).rejects.toThrow(
   117	      "Ephemeral pub keys from app proof:",
   118	    );
   119	    malformedBootProof2.awsAttestationDocB64 =
   120	      testBootProof2.awsAttestationDocB64;
   121	
   122	    // Wrong qosManifestB64 (randomly generated) - should cause user_data verification failure
   123	    malformedBootProof2.qosManifestB64 =
   124	      "puwpDDoA3dqZpFV0nDnSgj2iFyy2VDUnDSE7u+awts0=";
   125	    await expect(verify(testAppProof2, malformedBootProof2)).rejects.toThrow(
   126	      "attestationDoc's user_data doesn't match the hash of the manifest. ",
   127	    );
   128	  });
   129	});

Pass criterion for round 3: **not met**. The plan is much improved, but I found blocking issues in B/C/F/G.

**A. Plan Provenance**
- Plan file path: `plans/PLAN-EQUIVALENCE-VERIFICATION.md`
- Plan version: **Draft v3**, from `Status:` at `plans/PLAN-EQUIVALENCE-VERIFICATION.md:3`; v3 delta table at `:5-22`, v2 history at `:23-30`.
- Existing internal references checked: all exist.
  `codex-crypto-reviews/README.md`, `tests/Fixtures/README.md`, `codex-crypto-reviews/FINAL-INTEGRATED-REVIEW-20260523.md`, `codex-crypto-reviews/Http.cs-codex-findings-reconciliation.md`, `codex-crypto-reviews/ApiKeyStamper.cs-codex-findings-reconciliation.md`, `plans/plan-v2-codex-reviewed.md`, `plans/PLAN-RELEASE-WORKFLOW.md`, `codex-crypto-reviews/turnkey-source-pins.md`, `src/Crypto.cs`, the 3 existing `tests/Fixtures/{encoding,crypto,api-key-stamper}/...json`, and cited upstream snapshot files all exist.
- Broken links: none among existing internal references. Future artifacts such as `coverage-map.sh`, `test-file-checksums.txt`, `fixture-regen.yml`, and `tests/Fixtures/proofs/` are planned outputs, not current broken links.

**B. Internal-Consistency Audit**
| Section | Result |
|---|---|
| 1 | No conflict. |
| 2 | Conflict: Section 2 says HPKE uses `aead_id=0x0002 = AES-256-GCM` and derives a 32-byte AES key (`plans/...:70-78`, `:109-116`), but Section 6.3 says “HPKE は 128bit AES” (`plans/...:400-403`). Fix: change Section 6.3 comment to “HPKE derives a 32-byte AES-256-GCM key; include AES-GCM-256 vectors, and AES-GCM-128 only if separately justified.” |
| 3 | No conflict with final review or fixture provenance. |
| 4 | No conflict. |
| 5 | No conflict. |
| 6 | Same AES conflict above. Also PR-2/coverage gate says `MISSING` exits non-zero (`plans/...:266-270`) while PR-2 says MISSING zero but missing tests are deferred to PR-3 (`plans/...:541-542`). Fix: allow PR-2 to merge with documented `MISSING` rows and enable fail-on-MISSING only in PR-3, or merge PR-2+PR-3 together. |
| 7 | Conflict: PR-3 is “tests only / code untouched” (`plans/...:542`), but upstream `hpkeAuthEncrypt` has a test (`upstream-snapshots/.../crypto-test.ts:31-63`) and C# explicitly does not port `hpkeAuthEncrypt` (`src/Crypto.cs:21-26`). Fix: mark `hpkeAuthEncrypt` as explicit N/A unless a feature PR adds the API before PR-3. |
| 8 | No conflict. |
| 9 | No unbounded issue risk; idempotent issue update is consistent (`plans/...:462-484`, `:584`). |
| 10 | Conflict: FAQ says peak proof usage “判定済み” / confirmed (`plans/...:627-630`), but Section 12.1 says the grep is future Phase A work (`plans/...:675-678`). Fix: change FAQ to “Phase Aで確認する.” |
| 11 | No conflict. |
| 12 | No internal conflict, but it intentionally records assumptions not mechanically verified; see G. |
| 13 | Internal references resolve. External references were not live-verified in this local-only review. |

**C. Cryptographic-Claim Audit**
- HPKE/QOS: v3 no longer claims SDK HPKE is QOS. Upstream confirms SDK `hpkeEncrypt/hpkeDecrypt` JSdoc references RFC 9180 and uses HPKE labels/suite IDs (`crypto.ts:87-152`, `:301-347`, `constants.ts:1-23`); QOS is separate, SHA-512-HMAC/AES-GCM/borsh (`crypto.ts:218-276`, `:792-856`). C# ports SDK HPKE only (`src/Crypto.cs:404-487`), not QOS (`src/Crypto.cs:21-26`). Confirmed.
- Noble purejs deterministic low-S: pinned snapshot proves purejs calls `p256.sign(hash, privateKey)` with no opts (`api-key-stamper/.../purejs.ts:21-23`) and `package.json` uses `@noble/curves: ^1.3.0` (`package.json:50-53`). The exact noble source is not in `upstream-snapshots`, so v3 correctly makes this fail-closed via exact lock + preflight (`plans/...:342-346`). Not load-bearing without that PR-4 preflight.
- Stamper JSON order/scheme: confirmed in TS source and dist: `{ publicKey, scheme, signature }`, scheme `SIGNATURE_SCHEME_TK_API_P256` (`index.ts:94-103`, `dist/index.js:63-70`).
- Tarball contents: actual `.tgz` files are not present, but extracted `package/` contents and `files` arrays show published packages contain `dist/`, `CHANGELOG.md`, `README.md`, no tests/fixtures (`crypto/package.json:30-34`, `api-key-stamper/package.json:36-40`, `encoding/package.json:26-30`, `http/package.json:33-37`).
- Correction: Section 6.3’s “HPKE is 128bit AES” note is wrong against the pinned source/plan constants; see B.

**D. Coverage / Scope Audit**
PR-3 scope is non-trivial. Upstream tests that need C# implementation or explicit N/A mapping include:
- API key stamper: `pointDecode -> uncompressed invalid`, `uncompressed valid`, `compressed`; `sign with Turnkey fixture: sign (node crypto/WebCrypto/PureJS/universal)`; `sign with openssl generated key pairs: stamp (node/WebCrypto/universal)`; `uses provided signature to make stamp`.
- Crypto: `hpkeAuthEncrypt and hpkeDecrypt...` (currently N/A unless API added), `decryptExportBundle... mnemonic`, `... non-mnemonic`, `extractPrivateKeyFromPKCS8Bytes`, `verifyRequestStamp`, all 14 DER parser tests at `crypto-test.ts:263-454`, positive `Session JWT signature`.
- HTTP: all 6 `withAsyncPolling` tests, plus `requests return grpc status details as part of their errors`.
- Proof: 4 proof tests are N/A for verifier parity, but PR-11 must at least parse/provenance-check fixtures.
- Forgotten primitives: SHA-512 is only QOS, so fine if QOS remains out of scope (`plans/...:661-663`, `:702-704`). If proof implementation becomes in-scope later, add P-384 ECDSA, X.509 chain, COSE/CBOR parsing vectors. Current fixture-only seeding is not harmful because PR-11 adds `ProofFixtureProvenanceTests` (`plans/...:552`, `:631-636`), but it is staging data, not equivalence coverage.

**E. Operational Risk Audit**
- Existing workflows are .NET-only where relevant: CI uses setup-dotnet and `dotnet test` (`.github/workflows/ci.yml:19-41`), release uses setup-dotnet and `dotnet test` (`release.yml:99-123`), consumer smoke uses setup-dotnet (`consumer-smoke.yml:117-207`). No existing workflow needs Node unless it executes the new generator workflow.
- The current test csproj copies all `Fixtures/**/*` (`tests/turnkey-sdk-csharp.Tests.csproj:23-26`), so PR-4’s generator exclusion is required before adding `Generators/`.
- Drift issue creation is bounded by label+package open-issue reuse (`plans/...:462-484`).
- Platform risk appears bounded: dependencies are JS packages, no native/optional native modules in the pinned package manifests (`crypto/package.json:41-49`, `api-key-stamper/package.json:50-53`, `encoding/package.json:37-39`). Generator must force `purejs`; Node/WebCrypto paths are runtime-dependent.

**F. Plan-Writing-Quality Audit**
- Blocking: PR-2 and PR-3 are not independently mergeable as written because PR-2 both introduces a fail-on-MISSING gate and defers missing tests to PR-3 (`plans/...:266-270`, `:541-542`).
- Blocking: PR-3 “tests only” conflicts with the `hpkeAuthEncrypt` upstream test unless that test is declared N/A (`plans/...:288`, `src/Crypto.cs:21-26`).
- Goals are mostly measurable. The vague parts are resolved if PR-2/PR-3 gate sequencing and `hpkeAuthEncrypt` N/A wording are fixed.
- Redundancy: FAQ repeats HPKE/Tier content (`plans/...:607-619`), but this is not blocking.

**G. Unresolved Assumptions**
- Other-language SDK fixture facts are explicitly not machine-verified in this plan (`plans/...:671-677`).
- peak proof / `withAsyncPolling` usage is still future grep work, despite FAQ wording implying it is already decided (`plans/...:627-630`, `:675-678`).
- `tkhq/python-sdk` live-e2e uniqueness is recorded as agent investigation, not mechanically verified (`plans/...:677`).
- Fixed-ephemeral injection feasibility is intentionally deferred to PR-7a (`plans/...:422-434`, `:678`).
- Exact noble low-S source is not present under `upstream-snapshots`; PR-4 preflight is the proposed verifier (`plans/...:342-346`, `api-key-stamper/package.json:50-53`).

**E. Operational Risk Audit**
- Existing workflows are .NET-only where relevant: CI uses setup-dotnet and `dotnet test` (`.github/workflows/ci.yml:19-41`), release uses setup-dotnet and `dotnet test` (`release.yml:99-123`), consumer smoke uses setup-dotnet (`consumer-smoke.yml:117-207`). No existing workflow needs Node unless it executes the new generator workflow.
- The current test csproj copies all `Fixtures/**/*` (`tests/turnkey-sdk-csharp.Tests.csproj:23-26`), so PR-4’s generator exclusion is required before adding `Generators/`.
- Drift issue creation is bounded by label+package open-issue reuse (`plans/...:462-484`).
- Platform risk appears bounded: dependencies are JS packages, no native/optional native modules in the pinned package manifests (`crypto/package.json:41-49`, `api-key-stamper/package.json:50-53`, `encoding/package.json:37-39`). Generator must force `purejs`; Node/WebCrypto paths are runtime-dependent.

**F. Plan-Writing-Quality Audit**
- Blocking: PR-2 and PR-3 are not independently mergeable as written because PR-2 both introduces a fail-on-MISSING gate and defers missing tests to PR-3 (`plans/...:266-270`, `:541-542`).
- Blocking: PR-3 “tests only” conflicts with the `hpkeAuthEncrypt` upstream test unless that test is declared N/A (`plans/...:288`, `src/Crypto.cs:21-26`).
- Goals are mostly measurable. The vague parts are resolved if PR-2/PR-3 gate sequencing and `hpkeAuthEncrypt` N/A wording are fixed.
- Redundancy: FAQ repeats HPKE/Tier content (`plans/...:607-619`), but this is not blocking.

**G. Unresolved Assumptions**
- Other-language SDK fixture facts are explicitly not machine-verified in this plan (`plans/...:671-677`).
- peak proof / `withAsyncPolling` usage is still future grep work, despite FAQ wording implying it is already decided (`plans/...:627-630`, `:675-678`).
- `tkhq/python-sdk` live-e2e uniqueness is recorded as agent investigation, not mechanically verified (`plans/...:677`).
- Fixed-ephemeral injection feasibility is intentionally deferred to PR-7a (`plans/...:422-434`, `:678`).
- Exact noble low-S source is not present under `upstream-snapshots`; PR-4 preflight is the proposed verifier (`plans/...:342-346`, `api-key-stamper/package.json:50-53`).
